--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/CallsignService.lua ---

--[[
    CallsignService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local NetworkService;
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

local SET_CALLSIGN_EVENT = 'SetCallsign';

local prefixes;
local ProfileDataService;

local CallsignService = {Client = {}, Callsigns = {}, SwitchTeamsConnections = {}};

local Comm = require(ReplicatedStorage.Packages.Comm)
local ServerComm = Comm.ServerComm.new(ReplicatedStorage, 'cov')
local CallsignsProperty = ServerComm:CreateProperty('saved_callsigns', {})

local function VerifiedPrefix(teamName, prefix, plr)
    if plr:GetAttribute('Division') ~= nil then
        teamName = plr:GetAttribute('Division');
    end;
    for i, v in next, prefixes do
        if i == teamName then
            if v == prefix then
                return true;
            else
                return false;
            end;
        end;
    end;
end;

function CallsignService:IsCallsignTaken(plr, callsign)
    if string.sub(callsign, #callsign - 2) == "047" and plr.UserId ~= 71812450 then
        return true
    end

    for p, v in self.Callsigns do
        if v[1] == callsign and plr ~= p then
            return true
        end
    end

    return false
end;

function CallsignService:ReloadData(player: Player)
    local callsigns = ProfileDataService.GetData(player, 'Callsigns')
    CallsignsProperty:SetFor(player, callsigns or {})
end

function CallsignService:Start()
    NetworkService.ConnectFunction('IsCallsignTaken', function(plr, callsign)
        return CallsignService:IsCallsignTaken(plr, callsign);
    end)

    NetworkService.ConnectFunction('HasRegisteredCallsign', function(plr, teamName)
        for i, v in next, self.Callsigns do
            if i == plr then
                if v[2] == teamName then
                    return true;
                end;
                return;
            end;
        end;
    end)

	NetworkService.Connect(SET_CALLSIGN_EVENT, function(plr, callsign)
		if tonumber(callsign:sub(3,3)) == nil or tonumber(callsign:sub(4,4)) == nil or tonumber(callsign:sub(5,5)) == nil then return; end
        if #callsign ~= 5 then return; end;
        local teamName = plr:GetAttribute('Division') or plr.Team.Name;
        local prefix = callsign:sub(1, 2)
        local number = callsign:sub(3)
        if not VerifiedPrefix(teamName, prefix, plr) then return; end;

		self.Callsigns[plr] = {callsign, teamName};
        ProfileDataService.SetCategorisedData(plr, 'Callsigns', prefix, number);
        self:ReloadData(plr);

        if not self.SwitchTeamsConnections[plr] then
			self.SwitchTeamsConnections[plr] = {}
			self.SwitchTeamsConnections[plr][1] = plr:GetPropertyChangedSignal('Team'):Connect(function()
				plr:SetAttribute('Division', nil);
                if self.SwitchTeamsConnections[plr] then
                    for _,v in next, self.SwitchTeamsConnections[plr] do
                        v:Disconnect();
                        v = nil;
                    end;
					self.Callsigns[plr] = nil;
                    self.SwitchTeamsConnections[plr] = nil;
				end
			end)
			self.SwitchTeamsConnections[plr][2] = game.Players.PlayerRemoving:Connect(function(plrLeaving)
				if plrLeaving == plr then
					if self.SwitchTeamsConnections[plr] then
                        for _,v in next, self.SwitchTeamsConnections[plr] do
                            v:Disconnect();
                            v = nil;
                        end;
						self.Callsigns[plr] = nil;
                        self.SwitchTeamsConnections[plr] = nil;
					end
				end
			end)
            self.SwitchTeamsConnections[plr][3] = plr:GetAttributeChangedSignal('Division'):Connect(function()
                if self.SwitchTeamsConnections[plr] then
                    for _,v in next, self.SwitchTeamsConnections[plr] do
                        v:Disconnect();
                        v = nil;
                    end;
                    self.Callsigns[plr] = nil;
                    self.SwitchTeamsConnections[plr] = nil;
                end
            end)
		end
    end);
end;

function CallsignService:Init()
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    prefixes = self.Shared.CallsignPrefixes;
    ProfileDataService = self.Modules.ProfileDataService;
end;

return CallsignService;



================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/CarModificationService.lua ---

--[[
    CarModificationService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage');

local carColors = {
    Color3.fromRGB(159, 161, 172),
    Color3.fromRGB(91, 93, 105),
    Color3.fromRGB(151, 0, 0),
    Color3.fromRGB(51, 88, 130),
    Color3.fromRGB(27, 42, 53),
    Color3.fromRGB(202, 203, 209)
};

local GlobalStorage = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.GlobalStorage);
local Comm = require(ReplicatedStorage.Packages.Comm);


local LogoStorage = GlobalStorage.new('BusinessLogoData');
local ServerComm = Comm.ServerComm.new(ReplicatedStorage, 'BusinessLogos');

local NetworkService;
local LicenseDataService;
local ProfileDataService;
local MoneyService;
local NotificationService;
local CooldownService;
local FilterStringAsync;

local PAINT_COST = 400
local PLATE_COST = 1000

local BANNED_PLATES = {
    'CANUCK',
    'C4NUCK',
    'POZZAR',
    'PIZZAR',
    'P1ZZAR',
    'P1ZZ4R',
    'PIZZ4R',
    'BC0001'
}

local DEFAULT_BUSINESS_LOGOS = {};

type PlateData = {
    UserId: number,
    CarType: string,
    Color: Color3
};

type BusinessLogoData = {
    GroupID: number,
    MinimumRank: number,
    LogoID: number
}

local CarModificationService = {
    Client = {};
    BusinessLogosProperty = ServerComm:CreateProperty('CarBusinessLogos', {});
    LogoStorage = LogoStorage;
};

function CarModificationService.GetRandomCarColor()
    return carColors[math.random(1, #carColors)];
end;

function CarModificationService:PaintCar(car: Model, color)
    if not color then
        color = self.GetRandomCarColor();
    end;

    for i, v in next, car.Body.Paint:GetDescendants() do
        if (v:IsA('BasePart') or v:IsA('UnionOperation')) and (v.Name == 'Color') then
            v.Color = color;
        end;
    end;
end;

function CarModificationService:AddBusinessLogo(car: Model, logo: string)
    if not logo then return; end;

    local businessLogos: {string: BusinessLogoData} = self.BusinessLogosProperty:Get();
    local targetLogo: BusinessLogoData = businessLogos[logo];

    if not targetLogo then return; end;

    for _,v in next, car.Body:GetChildren() do
        if v.Name == 'BusinessLogo' then
            v.LogoDecal.Texture = `https://www.roblox.com/Thumbs/Asset.ashx?width=420&height=420&assetId={targetLogo.LogoID}`;
        end;
    end;
end

function CarModificationService:_setupBusinessLogos()
    local succ: boolean, res: {BusinessLogoData} = pcall(LogoStorage.Get, LogoStorage ,'Logos', DEFAULT_BUSINESS_LOGOS);
    if succ then
        self.BusinessLogosProperty:Set(res or DEFAULT_BUSINESS_LOGOS);
    else
        warn(res);
        task.wait(5);
        self:_setupBusinessLogos();
    end;
end

function CarModificationService:Start()
    self:_setupBusinessLogos();
    CooldownService:Create('BusinessLogo');

    LogoStorage:GetKeyChangedSignal('Logos'):Connect(function(newValue)
        self.BusinessLogosProperty:Set(newValue);
    end);

    NetworkService.Connect('PaintCar', function(plr, color)
        if typeof(color) ~= 'Color3' then return; end;
        if plr:GetAttribute('Division') ~= 'GCPS' and plr.Money.Value < PAINT_COST then return; end;

        local car = plr.Car.Value;

        if not car then return; end;

        if car:GetAttribute('Owner') ~= plr.Name then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'You do not own this car.');
            return;
        end;

        local id = car.Config.ID.Value;

        local canBePainted = car.Config:FindFirstChild('CanBePainted');

        if not canBePainted then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'This car cannot be painted.');
            return;
        end;

        local carData = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'BoughtCars');

        for _,v in next, carData do
            if tonumber(v.ID) == id or tostring(v.ID) == id then
                v.Color = {
                    R = color.R,
                    G = color.G,
                    B = color.B
                };
            end;
        end;


        if canBePainted.Value == false then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'This car cannot be painted.');
            return;
        end

        local licensePlate = car.Config:FindFirstChild('LicensePlate');
        local succ, err = pcall(function()
            LicenseDataService:SetColor(licensePlate.Value, color);
        end);

        if not succ then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'Error assigning car data. Try again.');
            return;
        end

        if plr:GetAttribute('Division') ~= 'GCPS' then
            MoneyService:SubtractMoney(plr, PAINT_COST);
        end
        ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'BoughtCars', carData);
		self:PaintCar(car, color)
    end);

    NetworkService.Connect('EditLicensePlate', function(plr, plate)
        if type(plate) ~= 'string' then return; end;

        plate = plate:gsub("[^%w%s_]+", "");

        if string.len(plate) ~= 6 then return; end;

        if plr:GetAttribute('Division') ~= 'GCPS' and plr.Money.Value < PLATE_COST then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'You do not have enough money to edit your license plate. It costs $1000.');
            return;
        end;

        local car = plr.Car.Value;

        if not car then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'You do not have a car spawned.');
            return;
        end;

        if car:GetAttribute('Owner') ~= plr.Name then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'You do not own this car.');
            return;
        end;

        local filterResult = FilterStringAsync(plate, plr.UserId, Enum.TextFilterContext.PublicChat);
        if not filterResult then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'Text was filtered.');
            return;
        end;

        local succ, res = pcall(LicenseDataService.IsPlateTaken, LicenseDataService, plate);
        if not succ then
            _G.AeroError('There was an error. Please try again. Error Code: CD-LP');
            return;
        end;

        if res == true then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'This license plate is already taken.');
            return;
        end;

        local id = car.Config.ID.Value;

        local carData = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'BoughtCars');

        local filteredPlate = string.upper(filterResult:GetNonChatStringForBroadcastAsync());

        if string.find(filteredPlate, '#') or table.find(BANNED_PLATES, filteredPlate) then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'Text was filtered.');
            return;
        end;

        local oldPlate;

        for _,v in next, carData do
            if tostring(v.ID) == id or tonumber(v.ID) == id then
                oldPlate = v.LicensePlate;
                v.LicensePlate = filteredPlate;
                break;
            end;
        end;

        local succ2, oldPlateTbl: PlateData = pcall(function()
            return LicenseDataService:GetPlateData(oldPlate);
        end);

        if not succ2 then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'Error getting old plate data. Try again.');
            return;
        end;

        local succ3, _ = pcall(function()
            LicenseDataService:InitPlateData(filteredPlate, plr.UserId, oldPlateTbl.CarType, oldPlateTbl.Color);
        end);

        if not succ3 then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'Error assigning new plate data. Try again.');
            return;
        end;

        local succ4, _ = pcall(function()
            LicenseDataService:RemovePlateData(oldPlate);
        end);

--        LicenseDataService:MovePlateData(oldPlate, filteredPlate);

        ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'BoughtCars', carData);

        if plr:GetAttribute('Division') ~= 'GCPS' then
            MoneyService:SubtractMoney(plr, PLATE_COST);
        end

        car.Config.LicensePlate.Value = filteredPlate;

        NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Notification', 'Success', 'New Plate: '..filteredPlate..'.', nil, 'Green')
    end);

    NetworkService.Connect('AddBusinessLogo', function(plr: Player, newLogoName: string)
        if CooldownService:Check('BusinessLogo', plr) then return end;
        CooldownService:Add('BusinessLogo', plr, 1.5);
        local carValue = plr:FindFirstChild('Car')
        if not carValue then return end;

        local car = carValue.Value;
        if not car then return end;

        local carConfig = car:FindFirstChild('Config')
        if not carConfig then return end;

        local CanHaveBusinessLogo = carConfig:GetAttribute('CanHaveBusinessLogo');
        if not CanHaveBusinessLogo then
            return _G.AeroError(plr, 'This car cannot have a business logo.');
        end;

        local businessLogos: {string: BusinessLogoData} = self.BusinessLogosProperty:Get();

        local targetLogo: BusinessLogoData;

        if newLogoName ~= 'None' then
            targetLogo = businessLogos[newLogoName];
            if not targetLogo then
                return _G.AeroError(plr, 'Invalid business logo.');
            end;

            if plr:GetRankInGroup(targetLogo.GroupID) < targetLogo.MinimumRank and plr:GetAttribute("Developer") ~= true then
                return _G.AeroError(plr, 'You do not have permission to use this business logo.');
            end;
        end;

        for _,v in next, car.Body:GetChildren() do
            if v.Name == 'BusinessLogo' then
                v.LogoDecal.Texture = if newLogoName == 'None' then '' else `https://www.roblox.com/Thumbs/Asset.ashx?width=420&height=420&assetId={targetLogo.LogoID}`;
            end;
        end;

        local carId = carConfig.ID.Value;

        local carData = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'BoughtCars');

        for _,v in carData do
            if v.ID == carId then
                v.BusinessLogo = (newLogoName ~= 'None' and newLogoName) or nil;
            end;
        end;

        ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'BoughtCars', carData);

        if newLogoName == 'None' then
            NotificationService.Send(plr, "Car Modification", "Business logo removed from vehicle", nil, "Green");
        else
            NotificationService.Send(plr, "Car Modification", "Business logo updated or added to vehicle", nil, "Green");
        end;

        return;
    end)
end;

function CarModificationService:Init()
    MoneyService = self.Services.MoneyService;
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    CooldownService = self.Shared.CooldownService;
    NotificationService = self.Services.NotificationService;
    local Filter = self.Modules.Filter;
    FilterStringAsync = Filter.FilterStringAsync;
    LicenseDataService = self.Modules.LicenseDataService;
    ProfileDataService = self.Modules.ProfileDataService;
end;

return CarModificationService;



================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/CarService.lua ---

--[[
    CarService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local CollectionService = game:GetService("CollectionService")
local MarketplaceService = game:GetService("MarketplaceService")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local Raycast;

local NetworkService;
local DeveloperCheck;
local MoneyService;
local ProfileDataService;

local UP_DIRECTION = Vector3.new(0, 10, 0);
local OFFSET = CFrame.new(0, 4, 0);

local newCFrame = CFrame.new;

local CIVILIAN_CARS = {};
local IDToCar = {};

local UniqueCars = {'Ferrari F40', '3AM F-350'}

local function GetCarFromDescendant(descendant)
	if not descendant then return; end;
	local currentInstance = descendant;
	repeat
		currentInstance = currentInstance.Parent;
		wait();
	until currentInstance:FindFirstChild('Chassis');
	return currentInstance;
end;

local function ExitSeat(seat, rootPart, isExitBlocked)
	local seatWeld = seat:FindFirstChild('SeatWeld');
	if seatWeld then
		seatWeld:Destroy();
	end;
	if isExitBlocked then
		local raycastResult = Raycast.Cast(seat.Position, UP_DIRECTION, {seat, rootPart.Parent, GetCarFromDescendant(seat).Chassis});
		if raycastResult then
			rootPart.CFrame = newCFrame(raycastResult.Position) * OFFSET;
		else
			rootPart.CFrame = seat.CFrame * OFFSET;
		end;
	else
		rootPart.CFrame = seat.Exit.WorldCFrame;
	end;
end;

local function getsFreeGas(player, car)
	local config = car.Config;
	local id = config:FindFirstChild('ID', true);
	local rootCar: Model = IDToCar[id.Value]
	return rootCar:IsDescendantOf(game.ReplicatedStorage.Cars.Translink['SO: Snow'])
end

local CarService = {Client = {}};

function CarService.DestroyCar(car)
	local seats = {};

	pcall(function()
		for i, v in next, car.Body:GetDescendants() do
			if v:IsA('Seat') or v:IsA('VehicleSeat') then
				table.insert(seats, v);
			end;
		end;
	end)

	pcall(function()
		for i, v in next, seats do
			local seatWeld = v:FindFirstChild('SeatWeld');
			if seatWeld then
				seatWeld:Destroy();
			end;
		end;
	end)

	pcall(function()
		local seatWeld = car.Chassis:FindFirstChildOfClass('VehicleSeat'):FindFirstChild('SeatWeld');
		if seatWeld then
			seatWeld:Destroy();
		end;
	end)

	pcall(function()
		car:Destroy();
	end)
end;

function CarService.ClearCars(plr)
	local car = plr:FindFirstChild('Car') and plr.Car.Value;
	if car and not car:GetAttribute('BeingTowed') then
		CarService.DestroyCar(car);
	end;
	for _, c in workspace.Cars:GetChildren() do
		if
			(c:GetAttribute('LastDriver') == plr.Name and not c:GetAttribute('BeingTowed'))
			or (c:GetAttribute('LastDriver') == nil and c:GetAttribute('Owner') == plr.Name and not c:GetAttribute('BeingTowed'))
			or (c:GetAttribute('Owner') == plr.Name and c:GetAttribute('Inserted') == true)
			or (c:GetAttribute('Owner') == plr.Name
				-- and table.find(UniqueCars, c.Name)
				and CarService.IsCivilianCar(c) -- this is why we can't have nice things
				and not c:GetAttribute('BeingTowed'))
		then
			CarService.DestroyCar(c)
		end
	end
end

function CarService.IsCivilianCar(car)
	local config = car.Config;
	local id = config:FindFirstChild('ID', true);
	if table.find(CIVILIAN_CARS, id.Value) then
		return true;
	end;
	return false;
end;

function CarService.IsEmergencyCar(car)
	return CarService.IsCivilianCar(car) == false;
end

CarService.GetCarFromDescendant = GetCarFromDescendant;

function CarService:_duplicateCheck()
	local carIDs = {}
	local carNames = {}

	for _,v in next, game.ReplicatedStorage.Cars:GetDescendants() do
        if v:IsA('IntValue') and v.Name == 'ID' then
            local car = v.Parent.Parent.Parent;
            local carName = car.Name;
            if carIDs[v.Value] then
								if carName ~= carIDs[v.Value] then
                  warn('Duplicate car ID found: '..v.Value..' for '..carName..' and '..carIDs[v.Value]);
								end
							else
                carIDs[v.Value] = carName;
            end;

						if carNames[carName] ~= nil and carNames[carName] ~= v.Value and not v:IsDescendantOf(game.ReplicatedStorage.Cars.GCPS) and carNames[carName] < 50000 then
							warn(`Duplicate car name found: {carName} (IDs {v.Value} and {carNames[carName]})`)
						end
						carNames[carName] = v.Value
        end;
    end;
end;

function CarService:Start()
	-- GCPS stuff
	do
		local cars = ReplicatedStorage.Cars
		local gcps = cars.GCPS

		local IGNORE = {"Ferrari F40", "'18 Mustang"}

		local FOLDERS = {
			[cars.Civilian] = gcps['Civilian Replica'],
			[cars['Canada Post']] = gcps['Business Replica'],
		}

		local function addCar(c, parent)
			local car = c:Clone()
			car.Config.SpawnerSettings.ID.Value += 50000
			if car.Config.SpawnerSettings:FindFirstChild("Price") then
				car.Config.SpawnerSettings.Price.Value = 0
			end
			if car.Config.SpawnerSettings:FindFirstChild("MinRank") then
				car.Config.SpawnerSettings.MinRank.Value = 0
			end
			car.Parent = parent
		end

		for folder, parent in FOLDERS do
			for _, car in folder:GetChildren() do
				if table.find(IGNORE, car.Name) then continue end
				if car:IsA("Folder") then continue end
				addCar(car, parent)
			end
		end

		local function restrictSeat(car)
			for _, x in car.Body:GetDescendants() do
				if x:IsA("VehicleSeat") and CollectionService:HasTag(x, "VehicleSeat") then
					x.Name = "Rear"
					x:SetAttribute("RestrictedSeat", true)
				end
			end
		end

		for _, a in ReplicatedStorage.Cars.GCPS:GetChildren() do
			if a:IsA("Folder") then
				for _, b in a:GetChildren() do
					restrictSeat(b)
				end
			elseif a:IsA("Model") then
				restrictSeat(a)
			end
		end
	end

	self:_duplicateCheck();

    for _,v in next, game.ReplicatedStorage.Cars.Civilian:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('Model') then
            table.insert(CIVILIAN_CARS, v.Config.SpawnerSettings.ID.Value);
        elseif v:IsA('Folder') then
            for _,v2 in next, v:GetChildren() do
                table.insert(CIVILIAN_CARS, v2.Config.SpawnerSettings.ID.Value);
            end;
        end;
    end;

		for _,v in next, game.ReplicatedStorage.Cars.GCPS:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('Model') then
            table.insert(CIVILIAN_CARS, v.Config.SpawnerSettings.ID.Value);
        elseif v:IsA('Folder') then
            for _,v2 in next, v:GetChildren() do
                table.insert(CIVILIAN_CARS, v2.Config.SpawnerSettings.ID.Value);
            end;
        end;
    end;

	for _, obj in game.ReplicatedStorage.Cars:GetDescendants() do
		if obj.Name == "ID" and obj:IsA("IntValue") and obj.Parent.Name == "SpawnerSettings" then
			local id = obj.Value
			local car = obj.Parent.Parent.Parent
			IDToCar[id] = car
		end
	end

	NetworkService.Connect('Car', function(plr, event, ...)
		if event == 'Exit' then
			local char = plr.Character;
			local seat = char.Humanoid.SeatPart;
			if plr:GetAttribute('HandcuffedBy') then return; end;
			if plr:GetAttribute('GrabbedBy') then return; end;
			if plr:GetAttribute('PlacedInVehicle') then return; end;
			if seat then
				seat.SeatWeld:Destroy();
				ExitSeat(seat, char.HumanoidRootPart, ...);
			end;
		end;
	end);

	NetworkService.Connect('CAR_RADIO', function(plr, event, id)
		local car = plr.Car.Value;
		if not car then return; end;
		local ownsGamepass = plr:GetAttribute('OwnsRadio');
		if not ownsGamepass and not DeveloperCheck(plr) then
			MarketplaceService:PromptGamePassPurchase(plr, 27439586);
			return;
		end;

		local musicSound = car.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Radio;

		if event == 'PLAY' then
		id = id:match('%d+');
		if #id < 3 then return; end;
			musicSound.SoundId = 'rbxassetid://'..id;
			musicSound:Play();
		else
			musicSound:Stop();
		end;
	end)

	NetworkService.Connect('GasPump', function(plr)
		if not plr.Car.Value then return; end;
		local car = plr.Car.Value;
		local state = car.Config.State;
		local gas = state.Gas;

		local gasPrice = game.ReplicatedStorage.GasPrice;
		local freeGas = getsFreeGas(plr, car);
		if (not freeGas) and plr.Money.Value < gasPrice.Value then return; end;

		if gas.Value >= (gas:GetAttribute('MaxGas') or 100) then return; end;
		local newGasValue = gas.Value + 1;

		local boughtCars = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'BoughtCars');
		for _,v in next, boughtCars do
			if tonumber(v.ID) == car.Config.ID.Value then
				v.Gas = newGasValue
			end;
		end;
		gas.Value = newGasValue;
		ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'BoughtCars', boughtCars);
		if not freeGas then MoneyService:SubtractMoney(plr, gasPrice.Value); end
	end)
end;

function CarService:Init()
	DeveloperCheck = self.Shared.DeveloperCheck;
	Raycast = self.Shared.Raycast;
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
	MoneyService = self.Services.MoneyService;
	ProfileDataService = self.Modules.ProfileDataService;
end;

return CarService;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/CarSpawner/CarSpawnerModel.lua ---

--[[
    CarSpawnerModel (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → CarSpawner
    Parent: CarSpawner
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local cars = game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage'):WaitForChild('Cars');

local ProfileDataService;
local MoneyService;
local CarModificationService;
local LicensePlateService;
local LicenseDataService;
local CarService;

-- local CIVILIAN_REDIRECT_TEAMS = {
--     ['Provincial Court'] = true,
--     ['Legislative Assembly'] = true,
-- }

local CarSpawnerModel = {};

function CarSpawnerModel.GetCarsFolderForPlayer(plr)
    local jobName = plr:GetAttribute('CurrentJob');
    local division = plr:GetAttribute('Division');
    local folder = (jobName and cars:FindFirstChild(jobName)) or (division and cars:FindFirstChild(division)) or cars:FindFirstChild(plr.Team.Name)
    if folder:GetAttribute("Redirect") then
        local newFolder = cars:FindFirstChild(folder:GetAttribute("Redirect"))
        if not newFolder then
            warn(`Invalid redirect folder \`{folder:GetAttribute("Redirect")}\` for {folder.Name}`)
            return folder
        end
        return newFolder
    end
    return folder

    --return (CIVILIAN_REDIRECT_TEAMS[plr.Team.Name] == true and cars['Civilian']) or (jobName and cars[jobName]) or (division and cars[division]) or cars[plr.Team.Name];
end;

function CarSpawnerModel:GetCarFromID(plr, carID)
    local carsFolder = self.GetCarsFolderForPlayer(plr);
    for i, v in next, carsFolder:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('Model') then
            local spawnerSettings = v.Config.SpawnerSettings;
            if spawnerSettings.ID.Value == carID then
                return v;
            end;
        else
            for i2, v2 in next, v:GetChildren() do
                local spawnerSettings = v2.Config.SpawnerSettings;
                if spawnerSettings.ID.Value == carID then
                    return v2;
                end;
            end
        end;
    end;
end;

function CarSpawnerModel:GetCarPriceFromID(plr, carID)
    local car = self:GetCarFromID(plr, carID);
    if not car then return; end;
    return car.Config.SpawnerSettings.Price.Value;
end;

function CarSpawnerModel.GetOpenSpawner(carSpawner, destroyIfFull)
    local spawns = {};
    local openSpawner;

    for i, v in next, carSpawner.Parent.Spawns:GetChildren() do
        local orderNumber = v.Name:gsub('Spawn', '');
        spawns[tonumber(orderNumber)] = v;
    end;

    for i, v in next, spawns do
        if openSpawner then break; end;
        openSpawner = v;

        local overlapParams = OverlapParams.new();
        overlapParams.FilterDescendantsInstances = {workspace.Cars};
        overlapParams.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Whitelist;
        overlapParams.MaxParts = 75;

        local touchingParts = workspace:GetPartsInPart(v);
        --local touchingParts = workspace:FindPartsInRegion3WithWhiteList(region3, {workspace.Cars}, 50);
        for i2, v2 in next, touchingParts do
            local body = v2.Parent;
            if body.Name == 'Body' then
                if i == #spawns and destroyIfFull then
                    -- body.Parent:Destroy();
                    CarService.DestroyCar(body.Parent);
                else
                    openSpawner = nil;
                end;
                break;
            elseif body.Name == 'Paint' then
                if i == #spawns and destroyIfFull then
                    -- body.Parent.Parent:Destroy();
                    CarService.DestroyCar(body.Parent.Parent);
                else
                    openSpawner = nil;
                end;
                break;
            end;
        end;
    end;
    return openSpawner;
end;

function CarSpawnerModel.SetupCar(car: Model, carInfo)
    local config = car:WaitForChild('Config');
    if config:WaitForChild('CanBePainted').Value then
        CarModificationService:PaintCar(car, Color3.new(carInfo.Color.R, carInfo.Color.G, carInfo.Color.B));
    end;

    local body = car:WaitForChild('Body');
    if body:FindFirstChild('BusinessLogo') then
        CarModificationService:AddBusinessLogo(car, carInfo.BusinessLogo);
    end;

    local plr = carInfo.Player

    --Fixed an error where they had no plate
    if carInfo.LicensePlate == nil then
        local licensePlate = LicensePlateService.Create();
        local carID = car.Config.SpawnerSettings.ID.Value

        local existingData = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'BoughtCars');

        local newData = {
            ID = carID;
            LicensePlate = licensePlate;
            Color = existingData.Color;
            BusinessLogo = existingData.BusinessLogo
        };

        table.insert(existingData, newData);

        ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'BoughtCars', existingData);
        carInfo = newData;
    end;

    config:WaitForChild('LicensePlate').Value = carInfo.LicensePlate;

    car:SetAttribute('Owner', plr.Name);
    car:SetAttribute('LicensePlate', carInfo.LicensePlate);
    car:SetAttribute('Color', Color3.new(carInfo.Color.R, carInfo.Color.G, carInfo.Color.B));
end;

function CarSpawnerModel.DoesCarRequireMinRank(car)
    local spawnerSettings = car.Config.SpawnerSettings;
    local groupID = spawnerSettings:FindFirstChild('GroupID');
    local minRank = groupID and spawnerSettings:FindFirstChild('MinRank');
    if not minRank then return; end;

    local condition = spawnerSettings:FindFirstChild('Condition');
    local conditionFunc;
    if condition then
        conditionFunc = require(condition);
    end;

    return groupID.Value, minRank.Value, conditionFunc;
end;

function CarSpawnerModel.BuyCar(plr, carID, price)
    local color = CarModificationService.GetRandomCarColor();
    local plate = LicensePlateService.Create();

    local car = CarSpawnerModel:GetCarFromID(plr, carID);

    local succ, res = pcall(function()
        LicenseDataService:InitPlateData(plate, plr.UserId, car.Name, color);
    end);

    if not succ then
        _G.AeroError(plr, 'Error generating plate data. Try buying this car again.');
        warn("Stopped a car purchase: ".. res);
        return;
    end;

    MoneyService:SubtractMoney(plr, price);

    local carData = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'BoughtCars');

    table.insert(carData, {
        ID = carID;
        LicensePlate = plate;
        Color = {
            R = color.R;
            G = color.G;
            B = color.B;
        };
        Inventory = {}
    });

    ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'BoughtCars', carData);
end;

function CarSpawnerModel.HasBoughtCar(plr, carID)
    local found = false;
    local carInfo;

    local carData = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'BoughtCars');

    for _, v in carData do
        if tonumber(v.ID) == carID or tostring(v.ID) == carID then
            found = true;
            carInfo = v;
            break;
        end;
    end;

    if found == false then return false; end;

    return {
        Color = carInfo.Color;
        LicensePlate = carInfo and carInfo.LicensePlate or nil;
        BusinessLogo = carInfo and carInfo.BusinessLogo or nil;
        Player = plr;
    };
end;

function CarSpawnerModel:Start()

end;

function CarSpawnerModel:Init()
    LicenseDataService = self.Modules.LicenseDataService;
    CarModificationService = self.Services.CarModificationService;
    CarService = self.Services.CarService;
    LicensePlateService = self.Services.LicensePlateService;
    ProfileDataService = self.Modules.ProfileDataService;
    MoneyService = self.Services.MoneyService;
end;

return CarSpawnerModel;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/CarSpawner/CarSpawnerService.lua ---

--[[
    CarSpawnerService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → CarSpawner
    Parent: CarSpawner
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local CarSpawnerModel;
local NetworkService;
local NotificationService;
local DeveloperCheck;
local CarService;
local ToolContainerService;
local ProfileDataService;

local BUY_CAR_EVENT;
local PAY_OFF_CAR_EVENT;
local SPAWN_CAR_EVENT;

local MoneyService;

local carsFolder = workspace:WaitForChild('Cars');

_G.CarDamages = {}

local GlobalStorage = require(script.Parent.Parent.Parent.Modules.GlobalStorage);

local LimitedCarStore = GlobalStorage.new('LimitedCarData');
local CarSpawnerService = {Client = {}, LastSpawned = {}};

function CarSpawnerService:Start()
    NetworkService.ConnectFunction('HasBoughtCar', function(plr, carName)
        return CarSpawnerModel.HasBoughtCar(plr, carName) and true or false;
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect(BUY_CAR_EVENT, function(plr, carID)
        if CarSpawnerModel.HasBoughtCar(plr, carID) then return; end;
        local price = CarSpawnerModel:GetCarPriceFromID(plr, carID);
        if not price then return; end;
        if plr.Money.Value < price then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'Insufficient money.');
            return;
        end;

        local car = CarSpawnerModel:GetCarFromID(plr, carID);
        if not car then return; end;
        local isLimitedQuantity = car.Config.SpawnerSettings:FindFirstChild('LimitedQuantity');
        local limitedQuantity = (isLimitedQuantity and car.Config.SpawnerSettings.LimitedQuantity.Value) or nil;
        local isDeveloper = DeveloperCheck(plr);

        if isLimitedQuantity and not isDeveloper then
            local succ, res = pcall(function()
                return LimitedCarStore:Get(carID, {}, true)
            end)

            if not succ then return _G.AeroError(plr, 'There was an error checking the stock for this vehicle. Try again later.'); end;
            if #res >= limitedQuantity then return _G.AeroError(plr, 'This car is out of stock.'); end;

            local succ2 = pcall(function()
                LimitedCarStore:Update(carID, function(oldValue)
                    if not oldValue then oldValue = {}; end;
                    if table.find(oldValue, plr.UserId) then return oldValue; end;

                    table.insert(oldValue, plr.UserId);
                    return oldValue;
                end)
            end);

            if not succ2 then return _G.AeroError(plr, 'There was an error purchasing this car. Try again. If this continues, report this error code: UPD1'); end;
        end;

        CarSpawnerModel.BuyCar(plr, carID, price);
        NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Bought Car', CarSpawnerModel:GetCarFromID(plr, carID).Name, nil, 'Green');
        return true;
	end);

	NetworkService.Connect(PAY_OFF_CAR_EVENT, function(plr, carID)
		if _G.CarDamages then
			if _G.CarDamages[plr.UserId] then
				if _G.CarDamages[plr.UserId][carID] then
					if _G.CarDamages[plr.UserId][carID] <= 0 then
						if plr.Money.Value < 750 then NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'Insufficient money.') return; end
						MoneyService:SubtractMoney(plr, 750)
						_G.CarDamages[plr.UserId][carID] = 100
					end
				end
			end
		end
	end)

	NetworkService.Connect(SPAWN_CAR_EVENT, function(plr, carID, carSpawner)
		if _G.CarDamages[plr.UserId] then
			if _G.CarDamages[plr.UserId][carID] then
				if _G.CarDamages[plr.UserId][carID] <= 0 then
					NetworkService.Send(plr, 'PromptCarPayOff', 'Car Spawning Service', 'The car you attempted to spawn is damaged. Would you like to pay $750 to repair it?', carID)
					return;
				end
			end
		else
			_G.CarDamages[plr.UserId] = {}
		end
        if (carSpawner.Position - plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude > 7 then return; end;

        local lastSpawnTime = self.LastSpawned[plr];
        if lastSpawnTime then
            if os.time() - lastSpawnTime < 0.7 then
                NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'Spawning too quickly.');
                return;
            end;
        end;

        self.LastSpawned[plr] = os.time();
        CarService.ClearCars(plr)

        local carInfo = CarSpawnerModel.HasBoughtCar(plr, carID);
        if not carInfo then return; end;

        local existingCarModel = CarSpawnerModel:GetCarFromID(plr, carID);
        if not existingCarModel then return; end;

        local groupID, minRank, conditionFunc = CarSpawnerModel.DoesCarRequireMinRank(existingCarModel);
        if not ((not minRank) or DeveloperCheck(plr) or (plr:GetRankInGroup(groupID) >= minRank) or conditionFunc(plr)) then
            return
        end

        local car = existingCarModel:Clone();
        local openSpawner = CarSpawnerModel.GetOpenSpawner(carSpawner, plr.Team.Name == 'Civilian');
        if not openSpawner then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'No open spawner.');
            return;
        end
        car:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(openSpawner.CFrame);
        CarSpawnerModel.SetupCar(car, carInfo);
        car.ModelStreamingMode = Enum.ModelStreamingMode.Persistent;
        car.Parent = carsFolder;

        local config = car:WaitForChild('Config')
        config:WaitForChild('SpawnerSettings').ID:Clone().Parent = config;
        config:WaitForChild('SpawnerSettings'):Destroy();
		config:WaitForChild('State'):WaitForChild('Locked').Value = true;
		if _G.CarDamages then
			if _G.CarDamages[plr.UserId] then
				if _G.CarDamages[plr.UserId][carID] ~= nil then
					config:WaitForChild('State'):WaitForChild('Health').Value = _G.CarDamages[plr.UserId][carID] or 100
				end
			end
		end;

        if CarService.IsEmergencyCar(car) then
            ToolContainerService:CreateContainerForInstance(car);
        end;

        local boughtCars = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'BoughtCars');
        for _,v in next, boughtCars do
            if tonumber(v.ID) == carID then
                if v.Gas then
                    config.State.Gas.Value = v.Gas;
                end
            end
        end

        plr.Car.Value = car;
        plr:SetAttribute('LastVehicle', carID)

        NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Spawned Car', car.Name);
    end);
end;

function CarSpawnerService:Init()
    CarSpawnerModel = self.Services.CarSpawner.CarSpawnerModel;
    CarService = self.Services.CarService;
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    NotificationService = self.Services.NotificationService;
    CarService = self.Services.CarService;
    DeveloperCheck = self.Shared.DeveloperCheck;
    ToolContainerService = self.Services.ToolContainerService;
    ProfileDataService = self.Modules.ProfileDataService;

    local constants = self.Shared.Constants.CarSpawner;
    BUY_CAR_EVENT = constants.BUY_CAR_EVENT;
	SPAWN_CAR_EVENT = constants.SPAWN_CAR_EVENT;
	PAY_OFF_CAR_EVENT = constants.PAY_OFF_CAR_EVENT;
    MoneyService = self.Services.MoneyService;
end;

return CarSpawnerService;

--[[
    CarTrailerService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services

    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Car Trailer Service
-- Khizzer
-- January 22, 2023



local CarTrailerService = {Client = {}}

local NetworkService;


function CarTrailerService:Start()
	NetworkService.Connect('TruckHitchBegin', function(plr: Player, interactionPart: Attachment)
        if not typeof(interactionPart) == 'Instance' then return; end;

        local truck = interactionPart.Parent.Parent.Parent;
        if not truck:IsDescendantOf(workspace.Cars) then return; end;

        if not plr.Car.Value == truck then return; end;

        local truckForHitch = Instance.new('ObjectValue');
        truckForHitch.Name = 'TruckForHitch';
        truckForHitch.Value = truck;
        truckForHitch.Parent = plr;
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('AttachTrailer', function(plr: Player, interactionPart: Attachment)
        local truckForHitch = plr:FindFirstChild('TruckForHitch');
        if not truckForHitch then return; end;

        local truck = truckForHitch.Value;
        local trailerHinge = truck.Chassis.Platform:FindFirstChild('TrailerHinge');

        if not trailerHinge then return; end;
        if trailerHinge.Attachment0 then return; end; --stop it from doing weird stuff

        interactionPart.Parent.Anchored = false;

        trailerHinge.Attachment0 = interactionPart;

        truckForHitch:Destroy();
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('DetatchTrailer', function(plr: Player, interactionPart: Attachment)
        local trailerHinge = interactionPart.Parent:FindFirstChild("TrailerHinge");

        local attachment0 = trailerHinge.Attachment0;
        local trailerPlatform = attachment0.Parent;

        trailerPlatform.Anchored = true;

        trailerHinge.Attachment0 = nil;
    end)
end


function CarTrailerService:Init()
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
end


return CarTrailerService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/CitationService.lua ---

--[[
    CitationService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local NetworkService;

local MAX_MAGNITUDE = 7;
local CITATION_SEND_REMOTE = 'SendCitation';
local CitationsModule;
local CooldownName = "CitationSentCooldowns"
local CooldownTable;
local RecordService;
local CooldownService;
local WhitelistedTeams;

local MoneyService;

local PendingCitations = {};


local CitationService = {Client = {}; PendingCitations = PendingCitations};

function FindCitationPrice(Value)
	return CitationsModule[Value];
end

function CitationService:Start()
	NetworkService.Connect(CITATION_SEND_REMOTE, function(Player, Target, Citations, details)
		if not WhitelistedTeams.CheckLEO(Player) then return; end
		if CooldownService:Check(CooldownName, Player) == true then NetworkService.Send(Player, 'Error', 'On cooldown.') return; end
		if not Target then return; end;
		if not Citations then return; end;

		if PendingCitations[Target] ~= nil then NetworkService.Send(Player, 'Error', 'User already has a citation.') return; end
		if type(Citations) ~= "table" then return; end;

		local CharacterTarget = Target.Character or Target.CharacterAdded:Wait();
		local CharacterPlayer = Player.Character or Player.CharacterAdded:Wait();
		if (CharacterPlayer.HumanoidRootPart.Position - CharacterTarget.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude > 7 then return; end;
		local CitationsPrice = 0;
		local CitaionsLooped = 0;

		local offences = {};

		for name, _ in next, Citations do
			if CitaionsLooped < 3 then
				if FindCitationPrice(name) ~= nil then
					CitationsPrice = CitationsPrice + FindCitationPrice(name)
					CitaionsLooped = CitaionsLooped + 1
					offences[#offences+1] = name;
				end
			end
		end
		if CitationsPrice < 0  then return; end
		CooldownService:Add(CooldownName, Player, 30)
		PendingCitations[Target] = CitationsPrice

		local teamAbbreviation = Player.Team:GetAttribute('Abbreviation');

		RecordService:AddCitation(Player.Name, teamAbbreviation, Target, CitationsPrice, offences, details)

		NetworkService.Send(Target, 'PromptCitationPayOff', 'You have been fined!', 'Are you going to pay this citation off? (If you do not, a warrant will be put out on you.)')
	end);

	NetworkService.Connect('CitationPay', function(Player, Value)
		if Value == true then
			if PendingCitations[Player] == nil then return; end
			if PendingCitations[Player] <= 0 then PendingCitations[Player] = nil return; end
			MoneyService:SubtractMoney(Player, math.max(PendingCitations[Player], 0))
			PendingCitations[Player] = nil
		elseif Value == false or Value == nil then
			if PendingCitations[Player] == nil then return; end
			if PendingCitations[Player] <= 0 then PendingCitations[Player] = nil return; end
			RecordService:SetBolo(Player, 'AUTO-BOLO', 'DID NOT SIGN CITATION');
		end;
	end);
end;

function CitationService:Init()
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
	CitationsModule = require(game.ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild('CitationsModule'));
	CooldownService = self.Shared.CooldownService;
	WhitelistedTeams = self.Shared.Constants.WhitelistedTeams;
	RecordService = self.Services.RecordService;
	CooldownTable = CooldownService:Create(CooldownName);
	MoneyService = self.Services.MoneyService;
end;

return CitationService;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/CombatService.lua ---

--[[
    CombatService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Combat Service
-- Khizzer
-- November 26, 2022



local CombatService = {Client = {}, InCombat = {}}

local NetworkService;

function CombatService:SetCombat(plr, combatTime)
    if not typeof(plr) == 'Instance' then return end;
    if not self.InCombat[plr] then
        NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Notification', 'In Combat', 'You are in combat! Please wait 60 seconds to be able to reset.', nil, 'Red');
    end;

    self.InCombat[plr] = combatTime;
    NetworkService.Send(plr, 'CombatResetSys', combatTime);
end;

function CombatService:ResetCombat(plr)
    self.InCombat[plr] = nil;
    NetworkService.Send(plr, 'CombatResetSys', 0);
end;

function CombatService:IsInCombat(plr)
    return self.InCombat[plr] ~= nil;
end

function CombatService:Start()
	task.spawn(function()
        while wait(1) do
            for plr, combatTime in pairs(self.InCombat) do
                if combatTime <= 0 then
                    self.InCombat[plr] = nil;
                    NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Notification', 'Combat Ended', 'You are no longer in combat.', nil, 'Red');
                else
                    self.InCombat[plr] = combatTime - 1;
                end;
            end;
        end;
    end);
end


function CombatService:Init()
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
end


return CombatService

--[[
    DealerService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Dealer Service
-- Khizzer
-- June 22, 2021



local DealerService = {Client = {}}

local NetworkService;

local MoneyService;

function DealerService:Start()

    for i,v in next, game.ServerStorage.DealerItems:GetChildren() do
        local dummyTool = Instance.new('Model');
        dummyTool.Name = v.Name;
        for i,part in next, v:GetChildren() do
            if part:IsA('BasePart') then
                local clone = part:Clone();
                clone.Parent = dummyTool;
            end;
        end;

        local Attributes = v:GetAttributes()
        for name, value in next, Attributes do
            dummyTool:SetAttribute(name, value);
        end;
        dummyTool:SetAttribute('Module', nil);
        if dummyTool:FindFirstChild('Handle') then
            dummyTool.PrimaryPart = dummyTool.Handle
        end
        dummyTool.Parent = game.ReplicatedStorage.dummyTools;
    end

    NetworkService.Connect('DEALER_PURCHASE', function(plr, name)
        if not typeof(name) == 'string' then return; end;
        if not game.ServerStorage.DealerItems:FindFirstChild(name) then return; end;

        local item = game.ServerStorage.DealerItems[name]
        local price = item:GetAttribute('Price');

        if plr.Money.Value < tonumber(price) then return; end;

        MoneyService:SubtractMoney(plr, price);

        local newWeapon = item:Clone()
        local date = DateTime.now():FormatUniversalTime('L', 'en-us');
        newWeapon:SetAttribute('ToolSource', `Purchased by {plr.Name} ({date})`);
        newWeapon.Parent = plr.Backpack
    end)
end


function DealerService:Init()
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    MoneyService = self.Services.MoneyService;
end;


return DealerService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/DispatchService.lua ---

--[[
    DispatchService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Dispatch Service
-- Khizzer
-- October 6, 2021

--[[
	Dispatch Service
	Handles dispatch calls & creation of calls

	void | DispatchService:CreateCall(caller: string | Instance, location: string, details: string)
]]

local Players = game:GetService('Players');

local DispatchService = {Client = {}, Calls = {}};
local NetworkService;
local CheckEmergencyServices;
local FilterStringAsync;
local GetChatForUserAsync;
local CallsignService;
local NotificationService;
local FastRemoveFirstValue;

function DispatchService:CreateCall(caller, location: string, details: string)
	local locationFilterResult;
	local detailsFilterResult;

	local UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER: string;

	local isPlayer = typeof(caller) == 'Instance';

	if typeof(caller) ~= 'string' then --If its not the server creating a call
		if self.Calls[tostring(caller.UserId)] then
			NetworkService.Send(caller, 'Error', 'You already have an ongoing call!')
			return;
		end;

		locationFilterResult = FilterStringAsync(location, caller.UserId);
		detailsFilterResult = FilterStringAsync(details, caller.UserId);

--[[		if not locationFilterResult or not detailsFilterResult then
			NetworkService.Send(caller, 'Error', 'DispatchService could not filter text');
			return;
		end;

		local locationFiltered = locationFilterResult:GetNonChatStringForBroadcastAsync();
		local detailsFiltered = detailsFilterResult:GetNonChatStringForBroadcastAsync(); ]]

		UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER = tostring(caller.UserId);

		self.Calls[UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER] = {caller = caller.Name, location = location, details = details, units = {}}
		NotificationService.Send(caller, "911 Emergency", "Your call has been sent to the emergency services", nil, "Green")
		
		--TODO: CHANGE THIS TO BE LESS WEIRD
		caller = caller.Name;
	else
		UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER = game.HttpService:GenerateGUID(false)
		self.Calls[UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER] = {caller = caller, location = location, details = details, units = {}}
	end;

	for _,v in next, Players:GetPlayers() do
		if CheckEmergencyServices(v) or v:GetAttribute("Division") == "GCPS" then
			if isPlayer then
				local locationFiltered = GetChatForUserAsync(locationFilterResult, v.UserId);
				local detailsFiltered = GetChatForUserAsync(detailsFilterResult, v.UserId);

				if not locationFiltered then
					locationFiltered = 'FAILED TO FILTER'
				end;

				if not detailsFiltered then
					detailsFiltered = 'FAILED TO FILTER'
				end;

				location = locationFiltered;
				details = detailsFiltered;
			end;

			NetworkService.Send(v, 'NewDispatchCall', UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER, caller, location, details, {});
		end;
	end;
end;

function DispatchService:Start()
	NetworkService.ConnectFunction('GetCallUnits', function(plr, UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER)
		if not CheckEmergencyServices(plr) and plr:GetAttribute("Division") ~= "GCPS" then return; end;
		if not self.Calls[UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER] then return; end;

		return self.Calls[UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER]['units'];
	end)

	NetworkService.ConnectFunction('GetDispatchCalls', function(plr)
		if not CheckEmergencyServices(plr) and plr:GetAttribute("Division") ~= "GCPS" then return; end;

		type dispatchCall = {
			caller: string,
			location: string,
			details: string,
			units: {string}
		};

		local function filterString(string: string)
			local filterResult = FilterStringAsync(string, plr.UserId);
			if not filterResult then
				return 'FAILED TO FILTER';
			else
				local filteredString = GetChatForUserAsync(filterResult, plr.UserId);
				if not filteredString then
					return 'FAILED TO FILTER';
				else
					return filteredString;
				end;
			end;
		end;

		local callsToSend: {dispatchCall} = {};

		for i,v in next, self.Calls do
			callsToSend[i] = {
				caller = v['caller'],
				location = (v.caller ~= 'DISPATCH' and filterString(v['location'])) or v['location'],
				details = (v.caller ~= 'DISPATCH' and filterString(v['details'])) or v['details'],
				units = v['units']
			};
		end;
		return callsToSend;
	end)

	NetworkService.Connect('911_CALL', function(plr: Instance, location: string, details: string)
		if typeof(location) ~= "string" then return; end;
		if typeof(details) ~= "string" then return; end;

		self:CreateCall(plr, location, details)
	end)

	NetworkService.Connect('JOIN_CALL', function(plr, UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER)
		if not self.Calls[UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER] then return; end;
		if not CheckEmergencyServices(plr) then return; end;
		if not CallsignService.Callsigns[plr] then return; end;

		if table.find(self.Calls[UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER]['units'], CallsignService.Callsigns[plr][1]) then return; end;

		table.insert(self.Calls[UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER]['units'], CallsignService.Callsigns[plr][1]);

		for _,v in next, Players:GetPlayers() do
			if CheckEmergencyServices(v) or v:GetAttribute("Division") == "GCPS" then
				NetworkService.Send(v, 'UPDATE_UNITS', UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER, self.Calls[UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER]['units']);
			end;
		end;
	end)

	NetworkService.Connect('LEAVE_CALL', function(plr, UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER)
		if not self.Calls[UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER] then return; end;
		if not CheckEmergencyServices(plr) then return; end;
		if not CallsignService.Callsigns[plr] then return; end;

		if not table.find(self.Calls[UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER]['units'], CallsignService.Callsigns[plr][1]) then return; end

		FastRemoveFirstValue(self.Calls[UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER]['units'], CallsignService.Callsigns[plr][1]);

		for _,v in next, Players:GetPlayers() do
			if CheckEmergencyServices(v) or v:GetAttribute("Division") == "GCPS" then
				NetworkService.Send(v, 'UPDATE_UNITS', UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER, self.Calls[UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER]['units']);
			end;
		end;
	end)

	NetworkService.Connect('CODE4', function(plr, UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER)
		if not CheckEmergencyServices(plr) then return; end;
		for _,v in next, Players:GetPlayers() do
			if CheckEmergencyServices(v) or v:GetAttribute("Division") == "GCPS" then
				NetworkService.Send(v, 'REMOVE_CALL', UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER, plr.Name);
				self.Calls[UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER] = nil;
			end
		end;
	end)

--[[ 	while true do
		task.wait(5)
		self:CreateCall(tostring(math.random(1, 10)), tostring(math.random(1, 10)), tostring(math.random(1, 10)))
	end ]]
end


function DispatchService:Init()
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
	local WhitelistedTeams = self.Shared.Constants.WhitelistedTeams;
	CheckEmergencyServices = WhitelistedTeams.CheckEmergencyServices;
	FilterStringAsync = self.Modules.Filter.FilterStringAsync;
	GetChatForUserAsync = self.Modules.Filter.GetChatForUserAsync;
	CallsignService = self.Services.CallsignService;
	NotificationService = self.Services.NotificationService;
	FastRemoveFirstValue = self.Shared.TableUtil.FastRemoveFirstValue;
end



return DispatchService

--[[
    DivisionService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
-- Division Service
-- Khizzer
-- February 3, 2022



local DivisionService = {Client = {}}

local DivisionStorage = ReplicatedStorage.Divisions;


local DeveloperCheck;
local POLICE_TEAMS;
local WhitelistedTeams;
local LogsService;
local ToolService;
local GangService;

function DivisionService:Start()
    POLICE_TEAMS = WhitelistedTeams.GetLEOTeams();

	self.NetworkService.Connect('DIVISION_CHANGE', function(plr, division)
        if not DivisionStorage[plr.Team.Name]:FindFirstChild(division) then return; end;

        local targetDivision = DivisionStorage[plr.Team.Name]:FindFirstChild(division);
        local groupID = targetDivision:GetAttribute('GroupID');
        local minimumRank = targetDivision:GetAttribute('MinimumRank');

        if (plr:GetRankInGroup(groupID) < minimumRank) and not DeveloperCheck(plr) then return; end;
        if targetDivision:FindFirstChild('Condition') and not DeveloperCheck(plr) then
            if not require(targetDivision.Condition)(plr) then return end;
        end
        if plr:GetAttribute('Division') == division then return end

        if plr.Team.Name == 'Civilian' then
            --Switching onto NSEC
            ToolService:SaveCivilianTools(plr);
        end;

        plr:SetAttribute('Division', division);
        plr:LoadCharacter();
        if division ~= "GCPS" then
            LogsService:AddLog('Teams', `{plr.Name} changed to {division}`);
        end

        plr:SetAttribute('LastVehicle', nil);
        GangService:RemovePlayer(plr);
    end)
end


function DivisionService:Init()
    WhitelistedTeams = self.Shared.Constants.WhitelistedTeams;
    DeveloperCheck = self.Shared.DeveloperCheck;
    LogsService = self.Services.LogsService;
    ToolService = self.Services.ToolService;
    GangService = self.Services.GangService;
end


return DivisionService

local NetworkService;
local WhitelistedTeams;
local DamageCharacter;

local DrownService = {Client = {}}


function DrownService:Start()
	NetworkService.Connect('Drown', function(plr: Player)
        if WhitelistedTeams.CheckEmergencyServices(plr) and not WhitelistedTeams.CheckLEO(plr) then return end;
        local char = plr.Character;

        DamageCharacter(char, 2);
	end)
end


function DrownService:Init()
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    WhitelistedTeams = self.Shared.Constants.WhitelistedTeams;
    DamageCharacter = self.Modules.DamageCharacter;
end


return DrownService

--[[
    ElectionService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Election Service
-- Khizzer
-- October 16, 2021
local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")

local ServerStorage = game:GetService("ServerStorage")


local ElectionService = {Client = {}}
local ElectionDataService;
local NetworkService;
local DeveloperCheck;
local NotificationService;
local HandshakeService;
local WebUtil;
local ProfileDataService;

local ElectionPart = workspace.ElectionPart;
local electionGUI = ElectionPart.ElectionGUI;
local mainFrame = electionGUI.MainFrame;
local winnersListImage = mainFrame.WinnersListImage
local winnersListScrollingFrame = winnersListImage.WinnersListScrollingFrame;
local lastRefreshedLabel = mainFrame.LastRefreshedLabel;
local electionEndLabel = mainFrame.ElectionEndLabel;
local currentElectionLabel = mainFrame.CurrentElectionLabel;

local electionDecorations = ServerStorage.ElectionDecorations;

local components = electionGUI.Components;
local winnerPreFab = components.WinnerImage;

local electionDetails = Instance.new('Folder');
electionDetails.Name = 'ElectionDetails';
electionDetails.Parent = game.ReplicatedStorage;

local CooldownService;


local ELECTION_COMMISSION = {885226366}

function ElectionService:Start()
    electionDetails:SetAttribute('GUID', ElectionDataService.GetCurrentRunningElection());

    CooldownService:Create('CandidateRetrievalCooldown');
    CooldownService:Create('VoteCooldown');

    if electionDetails:GetAttribute('GUID') then
        electionDetails:SetAttribute('EndTime', ElectionDataService.Get(electionDetails:GetAttribute('GUID'), 'EndTime'));
        electionDetails:SetAttribute('Title', ElectionDataService.Get(electionDetails:GetAttribute('GUID'), 'Title'));
        electionDetails:SetAttribute('Winners', ElectionDataService.Get(electionDetails:GetAttribute('GUID'), 'Winners'));
    end;

    NetworkService.Connect('CREATE_ELECTION', function(plr, title: string , candidates: {string}, endTime: string, winners: number)
        if not DeveloperCheck(plr) and not table.find(ELECTION_COMMISSION, plr.UserId) then return; end;

        local runningElection = electionDetails:GetAttribute('GUID');
        local currentEnd = electionDetails:GetAttribute('EndTime');

        if runningElection and os.time() < currentEnd then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'Election already being held.');
            return;
        end;

        if table.find(candidates, "SPOIL_MY_BALLOT") or table.find(candidates, "Spoil my ballot") then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'Do not insert a spoil ballot candidate.');
            return;
        end;

        local randomID = game:GetService('HttpService'):GenerateGUID(false);
        ElectionDataService.InitialiseElection(randomID, title, candidates, endTime, winners);
    end)

    NetworkService.ConnectFunction('ElectionGetCandidateDetails', function(plr)
        if plr.AccountAge < 90 then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'You must be at least 90 days old to vote.');
            return;
        end;

        local electionID = electionDetails:GetAttribute('GUID');
        local endTime = electionDetails:GetAttribute('EndTime');

        if not electionID then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'No election is being held.');
            return;
		end;

		if os.time() > (tonumber(endTime) or 0) then
			NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'This election has ended.');
			return;
		end;

        if CooldownService:Check('CandidateRetrievalCooldown', plr) then return; end;
        CooldownService:Add('CandidateRetrievalCooldown', plr, 2.5);

        local candidatesData = ElectionDataService.Get(electionID, 'Candidates'); --{Canuckman = 4, Khizzer = 1};
        local candidates = {}
        for name in candidatesData do
            if name == "Spoil my ballot" or name == "SPOIL_MY_BALLOT" then
                continue;
            end
            table.insert(candidates, name);
        end;

        table.insert(candidates, "Spoil my ballot");

        return candidates
    end)

	NetworkService.Connect('ADD_VOTE', function(plr: Player, vote: string | {string})
        if CooldownService:Check('VoteCooldown', plr) then return; end;
        CooldownService:Add('VoteCooldown', plr,  10);

        local electionID = electionDetails:GetAttribute('GUID');
        local endTime = electionDetails:GetAttribute('EndTime');
        local winners = electionDetails:GetAttribute('Winners');

        if plr.AccountAge < 90 then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'You must be at least 90 days old to vote.');
            return;
        end;

        if not electionID then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'No election is being held.');
            return;
		end;

		if os.time() > (tonumber(endTime) or 0) then
			NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'This election has ended.');
			return;
		end;

        if plr:GetRankInGroup(5530527) < 220 then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'You must be a resident to vote.');
            return;
        end;

        if typeof(vote) == "table" and #vote > winners then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', `You can only vote for up to {winners} candidates.`);
            return;
        end

        local alreadyVotedTable = ElectionDataService.Get(electionID, 'AlreadyVoted');
        local suspiciousVotersTable = ElectionDataService.Get(electionID, 'SuspVoters');

        if alreadyVotedTable[plr.UserId] or suspiciousVotersTable[plr.UserId] then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'You have already voted in this election.');
            return;
        end;

        local renderedVote = if typeof(vote) == "string" then vote else table.concat(vote, ", ")

        if ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'VoteBan') then
            WebUtil.SendJSON('https://webhook.lewisakura.moe/api/webhooks/1137519272894152755/B9UClITeOhn6WTs96NB37OHK7AMlUMO82u3YOERt00-B4QKyizuk1TqWNg11XrvWUMK3', {
                embeds = {
                    {
                        title = 'Banned Voter Attempt',
                        fields = {
                            {
                                name = 'Player',
                                value = plr.Name,
                                inline = true
                            },
                            {
                                name = 'Vote',
                                value = renderedVote,
                                inline = true
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            })
            local succ1, err1 = pcall(ElectionDataService.Update, electionID, 'SuspVoters', function(oldKey)
                oldKey[plr.UserId] = true
                return oldKey;
            end);
            if not succ1 then
                NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'Your vote has NOT been recorded. Please try again or contact a developer quoting Error Code 2.');
                warn(err1);
                return;
            end;
            HandshakeService:LogPlayer(plr);
            if vote == 'Spoil my ballot' then
                NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Vote Recorded', 'You have successfully spoiled your ballot');
            else
                NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Vote Recorded', 'You have successfully voted for '.. renderedVote);
            end
            return;
        end;

        local isLogged, match = HandshakeService:IsPlayerLogged(plr);

        if isLogged and plr.UserId ~= match then
            local main = Players:GetNameFromUserIdAsync(match);
            ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'VoteBan', true);
            WebUtil.SendJSON('https://webhook.lewisakura.moe/api/webhooks/1137519272894152755/B9UClITeOhn6WTs96NB37OHK7AMlUMO82u3YOERt00-B4QKyizuk1TqWNg11XrvWUMK3', {
                embeds = {
                    {
                        title = 'Duplicate Vote Attempt',
                        fields = {
                            {
                                name = 'Player',
                                value = plr.Name,
                                inline = true
                            },
                            {
                                name = 'Main Account',
                                value = main,
                                inline = true
                            },
                            {
                                name = 'Vote',
                                value = renderedVote,
                                inline = true
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            })

            local succ1, err1 = pcall(ElectionDataService.Update, electionID, 'SuspVoters', function(oldKey)
                oldKey[plr.UserId] = true
                return oldKey;
            end);
            if not succ1 then
                NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'Your vote has NOT been recorded. Please try again or contact a developer quoting Error Code 2.');
                warn(err1);
                return;
            end;
            HandshakeService:LogPlayer(plr);
            if vote == 'Spoil my ballot' then
                NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Vote Recorded', 'You have successfully spoiled your ballot');
            else
                NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Vote Recorded', 'You have successfully voted for '.. renderedVote);
            end
            return;
        end;

        local succ1, err1 = pcall(ElectionDataService.Update, electionID, 'AlreadyVoted', function(oldKey)
            oldKey[plr.UserId] = true
            return oldKey;
        end);

        if not succ1 then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'Your vote has NOT been recorded. Please try again or contact a developer quoting Error Code 2.');
            warn(err1);
            return;
        end;

        local succ2, err2 = pcall(ElectionDataService.Update, electionID, 'Candidates', function(oldKey)
            if typeof(vote) == "string" then
                oldKey[vote] = (oldKey[vote] or 0) + 1;
            else
                for _, candidate in vote do
                    oldKey[candidate] = (oldKey[candidate] or 0) + 1;
                end
            end
            return oldKey;
        end);

        if not succ2 then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'Your vote has NOT been recorded. Please try again or contact a developer quoting Error Code 4.');
            warn(err2);
            return;
        end;

        HandshakeService:LogPlayer(plr);

        if vote == 'Spoil my ballot' then
            NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Vote Recorded', 'You have successfully spoiled your ballot');
        else
            NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Vote Recorded', 'You have successfully voted for '.. renderedVote);
        end
    end)

    local function CheckElection()
        local electionID = ElectionDataService.GetCurrentRunningElection();
        if not electionID then return; end;
        electionDetails:SetAttribute('GUID', electionID);
        electionDetails:SetAttribute('EndTime', ElectionDataService.Get(electionID, 'EndTime'));
        electionDetails:SetAttribute('Title', ElectionDataService.Get(electionID, 'Title'));
        electionDetails:SetAttribute('Winners', ElectionDataService.Get(electionID, 'Winners'));

        local endTime = ElectionDataService.Get(electionID, 'EndTime');

        if not endTime then return; end;

        lastRefreshedLabel.Text = 'Display refreshes every 2 minutes. Last refreshed: ' .. DateTime.now():FormatUniversalTime('LTS', 'en-us');
        currentElectionLabel.Text = 'CURRENT ELECTION ID: ' .. electionID;
        if os.time() > (tonumber(endTime) or 0) then
            electionEndLabel.Text = 'Election ended at: ' .. DateTime.fromUnixTimestamp(endTime):FormatUniversalTime('LLL', 'en-US');
        else
            electionEndLabel.Text = 'Election ends at: ' .. DateTime.fromUnixTimestamp(endTime):FormatUniversalTime('LLL', 'en-US');
        end

        if os.time() > endTime then
            electionDecorations.Parent = ServerStorage;
            local winners = ElectionDataService.GetWinners(electionID);

            -- clear the gui so we can populate it
            for _, obj in ipairs(winnersListScrollingFrame:GetChildren()) do
                if obj:IsA('GuiButton') or obj:IsA('GuiLabel') then
                    obj:Destroy();
                end
            end

            for _,v in ipairs(winners) do
                local winnerImage = winnerPreFab:Clone();
                winnerImage.Name = v;
                winnerImage.Parent = winnersListScrollingFrame;
                winnerImage.WinnerLabel.Text = v;
            end;
            winnersListImage.Visible = true;

            if (os.time() - endTime) < 14400 then
                for _,v in workspace.ElectionConfetti:GetDescendants() do
                    if v:IsA('ParticleEmitter') then
                        v.Enabled = true;
                    end;
                end;
            end
        else
            electionDecorations.Parent = workspace;
            winnersListImage.Visible = false;
            for _,v in workspace.ElectionConfetti:GetDescendants() do
                if v:IsA('ParticleEmitter') then
                    v.Enabled = false;
                end;
            end;
        end;
    end;

    while true do
        CheckElection()
        task.wait(math.random(120, 123));
    end
end


function ElectionService:Init()
    CooldownService = self.Shared.CooldownService;
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
	ElectionDataService = self.Modules.ElectionDataService;
    DeveloperCheck = self.Shared.DeveloperCheck;
    NotificationService = self.Services.NotificationService;
    HandshakeService = self.Services.HandshakeService;
    WebUtil = self.Modules.WebUtil;
    ProfileDataService = self.Modules.ProfileDataService;
end


return ElectionService

--[[
    BillboardService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Environment
