-- Billboard Service
-- Khizzer
-- July 11, 2022

local GlobalStorage = require(script.Parent.Parent.Parent.Modules.GlobalStorage);

local BillboardService = {
    Client = {};
    ImageData = {};
}

local MarketplaceService = game:GetService('MarketplaceService');
local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService');

local billboardDatastore = GlobalStorage.new('BillboardData');

local NetworkService;
local MoneyService;

local AD_DURATION = 43200; --12 hours in seconds = 43200

local boards = {};

type BillboardImage = {
    Image: string,
    Player: number,
    Expiry: number,
}

local function SetupBillboard(billboard: BasePart)
    local billboardGUI: SurfaceGui = billboard.BillboardGUI;
    local mainFrame: ImageLabel = billboardGUI.MainFrame;

    local Components = billboardGUI.Components;
    local imagePrefab: ImageLabel = Components.Image;

    for i,v in BillboardService.ImageData do
        BillboardService:AddImage(billboard, v.Image, v.Expiry, v.Player);
    end;

    billboardGUI.Enabled = #mainFrame:GetChildren() > 2;
    billboardGUI.Face = if #mainFrame:GetChildren() > 2 then Enum.NormalId.Back else Enum.NormalId.Right -- this makes the immersive ad be visible

    local adGui = Instance.new('AdGui');
    adGui.Adornee = billboard;
    adGui.Face = Enum.NormalId.Back;
    adGui.Enabled = #BillboardService.ImageData == 0;
    adGui.Name = 'Billboard';
    adGui.FallbackImage = 'rbxassetid://16937126354';
    adGui:AddTag('ImmersiveAd');
    adGui.Parent = billboard;
end;

function BillboardService:AddImage(billboard: BasePart, image: string, expiry: number, player: number)
    local billboardGUI: SurfaceGui = billboard.BillboardGUI;
    local mainFrame: ImageLabel = billboardGUI.MainFrame;

    local Components = billboardGUI.Components;
    local imagePrefab: ImageLabel = Components.Image;

    local image_ = imagePrefab:Clone();
    image_.Image = image;
    image_.Parent = mainFrame;
    image_.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255);

    billboardGUI.Enabled = #mainFrame:GetChildren() > 2;
    billboardGUI.Face = if #mainFrame:GetChildren() > 2 then Enum.NormalId.Back else Enum.NormalId.Right -- this makes the immersive ad be visible

    local adGui = billboard:FindFirstChildOfClass('AdGui');
    adGui.Enabled = #BillboardService.ImageData == 0;
end;

function BillboardService:RemoveImage(billboard: BasePart, image: string)
    local billboardGUI: SurfaceGui = billboard.BillboardGUI;
    local mainFrame: ImageLabel = billboardGUI.MainFrame;

    for _,v in mainFrame:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('ImageLabel') then
            if v.Image == image then
                v:Destroy();
            end;
        end;
    end;

    billboardGUI.Enabled = #mainFrame:GetChildren() > 2;
    billboardGUI.Face = if #mainFrame:GetChildren() > 2 then Enum.NormalId.Back else Enum.NormalId.Right -- this makes the immersive ad be visible

    local adGui = billboard:FindFirstChildOfClass('AdGui');
    adGui.Enabled = #BillboardService.ImageData == 0;
end;

--[[ for _,v in next, CollectionService:GetTagged('Billboard') do
    local mainframe = v:FindFirstChild('MainFrame', true);
    for _,v2 in mainframe:GetChildren() do
        if v2:IsA('ImageLabel') then
            v2:Destroy();
        end
    end
end; ]]

function BillboardService:Start()
    for _,v in CollectionService:GetTagged('Billboard') do
        boards[#boards+1] = v;
    end;

    CollectionService:GetInstanceAddedSignal('Billboard'):Connect(function(billboard)
        SetupBillboard(billboard);
    end);

    for _,v in pairs(boards) do
        SetupBillboard(v);
    end;

    local succ, imageData: {BillboardImage} = pcall(function()
        return billboardDatastore:Get('PurchasedImages');
    end) 
    if succ then
        if not imageData then imageData = {}; end;
        for _, image: BillboardImage in imageData do
            for _, v in boards do
                self:AddImage(v, image.Image, image.Expiry, image.Player);
            end;
        end;
    end;

    NetworkService.Connect('BillboardPurchase', function(plr, assetId)
        if not plr:GetAttribute('OwnsBillboard') == true then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'You need the vBoards gamepass to access this feature.')
            MarketplaceService:PromptPurchase(plr, 60041107);
            return;
        end;

        if plr.Money.Value < 50 then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'You need at least $50 to purchase a billboard ad space.');
            return;
        end;

        for _,v in next, self.ImageData do
            if v.Player == plr.UserId then
                _G.AeroError(plr, 'You already own a billboard image. You can only purchase one every 12 hours.');
                return;
            end;

            if v.Image == assetId then
                _G.AeroError(plr, 'An ad with this image is currently running. Try again later.');
                return;
            end;
        end;

        local _succ, err = pcall(billboardDatastore.Update, billboardDatastore, 'PurchasedImages', function(key)
            if not key then key = {}; end;

            key[#key+1] = {
                Image = assetId,
                Player = plr.UserId,
                Expiry = os.time() + AD_DURATION,
            };

            return key;
        end);

        if not _succ then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'An error occurred while trying to purchase this billboard image. (Code: D1)');
        end;

        self.ImageData[#self.ImageData+1] = {
            Image = assetId,
            Player = plr,
            Expiry = os.time() + AD_DURATION,
        };

        for _,v in boards do
            self:AddImage(v, assetId, os.time() + AD_DURATION, plr.UserId);
        end;

        MoneyService:SubtractMoney(plr, 50);

        NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Notification', 'vBoards', 'You have successfully purchased a billboard image.', nil, 'Green');
    end)

    task.spawn(function()
        while true do
            for i,v in self.ImageData do
                if v.Expiry < os.time() then
                    local _succ, err = pcall(billboardDatastore.Update, billboardDatastore, 'PurchasedImages', function(key)
                        for i3,v3 in key do
                            if v3.Image == v.Image then
                                table.remove(key, i3);
                            end;
                        end;
                        return key;
                    end);

                    if not _succ then warn(err) end;
                    table.remove(self.ImageData, i);
                    for _,v2 in boards do
                        self:RemoveImage(v2, v.Image);
                    end;
                end;
            end;
            task.wait(60)
        end;
    end);

    coroutine.wrap(function()
        while task.wait(45) do
            for _,v in boards do
                local billboardGUI = v.BillboardGUI;
                local mainFrame = billboardGUI.MainFrame;
                local uiPageLayout: UIPageLayout = mainFrame.UIPageLayout;
                uiPageLayout:Next();

				NetworkService.SendAll('BillboardUpdate', uiPageLayout, uiPageLayout.CurrentPage);
            end;
        end;
    end)()
end;

function BillboardService:Init()
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    MoneyService = self.Services.MoneyService;
end;


return BillboardService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Environment/DayCycleService.lua ---

--[[
    DayCycleService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Environment
    Parent: Environment
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local StreetlightService;

local Lighting = game:GetService('Lighting');
local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');
local HttpService = game:GetService('HttpService');

local LENGTH_OF_DAY = 120 * 60;

local DayCycleService = {Client = {}};

local timeTween
local state

function DayCycleService:SetTime(clock: number)
    local myState = HttpService:GenerateGUID()
    state = myState
    if timeTween then
        timeTween:Cancel()
        timeTween:Destroy()
    end

    local timeLeft = LENGTH_OF_DAY - (clock * 120)
    timeTween = TweenService:Create(Lighting, TweenInfo.new(timeLeft, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut), {
        ClockTime = 24
    })

    Lighting.ClockTime = clock
    timeTween:Play()
    timeTween.Completed:Connect(function()
        if state == myState then
            DayCycleService:SetTime(0)
        end
    end)
end

function DayCycleService:Start()
    Lighting:GetPropertyChangedSignal("ClockTime"):Connect(function()
        local clock = Lighting.ClockTime
        local minutes = clock * 120
        StreetlightService.UpdateStreetlights(clock)
        local value
        if minutes >= 360 and minutes < 1080 then -- day time, from 6:00 to 18:00
            local multiplier = math.min(minutes - 360, 15)
            value = 120 + (-50 * math.cos(math.pi * multiplier) / 15)
        else
            local isEvening = minutes >= 1080
            local multiplier = math.min(if isEvening then minutes - 1080 else minutes + 360, 15)
            value = 120 + (50 * math.cos(math.pi * multiplier) / 15)
        end
        local colour = Color3.fromRGB(value, value, value)
        Lighting.Ambient = colour
        Lighting.OutdoorAmbient = colour
        Lighting.Atmosphere.Color = colour
        workspace.Terrain.Clouds.Color = colour
    end)

    DayCycleService:SetTime(7)
end;

function DayCycleService:Init()
    StreetlightService = self.Services.Environment.StreetlightService;
end;

return DayCycleService;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Environment/DoorService.lua ---

--[[
    DoorService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Environment
    Parent: Environment
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService');

local Door;
local DoubleDoors;

local DOOR_TOGGLE_COOLDOWN = 0.02;

local wait;
local coroutineWrap = coroutine.wrap;
local osTime = os.time;

local doors = {};

local function iHateThisStupidDoorSystem(plr, doorModule)
    local doorConfig = doorModule.DoorConfig

    if doorConfig.SpecialCondition then
        if doorConfig.SpecialCondition(plr) then
            return true
        end
        if not doorConfig.GroupCondition and not doorConfig.WhitelistedTeams then return false end
    end

    if doorConfig.GroupCondition then
		if doorConfig.GroupCondition(plr) then
            return true
		end
        if not doorConfig.WhitelistedTeams then return false end;
	end;

    if doorConfig.WhitelistedTeams then
        if plr:GetAttribute('Division') ~= nil then
            if doorConfig.WhitelistedTeams[plr:GetAttribute('Division')] then
                return true
            end;
        end;

        if not doorConfig.WhitelistedTeams[plr.Team.Name] then
            return false
        end;
    end

    return true
end

local function DoorHandler(plr, doorInteractionPart)
    if (plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position - doorInteractionPart.Position).Magnitude > 8 then return; end;
    local doorModule = doors[doorInteractionPart.Parent];

    if iHateThisStupidDoorSystem(plr, doorModule) ~= true then return end

    if doorModule then
        if osTime() - doorModule.LastToggleTime < DOOR_TOGGLE_COOLDOWN then return; end;

        if not doorModule.IsOpen then
            doorModule:Open()
            coroutineWrap(function()
                local tag = osTime();
                doorModule.OpenTag = tag;
                if doorModule.TweenTime then
                    wait(doorModule.TweenTime + (doorModule.WaitTime or 2.6));
                else
                    wait(3);
                end
                if doorModule.OpenTag == tag then
                    doorModule:Close();
                end;
            end)();
        else
            doorModule:Close();
        end;
    end;
end;

local DoorService = {Client = {}};

function DoorService:Start()
	for i, v in next, CollectionService:GetTagged('Door') do
        local door = v.Parent;
        doors[door] = Door.new(door);
    end;

	for i, v in next, CollectionService:GetTagged('DoubleDoors') do
        local doubleDoors = v.Parent;
        doors[doubleDoors] = DoubleDoors.new(doubleDoors);
    end;

    self.Services.NetworkService.Connect('Door', DoorHandler);

    self.Services.NetworkService.Connect('DoubleDoors', DoorHandler);
end;

function DoorService:Init()
    wait = self.Shared.Wait;
    Door = self:WrapModule(require(script:WaitForChild('Door')));
    DoubleDoors = self:WrapModule(require(script:WaitForChild('DoubleDoors')));
end;

return DoorService;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Environment/DoorService_contents/Door.lua ---

--[[
    Door (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Environment → DoorService
    Parent: DoorService
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local NetworkService;

local osTime = os.time;
local GetPlayersWithinRadius;

local Door = {};
Door.__index = Door;

function Door.new(door)
    local self = setmetatable({}, Door);

    local primaryPart = door.PrimaryPart;
    assert(primaryPart, door:GetFullName().. ' has no primary part.')
    local primaryPartCFrame = door.PrimaryPart.CFrame;
    local doorConfig = require(door.DoorConfig);

    self.PrimaryPart = primaryPart;

    self.Door = door;
    self.IsOpen = false;
    self.OpenTag = 0;
    self.LastToggleTime = 0;
    self.OpenedCFrame = primaryPartCFrame * CFrame.Angles(0, math.rad(doorConfig.OpenedAngle), 0);
    self.ClosedCFrame = primaryPartCFrame;
    self.DoorConfig = doorConfig;

    return self;
end;

function Door:Open(speed)
    local nearbyPlayers = GetPlayersWithinRadius(self.PrimaryPart.Position, 600);
    self.NearbyPlayers = nearbyPlayers;
    for _,v in next, self.NearbyPlayers do
        NetworkService.Send(v, 'Door', self.Door, self.OpenedCFrame, self.DoorConfig.OpenSoundID, speed);
    end;
    self.IsOpen = true;
    self.LastToggleTime = osTime();
end;

function Door:Close(speed)
    for _,v in next, self.NearbyPlayers do
        NetworkService.Send(v, 'Door', self.Door, self.ClosedCFrame, self.DoorConfig.CloseSoundID, speed);
    end;
    self.IsOpen = false;
    self.OpenTag = 0;
    self.LastToggleTime = osTime();
end;

function Door:Init()
    GetPlayersWithinRadius = self.Shared.GetPlayersWithinRadius;
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
end;

return Door;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Environment/DoorService_contents/DoubleDoors.lua ---

--[[
    DoubleDoors (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Environment → DoorService
    Parent: DoorService
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local NetworkService;

local osTime = os.time;
local GetPlayersWithinRadius;

local DoubleDoors = {};
DoubleDoors.__index = DoubleDoors;

function DoubleDoors.new(doubleDoors)
    local self = setmetatable({}, DoubleDoors);

    local leftDoor = doubleDoors.LeftDoor;
    local rightDoor = doubleDoors.RightDoor;

    local primaryPart = leftDoor.PrimaryPart;
    assert(primaryPart, leftDoor:GetFullName().. ' has no primary part.');
    self.PrimaryPart = primaryPart;

    local primaryPartR = rightDoor.PrimaryPart;
    assert(primaryPartR, rightDoor:GetFullName().. ' has no primary part.');

    local primaryPartCFrameLeft = doubleDoors.LeftDoor.PrimaryPart.CFrame;
    local primaryPartCFrameRight = doubleDoors.RightDoor.PrimaryPart.CFrame;

    local doorConfig = require(doubleDoors.DoorConfig);

    local openedAngle = math.rad(doorConfig.OpenedAngle);

    self.LeftDoor = leftDoor;
    self.RightDoor = rightDoor;
    self.IsOpen = false;
    self.OpenTag = 0;
    self.LastToggleTime = 0;
    self.OpenedCFrameLeft = primaryPartCFrameLeft * CFrame.Angles(0, openedAngle, 0);
    self.ClosedCFrameLeft = primaryPartCFrameLeft;
    self.OpenedCFrameRight = primaryPartCFrameRight * CFrame.Angles(0, -openedAngle, 0);
    self.ClosedCFrameRight = primaryPartCFrameRight;
    self.DoorConfig = doorConfig;

    if doorConfig.TweenTime then
        self.TweenTime = doorConfig.TweenTime;
    end;

    return self;
end;

function DoubleDoors:Open()
    self.NearbyPlayers = GetPlayersWithinRadius(self.PrimaryPart.Position, 600);
    for _,v in next, self.NearbyPlayers do
        NetworkService.Send(v, 'DoubleDoors', self.LeftDoor, self.RightDoor, self.OpenedCFrameLeft, self.OpenedCFrameRight, self.DoorConfig.OpenSoundID, self.TweenTime);
    end;

    self.IsOpen = true;
    self.LastToggleTime = osTime();
end;

function DoubleDoors:Close()
    for _,v in next, self.NearbyPlayers do
        NetworkService.Send(v, 'DoubleDoors', self.LeftDoor, self.RightDoor, self.ClosedCFrameLeft, self.ClosedCFrameRight, self.DoorConfig.CloseSoundID, self.TweenTime);
    end;

    self.IsOpen = false;
    self.OpenTag = 0;
    self.LastToggleTime = osTime();
end;

function DoubleDoors:Init()
    GetPlayersWithinRadius = self.Shared.GetPlayersWithinRadius;
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
end;

return DoubleDoors;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Environment/FireService.lua ---

--[[
    FireService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Environment
    Parent: Environment
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Fire Service
-- Khizzer
-- September 27, 2021



local FireService = {
	FireCount = 0;
};

local Teams = game:GetService("Teams");
local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService');

local DispatchService;
local FastRemoveFirstValue;
local RegionalAlarmService;

local Fire;

local POSSIBLE_FIRES = CollectionService:GetTagged('PossibleFire');

local VFRS_TEAM: Team = game.Teams['Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service'];

--Recursive function which picks a random fire to start up to a maximum of 3 tries
local function chooseRandomFire(attemptNumber: number, attemptLimit: number): Instance?
	local randomFire = POSSIBLE_FIRES[math.random(1, #POSSIBLE_FIRES)];
	if #POSSIBLE_FIRES == 0 then return; end;

	local running = randomFire:GetAttribute('Running')
	local enoughFirefighters = #VFRS_TEAM:GetPlayers() >= (randomFire:GetAttribute("MinimumFirefighters") or 2)

	if running or not enoughFirefighters then
		if attemptNumber == attemptLimit then
			return; --Give up, try again in next cycle
		end;
		return chooseRandomFire(attemptNumber + 1, attemptLimit);
	end;

	return randomFire;
end;

function FireService:CreateFire(attemptLimit)
	local randomFire = chooseRandomFire(1, attemptLimit or 100);
	if not randomFire then return; end;

	self.FireCount = self.FireCount + 1;

	local newFire = Fire.new(randomFire);

	for _,v in next, randomFire:GetDescendants() do
		if v:IsA('BasePart') and v:GetAttribute('FirePart') then
		local isSmokePart = v:GetAttribute('SmokePart');
		newFire:BurnPart(v, isSmokePart);
		end;
	end;

	local connection
	connection = newFire.FireEndedSignal:Connect(function()
		connection:Disconnect();
		self.FireCount = math.max(self.FireCount - 1, 0);
		randomFire:SetAttribute('Running', false);
	end);

	RegionalAlarmService:AlarmOn('FireStation', 10)

	local callDetails: string = randomFire:GetAttribute('CallDetails');

	local location = callDetails:match("{(.-)}");

	callDetails = callDetails:gsub("{", ""):gsub("}", "");

	DispatchService:CreateCall('DISPATCH - FIRE', location, callDetails);
end;

function FireService:Start()
	while task.wait(500) do
		if workspace:GetAttribute("NoFires") then return end
		if self.FireCount < 2 then
			self:CreateFire(3);
		else
			continue;
		end;
	end;
end;

function FireService:Init()
	Fire = self.Modules.Fire;
	DispatchService = self.Services.DispatchService;
	RegionalAlarmService = self.Services.RegionalAlarmService;
end;

return FireService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Environment/GateService.lua ---

--[[
    GateService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Environment
    Parent: Environment
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService');

local SlidingGate;
local BoomGate;
local RotatingGate;
local PartToRegion3;

local MAX_REGION_PARTS = 200;

local coroutineWrap = coroutine.wrap;
local findPartsInRegion3WithWhitelist = workspace.FindPartsInRegion3WithWhiteList;

local carsFolder = workspace:WaitForChild('Cars');

local GateService = {Client = {}};

local rotatingGates = {};
local controllableBoomGates = {};
local toggleableGates = {};

local NetworkService;

local GATE_TOGGLE_COOLDOWN = 0.02;

local HttpService = game:GetService('HttpService');

function GateService:Start()
	for i, v in next, CollectionService:GetTagged('SlidingGate') do
        local gate = SlidingGate.new(v.Gate);
        -- local detectionRegion = PartToRegion3(v.DetectionRegion);
        local ShouldOpenGate = require(v.SlidingGateConfig);
        coroutineWrap(function()
            while true do
                local found = false;
                -- for i2, v2 in next, findPartsInRegion3WithWhitelist(workspace, detectionRegion, carsFolder:GetChildren(), MAX_REGION_PARTS) do
                for i2, v2 in next, workspace:GetPartsInPart(v.DetectionRegion) do
                    if ShouldOpenGate(v2) then
                        if not gate.IsOpen then
                            gate:Open();
                        end;
                        found = true;
                        break;
                    end;
                end;
                if (not found) and (gate.IsOpen) then
                    gate:Close();
                end;
                task.wait(0.4);
            end;
        end)();
    end;

	for i, v in next, CollectionService:GetTagged('BoomGate') do
        local gate = BoomGate.new(v.Gate);

        local boomGateConfig = require(v.BoomGateConfig);
        local ShouldOpenGate = boomGateConfig.ShouldOpenGate;
        local controllable = boomGateConfig.Controllable;
        if not controllable then
            -- local detectionRegion = PartToRegion3(v.DetectionRegion);
            coroutineWrap(function()
                while true do
                    local found = false;
                    -- for i2, v2 in next, findPartsInRegion3WithWhitelist(workspace, detectionRegion, carsFolder:GetChildren(), MAX_REGION_PARTS) do
                    for i2, v2 in next, workspace:GetPartsInPart(v.DetectionRegion) do
                        if ShouldOpenGate(v2) then
                            if not gate.IsOpen then
                                gate:Open();
                            end;
                            found = true;
                            break;
                        end;
                    end;
                    if (not found) and (gate.IsOpen) then
                        gate:Close();
                    end;
                    task.wait(0.4);
                end;
            end)();
        else
            controllableBoomGates[v.Gate] = gate;
            gate.LastToggleTime = 0;
        end
    end;

    for i, v in next, CollectionService:GetTagged('RotatingGate') do
        for _,v2: BasePart in next, v:GetDescendants() do
            if v2:IsA('BasePart') then
                if v2.Anchored == false then
                    local ok, err = pcall(v2.SetNetworkOwner, v2)
                    if not ok then
                        warn(`Could not set part {v2:GetFullName()}: {err}`)
                    end
                end;
            end;
        end;
        local gate = RotatingGate.new(v.Gate);
        rotatingGates[v.Gate] = gate;
--[[         local detectionRegion = PartToRegion3(v.DetectionRegion);
        local ShouldOpenGate = require(v.RotatingGateConfig).ShouldOpenGate;
        coroutineWrap(function()
            while true do
                local found = false;
                for i2, v2 in next, findPartsInRegion3WithWhitelist(workspace, detectionRegion, carsFolder:GetChildren(), MAX_REGION_PARTS) do
                    if ShouldOpenGate(v2) then
                        if not gate.IsOpen then
                            gate:Open();
                        end;
                        found = true;
                        break;
                    end;
                end;
                if (not found) and (gate.IsOpen) then
                    gate:Close();
                end;
                task.wait(0.4);
            end;
        end)(); ]]
    end;

    for _,v in next, CollectionService:GetTagged('ToggleableGate') do
        local gate = ToggleableGate.new(v.Gate);
        local gateName = HttpService:GenerateGUID();

        toggleableGates[gateName] = gate;
        gate.ToggleableGateModel:SetAttribute('Name', gateName);
    end;

    NetworkService.Connect('ToggleableGate', function(plr, gate: Model)
        local gateModule = toggleableGates[gate:GetAttribute('Name')];

        if os.time() - gateModule.LastToggleTime < GATE_TOGGLE_COOLDOWN then return; end;

        local gateConfig = require(gateModule.ToggleableGateConfig);
        if gateConfig.WhitelistedTeams and not gateConfig.WhitelistedTeams[plr.Team.Name]
            and not gateConfig.WhitelistedTeams[plr:GetAttribute('Division') or 'h']
        then return; end;
        if gateConfig.ShouldOpenGate and not gateConfig.ShouldOpenGate(plr) then return end

        if gateModule.IsOpen then
            gateModule:Close();
        else
            gateModule:Open();
        end;
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('ROTATING_GATE', function(plr, gate: Model)
        local gateModule = rotatingGates[gate.Gate];
        if os.time() - gateModule.LastToggleTime < GATE_TOGGLE_COOLDOWN then return; end;

        local gateConfig = require(gate.RotatingGateConfig);
        local check = gateConfig.ShouldOpenGate;

        if not check(plr) then return; end;

        if gateModule.IsOpen then
            gateModule:Close()
        else
            gateModule:Open();
        end;
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('BOOM_GATE', function(plr, gate: Model)
        local gateModule = controllableBoomGates[gate.Gate];
        if os.time() - gateModule.LastToggleTime < GATE_TOGGLE_COOLDOWN then return; end;

        local gateConfig = require(gate.BoomGateConfig);
        local check = gateConfig.ShouldOpenGate;

        if not check(plr) then return; end;

        if gateModule.IsOpen then
            gateModule:Close()
            gateModule.LastToggleTime = os.time();
        else
            gateModule:Open();
            gateModule.LastToggleTime = os.time();
        end;
    end)
end;

function GateService:Init()
    SlidingGate = self:WrapModule(require(script:WaitForChild('SlidingGate')));
    BoomGate = self:WrapModule(require(script:WaitForChild('BoomGate')));
    RotatingGate = self:WrapModule(require(script:WaitForChild('RotatingGate')));
    ToggleableGate = self:WrapModule(require(script:WaitForChild('ToggleableGate')));
    PartToRegion3 = self.Shared.PartToRegion3;
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
end;

return GateService;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Environment/GateService_contents/BoomGate.lua ---

--[[
    BoomGate (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Environment → GateService
    Parent: GateService
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local NetworkService;

local BoomGate = {};
BoomGate.__index = BoomGate;

function BoomGate.new(gate)
    local self = setmetatable({}, BoomGate);

    local primaryPartCFrame = gate.PrimaryPart.CFrame;

    self.Gate = gate;
    self.IsOpen = false;
    self.OpenedCFrame = primaryPartCFrame * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, math.rad(require(gate.Parent.BoomGateConfig).OpenedAngle));
    self.ClosedCFrame = primaryPartCFrame;

    return self;
end;

function BoomGate:Open()
    NetworkService.SendAll('BoomGate', self.Gate, self.OpenedCFrame);
    self.IsOpen = true;
end;

function BoomGate:Close()
    NetworkService.SendAll('BoomGate', self.Gate, self.ClosedCFrame);
    self.IsOpen = false;
end;

function BoomGate:Init()
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
end;

return BoomGate;

--[[
    RotatingGate (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Environment → GateService

    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script

-- Rotating Gate
-- Khizzer
-- February 6, 2022



local RotatingGate = {}
RotatingGate.__index = RotatingGate;

function RotatingGate.new(gate)
    local self = setmetatable({}, RotatingGate);

    self.PrimaryPart = gate.PrimaryPart;
    self.Gate = gate;
    self.IsOpen = false;
    self.LastToggleTime = 0;

    local cylindricalConstraint: CylindricalConstraint = gate.PrimaryPart:FindFirstChildOfClass('CylindricalConstraint');

    self.CylindricalConstraint = cylindricalConstraint;
    self.ClosedTargetPosition = cylindricalConstraint.TargetPosition;
    self.ClosedTargetAngle = cylindricalConstraint.TargetAngle;
    
    local gateConfig = require(gate.Parent.RotatingGateConfig);
    self.OpenedTargetPosition = gateConfig.OpenedTargetPosition;
    self.OpenedTargetAngle = gateConfig.OpenedTargetAngle;

    return self;
end;

function RotatingGate:Open()
    self.CylindricalConstraint.TargetAngle = self.OpenedTargetAngle;
    self.CylindricalConstraint.TargetPosition = self.OpenedTargetPosition;
    self.IsOpen = true;
    self.LastToggleTime = os.time();

    self.PrimaryPart.CanCollide = false;
end;

function RotatingGate:Close()
    self.CylindricalConstraint.TargetAngle = self.ClosedTargetAngle;
    self.CylindricalConstraint.TargetPosition = self.ClosedTargetPosition;
    self.IsOpen = false;
    self.LastToggleTime = os.time();
    self.PrimaryPart.CanCollide = true;
end

return RotatingGate

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Environment/MetalDetectorService.lua ---

--[[
    MetalDetectorService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Environment
    Parent: Environment
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local CollectionService = game:GetService("CollectionService")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")

local MetalDetectorService = {}

local DefaultColour = BrickColor.new('Light stone grey')
local DangerousModules = {'Gun', 'MeleeWeapon', 'Baton', 'RiotShield', 'PepperGun', 'PepperSpray', 'RadarGun', 'Taser'}
local DangerousNames = {'Fireworks', 'Handcuffs', 'RemoteMine', 'Bomb', 'C4'}

type MetalDetector = Part & {
  Safe: Sound,
  Danger: Sound,
  Parent: Model & {
    Light: (Part | UnionOperation)?
  }
}

local function isDangerous(tool: Tool)
  return table.find(DangerousModules, tool:GetAttribute("Module")) or table.find(DangerousNames, tool.Name)
end

local function scan(container)
  for _, tool in container:GetChildren() do
    if tool:IsA("Tool") then
      if isDangerous(tool) then return true end
    end
  end
  return false
end

local function quickSound(sound: Sound)
  local clone = sound:Clone()
  clone.PlayOnRemove = true
  clone.Parent = sound.Parent
  clone:Destroy()
end

local function setup(detector: MetalDetector)
  local model = detector.Parent
  local light = model:FindFirstChild("Light")
  local safeSound = detector.Safe
  local alertSound = detector.Danger
  local state = 0
  local alert = false

  local function indicate(danger: boolean)
    if not light then
      quickSound(if danger then alertSound else safeSound)
      return
    end

    local myState = tick()
    if state ~= 0 then
      if not danger then return end
      if danger and alert then return end
    end

    state = myState
    alert = danger
    local color = if danger then BrickColor.new('Bright red') else BrickColor.new('Lime green')
    light.BrickColor = color
    quickSound(if danger then alertSound else safeSound)

    if danger then
      task.delay(0.219, function()
        if state == myState then
          quickSound(alertSound)
        end
      end)

      for _ = 1, 5 do
        if state ~= myState then return end
        light.BrickColor = DefaultColour

        task.wait(0.1)
        if state ~= myState then return end

        light.BrickColor = color
        task.wait(0.1)
      end
    else
      task.wait(0.2)
      for _ = 1, 2 do
        if state ~= myState then return end
        light.BrickColor = DefaultColour

        task.wait(0.2)
        if state ~= myState then return end
        light.BrickColor = color
        task.wait(0.2)
      end
    end

    light.BrickColor = DefaultColour
    state = 0
  end

  detector.Touched:Connect(function(obj)
    local character = obj.Parent
    local humanoid = character and character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
    local player = humanoid and Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(humanoid.Parent)
    if not player then return end
    if character:GetAttribute("Scanned") and tick() - character:GetAttribute("Scanned") < 3 then
      return
    end
    character:SetAttribute("Scanned", tick())

    local detected = scan(character)
    detected = detected or scan(player)
    detected = detected or (player.Backpack and scan(player.Backpack))

    if not detected then
      indicate(false)
    else
      indicate(true)
    end
  end)
end

function MetalDetectorService:Start()
  CollectionService:GetInstanceAddedSignal("MetalDetector", setup)
  for _, x in CollectionService:GetTagged("MetalDetector") do
    setup(x)
  end
end

return MetalDetectorService

    PrisonCellService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Environment
    Parent: Environment
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53

local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
-- Prison Cell Service
-- Khizzer
-- December 31, 2021



local PrisonCellService = {}
local NetworkService;
local PrisonCell;
local DeveloperCheck;

local cells = {};

local osTime = os.time;

local original = workspace:WaitForChild("PrisonCells")
local clone = original and original:Clone()
if clone then
    if ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("PrisonCells") then
        ReplicatedStorage.PrisonCells:Destroy()
    end

    clone.Parent = ReplicatedStorage
end

function PrisonCellService:Start()
    for _,v in next, workspace.PrisonCells:GetChildren() do
        cells[v.Main] = PrisonCell.new(v.Main)
    end

    NetworkService.Connect('PrisonCell', function(plr, cell)
        cell = workspace.PrisonCells[cell];
        cell.Main.PrimaryPart:FindFirstChildOfClass('Sound'):Play();
        if not plr.Team == game.Teams['Correctional Service Canada'] and not DeveloperCheck(plr) then return; end;
        local cellModule = cells[cell.Main];
        if osTime() - cellModule.LastToggleTime < 2.3 then return; end;
        if cellModule then
            if not cellModule.IsOpen then
                cellModule:Open();
            else
                cellModule:Close();
            end;
        end;
    end);
end;

function PrisonCellService:Init()
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    PrisonCell = self:WrapModule(require(script.PrisonCell));
    DeveloperCheck = self.Shared.DeveloperCheck;
end;


return PrisonCellService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Environment/SnowService.lua ---

--[[
    SnowService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Environment
    Parent: Environment
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
-- Snow Service
-- Khizzer
-- November 20, 2022

local SnowService = {}

local NetworkService;
local MathUtil;

function SnowService:Start()
    NetworkService.Connect('SalterToggle', function(plr, interactionPart)
        if plr.Team.Name ~= 'Translink' then return; end;
        if typeof(interactionPart) ~= 'Instance' then return; end;

        local particlePart = interactionPart.Parent.ParticlePart;
        local sound = particlePart.Sound;
        local particleEmitter = particlePart.ParticleEmitter;

        local onSwitch = interactionPart.Parent.On;
        local offSwitch = interactionPart.Parent.Off;

        particleEmitter.Enabled = not particleEmitter.Enabled;

        if particleEmitter.Enabled then
            sound:Play();
        else
            sound:Stop();
        end;

        onSwitch.Material = particleEmitter.Enabled and Enum.Material.Neon or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
        offSwitch.Material = (not particleEmitter.Enabled) and Enum.Material.Neon or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
    end)

    local beginSnowDecline = DateTime.fromUniversalTime(2024, 1, 19, 14, 25, 0, 0).UnixTimestamp
    local minimalSnow = DateTime.fromUniversalTime(2024, 2, 2, 0, 0, 0, 0).UnixTimestamp
    local stopSnowDecline = DateTime.fromUniversalTime(2024, 2, 3, 12, 30, 0, 0).UnixTimestamp
    if stopSnowDecline < os.time() then return end -- Stop snow generation
    local snowHeight = MathUtil.Map(os.time(), minimalSnow, beginSnowDecline, 0, 1)

    print(`---\nSnow height: {snowHeight}\n---`)

    local function generateSnow(childName: string)
        if workspace:FindFirstChild(childName) then
            for _, v in ipairs(workspace[childName]:GetDescendants()) do
                if v:IsA('Part') then
                    local size = v.Size;
                    local cframe = v.CFrame;

                    if v.Shape == Enum.PartType.Block then
                        workspace.Terrain:FillBlock(v.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -0.1, 0), v.Size + Vector3.new(0, snowHeight, 0), Enum.Material.Sand);
                    elseif v.Shape == Enum.PartType.Cylinder then
                        local cframe_fix = cframe * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, math.rad(90));
                        local height = size.X - 0.48;
                        local radius = math.min(size.Y, size.Z) / 2;
                        workspace.Terrain:FillCylinder(cframe_fix, height, radius, Enum.Material.Sand);
                    end;
                elseif v:IsA('WedgePart') then
                    workspace.Terrain:FillWedge(v.CFrame, v.Size, Enum.Material.Sand);
                end;
            end;
        end;
    end;

    if not RunService:IsStudio() then
        generateSnow('Snow');
        generateSnow('Roads');
    end
end;



function SnowService:Init()
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    MathUtil = self.Shared.MathUtil;
end;


return SnowService;

    SpikeStripService (ModuleScript)

local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService');

local function CreateTirePopSound(part)
    local tirePopSound = Instance.new('Sound');
    tirePopSound.SoundId = 'rbxassetid://2694245144';
    tirePopSound.Volume = 0.7;
    tirePopSound.PlayOnRemove = true;
    tirePopSound.Parent = part;
    tirePopSound:Destroy();
end;

local function SetupSpikeStrip(spikeStrip)
    if not spikeStrip:IsDescendantOf(workspace) then return; end;

    local hitbox = spikeStrip.Hitbox;

    hitbox.Touched:Connect(function(hit)
        if (hit.Name == 'Wheel') and (hit.CanCollide) then
            hit.CanCollide = false;
            CreateTirePopSound(primaryPart);
        end;
    end);
end

local SpikeStripService = {Client = {}};

function SpikeStripService:Start()
    for i, v in next, CollectionService:GetTagged('SpikeStrip') do
        SetupSpikeStrip(v);
    end;

    CollectionService:GetInstanceAddedSignal('SpikeStrip'):Connect(SetupSpikeStrip);
end;

function SpikeStripService:Init()

end;

return SpikeStripService;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Environment/StreetlightService.lua ---

--[[
    StreetlightService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Environment
    Parent: Environment
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService');
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

local SMOOTH_MATERIAL = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
local NEON_MATERIAL = Enum.Material.Neon;

local tableRemove = table.remove;

local RandomDecimal;
local RegionalAlarmService;

local streetlights = CollectionService:GetTagged('Streetlight');
local areStreetlightsEnabled = false;

local glowingWindows = false;

local windows = CollectionService:GetTagged('GlowingPart');

local function SetStreetlight(streetlight, enabled)
    local light = streetlight.Light;
    light.Material = enabled and NEON_MATERIAL or SMOOTH_MATERIAL;
    light.Light.Enabled = enabled;
    light.LightBeam.Enabled = enabled;
end;

local StreetlightService = {Client = {}};
local NetworkService;

function StreetlightService.UpdateStreetlights(clockTime)
    if (clockTime > 17.5) or (clockTime < 6.2) then
        if not areStreetlightsEnabled then
            for i, v in next, streetlights do
                SetStreetlight(v, true);
                ReplicatedStorage.GasPrice.Value = RandomDecimal(1, 3);
            end;
            NetworkService.SendAll('AmbientSound', 'Night');
            areStreetlightsEnabled = true;
        end;
        if not glowingWindows then
            for i, v in windows do
                v.Material = NEON_MATERIAL;
            end;
            glowingWindows = true;
        end;
    elseif areStreetlightsEnabled then
        for i, v in next, streetlights do
            SetStreetlight(v, false);
        end;
        areStreetlightsEnabled = false;
        NetworkService.SendAll('AmbientSound', 'Day');
        if glowingWindows then
            for i, v in windows do
                v.Material = SMOOTH_MATERIAL;
            end;
            glowingWindows = false;
        end;
    end;

    if not RegionalAlarmService:GetAlarmStatus('CFB') then
        for _, v in CollectionService:GetTagged('CFBFloodlight') do
            v.Material = if (clockTime > 17.5) or (clockTime < 6.2) then Enum.Material.Neon else Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic
            v.Light.Enabled = (clockTime > 17.5) or (clockTime < 6.2)
            v.LightBeam.Enabled = (clockTime > 17.5) or (clockTime < 6.2)
            v.SurfaceLight.Enabled = (clockTime > 17.5) or (clockTime < 6.2)
        end
    end
end;

function StreetlightService:Start()
    CollectionService:GetInstanceAddedSignal('Streetlight'):Connect(function(streetlight)
        streetlights[#streetlights + 1] = streetlight;
    end);

    CollectionService:GetInstanceRemovedSignal('Streetlight'):Connect(function(streetlight)
		for i, v in next, streetlights do
			if v == streetlight then
				tableRemove(streetlights, i);
			end;
		end;
    end);
end;

function StreetlightService:Init()
    RandomDecimal = self.Shared.NumberUtil.RandomDecimal;
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    RegionalAlarmService = self.Services.RegionalAlarmService;
end;

return StreetlightService;

--[[
    WeatherService (ModuleScript)

local NetworkService;
local WeatherService = {Client = {}};

local random = Random.new()

type AtmosphereData = {
    Haze: number;
    Color: Color3;
    Density: number;
}

type RainData = {
    Enabled: boolean;
    IntensityRatio: number?;
    StraightTexture: string?;
    TopDownTexture: string?;
};

type CloudData = {
    Density: number;
    Cover: number;
};

type WeatherData = {
    Atmosphere: AtmosphereData;
    Rain: RainData?;
    Clouds: CloudData;
    Probability: number;
    Snow: boolean?;
};

local WeatherTemplates: {[string]: WeatherData} = {
    ['Clear'] = {
        Atmosphere = {

            Density = 0.2;
            Color = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200);

    };

    ['Light Rain'] = {

        };

    };

    ['Thunderstorm'] = {
        Atmosphere = {

            Color = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150);
        };
        Rain = {
            Enabled = true;
            IntensityRatio = 0.7;
            Thunder = true;
        };
        Clouds = {

            Cover = 0.8;
        };
        Probability = 0.09
    };

    ['Cloudy'] = {
        Atmosphere = {

            Color = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200);
        };

}

local function SelectRandomWeather(): WeatherData
    local possibleWeathers = {};
    for _, weather in pairs(WeatherTemplates) do
        if random:NextNumber(0, 1) < weather.Probability then
            table.insert(possibleWeathers, weather);
        end;
    end;
    if #possibleWeathers > 0 then
        return possibleWeathers[random:NextInteger(1, #possibleWeathers)];
    end;
    return WeatherTemplates['Clear'];
end;

local thundering = false;

function WeatherService.EnableThunder(state)
    thundering = state;
end;

function WeatherService:Start()
    local currentWeather = SelectRandomWeather();
    NetworkService.SendAll('InitialWeather', currentWeather);

    NetworkService.ConnectFunction('GetInitialWeather', function()
        return currentWeather;
    end);

    task.spawn(function()
        while true do
            if thundering then
                NetworkService.SendAll('Thunder');
            end;
            task.wait(60);
        end;
    end);

    while true do
        task.wait(math.random(300, 700));
        local newWeather = SelectRandomWeather();
        if newWeather ~= currentWeather then
            currentWeather = newWeather;
            local tweenTime = math.random(120, 180);
            NetworkService.SendAll('onWeatherChange', currentWeather, tweenTime);
        end;
        if newWeather.Rain.Thunderstorm then
            self.EnableThunder(true)
        else
            self.EnableThunder(false)
        end;
    end;
end;

function WeatherService:Init()
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
end;

return WeatherService;

--[[
    EvidenceDisposalService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")

local EvidenceDisposalService = {Client = {}};

local NetworkService;
local WebUtil;
local CheckLEO;

function EvidenceDisposalService:Start()
    NetworkService.Connect('EvidenceDisposal', function(plr)
        if not CheckLEO(plr) and plr:GetAttribute('Division') ~= 'GCPS' then return; end;

        local character = plr.Character;
        if not character then return; end;

        local tool = character:FindFirstChildOfClass('Tool')
        if not tool then return; end;

        local toolSource = tool:GetAttribute('ToolSource') or 'None';
        local toolName = tool.Name;
        local attributes = tool:GetAttributes();
        attributes.ToolSource = nil
        attributes.UserName = nil

        tool.Parent = nil

        local data = {
            embeds = {
                {
                    title = "Evidence Disposal",
                    fields = {
                        {
                            name = "Officer",
                            value = plr.Name
                        },
                        {
                            name = "Tool Name",
                            value = toolName
                        },
                        {
                            name = "Tool Source",
                            value = toolSource
                        },
                        {
                            name = "Raw Tool Attributes",
                            value = HttpService:JSONEncode(attributes)
                        },
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        local err = WebUtil.SendWebhook("https://webhook.lewisakura.moe/api/webhooks/1118634203278479370/sRLteXox8NNvrl3gLjrTVIPb7kmFq8KSLSQs1UWyivv8IFSmiA_kHnHQcP2ewLwEzxDi", "1118628183177175080", data)
        if err == nil then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Notification', 'Evidence Disposal', `Successfully disposed of {toolName}`);
            tool:Destroy()
            return
        end

        warn(`Could not log evidence disposal: {err}`)
        tool.Parent = plr.Backpack
        _G.AeroError(plr, "This action could not be logged and has been aborted. Please try again or alert a developer.")
    end)
end;

function EvidenceDisposalService:Init()
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    WebUtil = self.Modules.WebUtil;
    CheckLEO = self.Shared.Constants.WhitelistedTeams.CheckLEO;
end;

return EvidenceDisposalService;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/FirefighterService.lua ---

--[[
    FirefighterService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Fire Pole Service
-- Khizzer
-- March 29, 2022

local NetworkService;
local FIRE_GEAR_PREFAB;

local FirefighterService = {Client = {}, HiddenHats = {}}

local VFRS_TEAM = game:GetService('Teams')['Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service'];

local function weldParts(part0, part1)
    local weld = Instance.new('WeldConstraint');
    weld.Part0 = part0;
    weld.Part1 = part1;
    weld.Parent = part0;
end;

function FirefighterService:Start()
    NetworkService.Connect('GetFireGear', function(plr: Player, interactionPart: BasePart)
        if plr.Team ~= VFRS_TEAM then return; end;
        if plr.Character:FindFirstChild('FireGear') then return; end;

        if typeof(interactionPart) ~= "Instance" then return; end;
        if not interactionPart:IsA('BasePart') then return; end;

        if plr.Character:FindFirstChild('FireGear') then return _G.AeroError(plr, 'You already have fire gear!');  end;

        local helmetColour: Color3 = interactionPart:GetAttribute('HelmetColour');
        if not helmetColour then return; end;

        if not self.HiddenHats[plr] then
            self.HiddenHats[plr] = {};
        end;

        for _,v in next, plr.Character:GetChildren() do
            if v:IsA('Accessory') then
                table.insert(self.HiddenHats[plr], v);
                v.Parent = nil;
            end;
        end;

        local newGear = FIRE_GEAR_PREFAB:Clone();

        for _,v in next, newGear:GetChildren() do
            local primaryPartName = v.PrimaryPart.Name;

            v:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(plr.Character[primaryPartName].CFrame);

            weldParts(v.PrimaryPart, plr.Character[primaryPartName]);

            for _,v2 in next, v:GetDescendants() do
                if v2:IsA('BasePart') then
                    weldParts(v2, v.PrimaryPart);
                    v2:SetAttribute('OriginalTransparency', v2.Transparency);
                end;
            end;

            for _,v2 in next, v:GetDescendants() do
                if v2:IsA('BasePart') then
                    v2.Massless = true;
                    v2.CanCollide = false;
                    v2.Anchored = false;
                end;
            end;
        end;

        newGear.Helmet.Colour.Color = helmetColour;

        newGear.Parent = plr.Character;

        NetworkService.Send(plr, 'FireGearGUI');
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('FireGear', function(plr, gearNameToToggle)
        if plr.Team ~= VFRS_TEAM then return; end;

        local fireGear = plr.Character:FindFirstChild('FireGear');
        if not fireGear then return; end;

        local gearToToggle = fireGear:FindFirstChild(gearNameToToggle);
        if not gearToToggle then return; end;

        for _,v in next, gearToToggle:GetDescendants() do
            if v:IsA('BasePart') and v ~= gearToToggle.PrimaryPart then
                local setToOff = v.Transparency == v:GetAttribute('OriginalTransparency');
                if setToOff then
                    v.Transparency = 1;
                else
                    v.Transparency = v:GetAttribute('OriginalTransparency');
                end
            end;
        end;
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('VFRS_ToggleOriginalHats', function(plr)
        if plr.Team ~= VFRS_TEAM then return; end;

        local originalHats = self.HiddenHats[plr];
        if not originalHats then return; end;

        local hatsAreHidden = plr.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass('Accessory') == nil;

        if hatsAreHidden then
            for _,v in next, originalHats do
                if v:IsA('Accessory') then
                    v.Parent = plr.Character;
                end;
            end;
        else
            for _,v in next, originalHats do
                if v:IsA('Accessory') then
                    v.Parent = nil;
                end;
            end;
        end
    end)
end


function FirefighterService:Init()
    FIRE_GEAR_PREFAB = self.ServerAssets.FireGear;
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
end


return FirefighterService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/GangService.lua ---

--[[
    GangService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
-- Gang Service
-- Khizzer
-- May 21, 2022



local GangService = {Client = {}}

local NetworkService;
local GangStorage;
local FilterStringAsync;

local function SetupMember(member: Player, gangName: string, memberRank: string)
    local gangFolder = GangStorage:FindFirstChild(gangName);
    if not gangFolder then return; end;
    local memberFolder = gangFolder:FindFirstChild(member.Name);
    if memberFolder then warn('GangService: Attempting to make a member that already exists.', member.Name); return; end;

    local membersFolder: Folder = gangFolder.Members;

    local playerValue = Instance.new('ObjectValue');
    playerValue.Name = member.Name;
    playerValue.Value = member;
    playerValue.Parent = membersFolder;

    playerValue:SetAttribute('Rank', memberRank);
    playerValue:SetAttribute('Notoriety', 0);

    member:SetAttribute('Gang', gangName);
end;

local function CreateGang(gangName: string, leader: Player): nil
    local GangFolder = Instance.new('Folder');
    GangFolder.Name = gangName;
    GangFolder.Parent = GangStorage;
    GangFolder:SetAttribute('Notoriety', 0);
    GangFolder:SetAttribute('Leader', leader.Name);

    local members = Instance.new('Folder');
    members.Name = 'Members';
    members.Parent = GangFolder;

    SetupMember(leader, gangName, 'Leader');
end;

function GangService:RemovePlayer(player: Player)
    local gang = player:GetAttribute('Gang');
    if not gang then return; end;

    local gangFolder = GangStorage:FindFirstChild(gang);
    if not gangFolder then return; end;

    local playerStats = gangFolder.Members:FindFirstChild(player.Name);
    if not playerStats then return; end;

    playerStats:Destroy();
    player:SetAttribute('Gang', nil);
end;

function GangService:DisbandGang(gangName: string)
    local gangFolder = GangStorage:FindFirstChild(gangName);
    if not gangFolder then return; end;

    --Notify each member that they have been kicked
    for _, member in pairs(gangFolder.Members:GetChildren()) do
        member.Value:SetAttribute('Gang', nil);
        NetworkService.Send(member.Value, 'Notification', 'Gang Disbanded', 'Your gang has been disbanded.');
    end;
end;

function GangService:IsPlayerInGang(player: Player): boolean
    return player:GetAttribute('Gang') ~= nil;
end;

function GangService:AddNotoriety(player: Player, notorietyIncrement: number)
    local playerStats = GangStorage:FindFirstChild(player.Name, true);
    if not playerStats then return; end;

    local notoriety = playerStats:GetAttribute('Notoriety');
    playerStats:SetAttribute('Notoriety', notoriety + notorietyIncrement);

    local gangFolder = playerStats.Parent.Parent;
    gangFolder:SetAttribute('Notoriety', gangFolder:GetAttribute('Notoriety') + notorietyIncrement);
end;

function GangService:GetGangInfo(gangName: string)
    local gangFolder = GangStorage:FindFirstChild(gangName);
    if not gangFolder then return; end;

    local leader;

    local members = {};
    for _, member in pairs(gangFolder.Members:GetChildren()) do
        table.insert(members, member.Name);
        if member:GetAttribute('Rank') == 'Leader' then
            leader = member.Name;
        end;
    end;

    return {
        Name = gangName;
        Members = #members;
        Notoriety = gangFolder:GetAttribute('Notoriety');
        Leader = leader;
    };
end;

function GangService:GetGangFromPlayer(player: Player)
    local gang = player:GetAttribute('Gang');
    if gang then
        return self:GetGangInfo(gang);
    end;
end;

function GangService:Start()
--[[     repeat task.wait() until game.Players:FindFirstChild('kh1zzer');
	CreateGang('GangShoux', game.Players.kh1zzer); ]]

    NetworkService.ConnectFunction('GetOtherGangData', function(plr)
        if not plr.Team.Name == 'Civilian' and not plr.Team == 'Prisoner' then return; end;

        local gangs = {};

        for _,v in next, GangStorage:GetChildren() do
            local info = self:GetGangInfo(v.Name);
            if info then table.insert(gangs, info); end;
        end;

        return gangs;
    end)

    NetworkService.ConnectFunction('GetMyGangData', function(plr)
        local gang = plr:GetAttribute('Gang');
        if not gang then return; end;

        local gangFolder = GangStorage:FindFirstChild(gang);
        if not gangFolder then return; end;

        local leader;

        local members = {};
        for _,v in next, gangFolder.Members:GetChildren() do
            table.insert(members, {
                Name = v.Name;
                Rank = v:GetAttribute('Rank');
                Notoriety = v:GetAttribute('Notoriety');
            });
            if v:GetAttribute('Rank') == 'Leader' then
                leader = v.Name;
            end;
        end;

        return {
            GangData = {
                Name = gang;
                Members = #members;
                Notoriety = gangFolder:GetAttribute('Notoriety');
                Leader = leader;
            };
            IsLeader = plr.Name == leader;
            Members = members;
        } 
    end)
    
    NetworkService.Connect('JoinGang', function(plr, gangName)
        local gangFolder = GangStorage:FindFirstChild(gangName);
        if not gangFolder then return; end;

        local leader = gangFolder:FindFirstChild('Leader');
        if not leader then return; end;

        SetupMember(plr, gangName, 'Member');

--[[         local leaderPlr = Players:FindFirstChild(leader.Name); ]]
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('LeaveGang', function(plr)
        self:RemovePlayer(plr);
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('CreateGang', function(plr, gangName)
        if not plr.Team.Name == 'Civilian' and not plr.Team == 'Prisoner' then return; end;
        if #gangName < 3 then
            NetworkService.Send(plr ,'Error', 'Gang name must be at least 3 characters.');
            return;
        end;

        if plr:GetAttribute('Gang') then
            NetworkService.Send(plr ,'Error', 'You are already in a gang.');
            return;
        end;

        local gangFolder = GangStorage:FindFirstChild(gangName);
        if gangFolder then return; end;

        local filterResult = FilterStringAsync(gangName, plr.UserId, Enum.TextFilterContext.PublicChat);
        if not filterResult then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'Gang name was filtered.');
            return;
        end;

        local filteredName = filterResult:GetNonChatStringForBroadcastAsync();
        if string.find(filteredName, '#') then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'Gang name was filtered.');
            return;
        end

        local succ, err = pcall(CreateGang, filteredName, plr);
        if not succ then
            warn('GangService: Failed to create gang: ' .. err);
            NetworkService.Send(plr ,'Error', 'Failed to create gang. Report this to a developer if unexpected.');
            return;
        end;
        return true;
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('InviteToGang', function(plr, playerName)
        local gang = plr:GetAttribute('Gang');
        if not gang then return; end;

        local gangFolder = GangStorage:FindFirstChild(gang);
        if not gangFolder then return; end;

        local leader = gangFolder:GetAttribute('Leader');
        if not leader then return; end;
        if plr.Name ~= leader then return; end;

        local player = game.Players:FindFirstChild(playerName);
        if not player then return; end;

        if player.Team.Name ~= 'Civilian' and player.Team == 'Prisoner' then return; end;

        if player:GetAttribute('InvitedBy') then
            NetworkService.Send(plr ,'Error', 'Player is already pending an invitation to a gang by someone else.');
            return;
        end;

        if player.Name == plr.Name then
            NetworkService.Send(plr ,'Error', 'You cannot invite yourself to your own gang.');
            return;
        end;

        if player:GetAttribute('Gang') then
            NetworkService.Send(plr ,'Error', 'Player is already in a gang.');
            return;
        end;

        NetworkService.Send(player ,'InviteToGang', plr.Name, gang);
        player:SetAttribute('InvitedBy', player.Name);
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('AcceptGangInvite', function(plr, gangName)
        local gangFolder = GangStorage:FindFirstChild(gangName);
        if not gangFolder then return; end;

        if not plr:GetAttribute('InvitedBy') then return; end;
        if plr:GetAttribute('Gang') then return; end;

        SetupMember(plr, gangName, 'Member');
        plr:SetAttribute('InvitedBy', nil);
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('DeclineGangInvite', function(plr)
        if not plr:GetAttribute('InvitedBy') then return; end;

        plr:SetAttribute('InvitedBy', nil);
    end)

    NetworkService.ConnectFunction('KickFromGang', function(plr: Player, targetName: string)
        if not plr:GetAttribute('Gang') then return; end;

        local succ, targetPlr = pcall(Players.GetPlayerFromCharacter, Players, workspace:FindFirstChild(targetName))
        if not succ or not targetPlr then return; end;

        if not targetPlr:GetAttribute('Gang') then return; end;

        local gang = plr:GetAttribute('Gang');
        local gangFolder = GangStorage:FindFirstChild(gang);
        if not gangFolder then return; end;

        local leader = gangFolder:GetAttribute('Leader');
        if not leader then return; end;
        if plr.Name ~= leader then return; end;

        self:RemovePlayer(targetPlr);
        return true;
    end)

--[[     while true do
        task.wait(1);
        self:AddNotoriety(game.Players.kh1zzer, math.random(1, 5));
        print(self:GetGangInfo('GangShoux'));
    end; ]]
end;


function GangService:Init()
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;

    GangStorage = Instance.new('Folder');
    GangStorage.Name = 'GangStorage';
    GangStorage.Parent = game.ServerStorage;

    local Filter = self.Modules.Filter;
    FilterStringAsync = Filter.FilterStringAsync;
end


return GangService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/HotbarLayoutService.lua ---

--[[
    HotbarLayoutService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Hotbar Layout Service
-- Khizzer
-- March 6, 2022



local HotbarLayoutService = {Client = {}}
local NetworkService;
local CooldownService;
local ProfileDataService;

local function SaveBackpackLayouts(plr)
	local newData = {
		Layout1 = {Name = 'Layout 1', Tools = {}},
		Layout2 = {Name = 'Layout 2', Tools = {}},
		Layout3 = {Name = 'Layout 3', Tools = {}},
		Layout4 = {Name = 'Layout 4', Tools = {}},
		Layout5 = {Name = 'Layout 5', Tools = {}},
		Layout6 = {Name = 'Layout 6', Tools = {}},
		Layout7 = {Name = 'Layout 7', Tools = {}},
		Layout8 = {Name = 'Layout 8', Tools = {}},
		Layout9 = {Name = 'Layout 9', Tools = {}},
		Layout10 = {Name = 'Layout 10', Tools = {}},
		Layout11 = {Name = 'Layout 11', Tools = {}},
		Layout12 = {Name = 'Layout 12', Tools = {}},
		Layout13 = {Name = 'Layout 13', Tools = {}},
		Layout14 = {Name = 'Layout 14', Tools = {}},
		Layout15 = {Name = 'Layout 15', Tools = {}},
		Layout16 = {Name = 'Layout 16', Tools = {}},
		Layout17 = {Name = 'Layout 17', Tools = {}},
		Layout18 = {Name = 'Layout 18', Tools = {}},
		Layout19 = {Name = 'Layout 19', Tools = {}},
		Layout20 = {Name = 'Layout 20', Tools = {}},
	}

	for _,v in next, plr.BackpackLayouts:GetChildren() do
		local layoutNumber: string = v.Name;
		local layoutData = newData['Layout'..layoutNumber];
		local layoutName = v:GetAttribute('Name');
		layoutData.Name = layoutName;
		for i = 1, 10 do
			local tool = v:GetAttribute('Slot'..tostring(i));
			if tool == 'Tool Name' then break; end;
			layoutData.Tools[i] = tool;
		end;
	end;

	ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'BackpackLayouts', newData);
end;

function HotbarLayoutService:Start()
	CooldownService:Create('BackpackUpdate');

	NetworkService.Connect('UPDATE_BACKPACK_LAYOUT', function(plr, layoutNumber: string, hotbarOrder: table, layoutNickname: string)
		if typeof(layoutNumber) ~= 'string' then return; end;
		if typeof(hotbarOrder) ~= 'table' then return; end;
		if typeof(layoutNickname) ~= 'string' then return; end;

		if CooldownService:Check('BackpackUpdate', plr) then
			NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'Wait 3 seconds before saving your layout.');
			return;
		end;
		CooldownService:Add('BackpackUpdate', plr, 3);

		layoutNumber = (layoutNumber):sub(8)
		local backpackLayout = plr.BackpackLayouts:FindFirstChild(layoutNumber);

		--fills in the blanks, the loader on the client ignores anything called Tool Name & breaks for loop
		for i = 1, 10 do
			if not hotbarOrder[i] then
				hotbarOrder[i] = 'Tool Name';
			end;
		end;

		for i = 1, 10 do
			local tool = backpackLayout:SetAttribute('Slot'..tostring(i), hotbarOrder[i]);
		end;
		backpackLayout:SetAttribute('Name', layoutNickname);

		SaveBackpackLayouts(plr);

		NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Notification', 'Hotbar Layout', ('\"%s\" saved to slot %s'):format(layoutNickname, layoutNumber))
	end);
end;


function HotbarLayoutService:Init()
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
	CooldownService = self.Shared.CooldownService;
	ProfileDataService = self.Modules.ProfileDataService;
end


return HotbarLayoutService

-- T Est Service
-- Khizzer

local HouseService = {Client = {}}

local Houses = {};

local MemoryService;

local HOUSE_EXPIRY = 345600; --4 days in seconds

type dataType = {
	Owner: number,
	Color: Color3
};

local function SetupHouse(house: Model)
	if Houses[house] then return; end;

	Houses[house] = true;

	local identifier = house:GetAttribute('Identifier');

	local data: dataType = MemoryService.RawGet(identifier..'House');

	house:SetAttribute('Locked', true);

	if not data then
		--Assume no owner.
		house:SetAttribute('Owner', nil);
	else
		house:SetAttribute('Owner', data.Owner);
		house:SetAttribute('Color', data.Color);
	end;
end;

end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/IncomeService.lua ---

--[[
    IncomeService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
-- Income Service
-- Automationeer :^)
-- December 28, 2023

local IncomeService = {Client = {}}

local NetworkService
local MoneyService
local IncomeData

local PAY_EVERY_MINUTES = 5

function IncomeService:SendCheque(player: Player, value: number)
    local label = `You received a pay cheque of ${value}`
    if player:GetAttribute("Welfare") == true then
        label = `You received a welfare cheque of ${value}`
    end
    if player:GetAttribute("Pension") == true then
        label = `You received a pension cheque of ${value}`
    end
    NetworkService.Send(player, "Notification", "Money Transfer", label, nil, 'Green')
    MoneyService:AddMoney(player, value)
end

function IncomeService:ComputeIncome(player: Player)
    local teamName = player.Team and player.Team.Name
    local divisionName = player:GetAttribute("Division") or "h"
    local income = IncomeData.TeamsDivisions[divisionName]
        or IncomeData.TeamsDivisions[teamName]
        or IncomeData.Welfare
    local inCode = nil

    local entitled = table.find(IncomeData.GovernmentTeams, player.Team.Name)
    for _, role in ipairs(IncomeData.GovernmentValues) do
        if player:GetRankInGroup(role[1]) == role[2] and role[3] > income then
            if (role[4] == "P" or role[4] == "W") and not entitled then continue end
            income = role[3]
            inCode = role[4]
        end
    end

    player:SetAttribute("Welfare", if income == IncomeData.Welfare or inCode == "W" then true else nil)
    player:SetAttribute("Pension", if inCode == "P" then true else nil)
    if player:GetAttribute("X2Income") == true then
        income *= 2
	end
    return income
end

function IncomeService:PlayerAdded(player: Player)
    local function event()
        local income = IncomeService:ComputeIncome(player)
        if typeof(income) ~= "number" or income < 0 then
            warn(`Error computing income for {player.Name}: got {tostring(income)}`)
            return
        end
        player:SetAttribute("Income", income)
    end

    task.defer(event)
    player:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Team"):Connect(event)
    player:GetAttributeChangedSignal("Division"):Connect(event)
end

function IncomeService:Start()
    if game.PrivateServerId ~= "" and game.PrivateServerOwnerId ~= 0  and game.PrivateServerOwnerId ~= 71812450 then
        print("Income disabled, private server")
        return
    end

    while true do
        task.wait(PAY_EVERY_MINUTES * 60)
        for _, player in Players:GetPlayers() do
            local income = player:GetAttribute("Income")
            if
                typeof(income) ~= "number"
                or player.Team.Name == "Prisoner"
                or not player.Character
                or not player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                or player:GetAttribute("HandcuffedBy") ~= nil
                or player.Character.Humanoid.Health <= 1
            then
                continue
            end
            task.defer(IncomeService.SendCheque, IncomeService, player, income * PAY_EVERY_MINUTES)
        end
    end
end;

function IncomeService:Init()
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService
    MoneyService = self.Services.MoneyService
    IncomeData = self.Modules.Income
end

return IncomeService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/InheritanceService.lua ---

--[[
    InheritanceService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local CollectionService = game:GetService("CollectionService")
local InheritanceService = {}

local function process(ov: ObjectValue)
  if ov:IsA("ObjectValue") and ov.Value ~= nil then
    for _, child in ov.Value:GetChildren() do
      local clone = child:Clone()
      clone.Parent = ov.Parent
    end
  else
    warn(`Inheritance {ov:GetFullName()} is invalid`)
  end
  ov:Destroy()
end

local function processShallow(ov: ObjectValue)
  if ov:IsA("ObjectValue") and ov.Value ~= nil then
    for _, child in ov.Value:GetChildren() do
      if child:IsA("Folder") then continue end
      local clone = child:Clone()
      clone.Parent = ov.Parent
    end
  else
    warn(`Inheritance (shallow) {ov:GetFullName()} is invalid`)
  end
  ov:Destroy()
end

function InheritanceService:Init()
  CollectionService:GetInstanceAddedSignal("Inheritance"):Connect(process)
  for _, ov in CollectionService:GetTagged("Inheritance") do
    process(ov)
  end

  CollectionService:GetInstanceAddedSignal("InheritanceShallow"):Connect(processShallow)
  for _, ov in CollectionService:GetTagged("InheritanceShallow") do
    processShallow(ov)
  end
end

return InheritanceService
