--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/JobService.lua ---

--[[
    JobService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local CollectionService = game:GetService("CollectionService")
-- Job Service
-- Khizzer
-- August 28, 2023

local Trove;
local NotificationService;
local NetworkService;
local MoneyService;
local Map;

local JobService = {Client = {}}

local JobTroves = {};

local CANADA_POST_SHIRT = 'http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=14593884256';
local CANADA_POST_PANTS = 'http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=14593891190';

local POST_DESTINATIONS = workspace.PostDestinations;

local JOB_START_CALLBACKS = {
    ['Canada Post'] = function(plr: Player, trove, interactionPart: BasePart)
        local char = plr.Character;

        local shirt = char:FindFirstChildOfClass('Shirt');
        local pants = char:FindFirstChildOfClass('Pants');

        if shirt then
            local original = shirt.ShirtTemplate;
            shirt.ShirtTemplate = CANADA_POST_SHIRT;
            trove:Add(function()
                shirt.ShirtTemplate = original;
            end)
        else
            shirt = Instance.new('Shirt');
            shirt.Parent = char;
            shirt.ShirtTemplate = CANADA_POST_SHIRT;
            trove:Add(shirt);
        end;

        if pants then
            local original = pants.PantsTemplate;
            pants.PantsTemplate = CANADA_POST_PANTS;
            trove:Add(function()
                pants.PantsTemplate = original;
            end)
        else
            pants = Instance.new('Pants');
            pants.Parent = char;
            pants.PantsTemplate = CANADA_POST_PANTS;
            trove:Add(pants);
        end;

        local startLocation = Instance.new('ObjectValue');
        startLocation.Name = 'StartLocation';
        startLocation.Value = interactionPart;
        startLocation.Parent = plr;

        trove:Add(startLocation);

        trove:Add(function()
            plr:SetAttribute('LastVehicle', nil);
        end)

        NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Canada Post', 'Spawn a Postal Truck and fill it up with packages from the post office. Then, deliver them to the destinations shown.');
    end
}

local function UpdatePackageVisibility(truck: Model)
    local packagesModel = truck.Body.Packages;

    local packageCount = truck:GetAttribute('Packages');

    for _,v in next, packagesModel:GetChildren() do
        for _,v2 in v:GetDescendants() do
            if v2:IsA('BasePart') then
                v2.Transparency = (tonumber(v.Name) <= packageCount) and 0 or 1;
            end;
        end;
    end;
end;

--local function to Get player count in job which is a string attribute
local function GetPlayerCountInJob(jobName: string)
    local count = 0;
    for _,v in next, game.Players:GetPlayers() do
        if v:GetAttribute('CurrentJob') == jobName then
            count += 1;
        end;
    end;
    return count;
end;

function JobService:Start()
	NetworkService.Connect('StartCivilianJob', function(plr: Player, interactionPart: BasePart)
        if typeof(interactionPart) ~= "Instance" then return; end;
        if not interactionPart:IsA("BasePart") then return; end;

        if plr:DistanceFromCharacter(interactionPart.Position) > 10 then return; end;

        local jobName = interactionPart:GetAttribute('JobName');

        if jobName == nil then return; end;

        local playersInJob = GetPlayerCountInJob(jobName);
        if playersInJob > 5 then
            _G.AeroError(plr, `There are already {playersInJob} players in this job! Wait for a job opening.`);
            return;
        end;

        local trove = Trove.new();
        JobTroves[plr] = trove;

        plr:SetAttribute('CurrentJob', jobName);

        trove:AttachToInstance(plr.Character);
        trove:Add(function()
            plr:SetAttribute('CurrentJob', nil);
            plr:SetAttribute('JobMoney', nil);
        end)

        local callback = JOB_START_CALLBACKS[jobName];
        if callback then
            callback(plr, trove, interactionPart);
        end;
        NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Job Started', `You have started your {jobName} job. Complete the tasks to earn your paycheque!`);
	end)

    NetworkService.Connect('RequestPostOfficePackage', function(plr: Player, interactionPart: BasePart)
        if plr:GetAttribute('CurrentJob') ~= 'Canada Post' then return; end;

        if typeof(interactionPart) ~= "Instance" then return; end;

        if plr:DistanceFromCharacter(interactionPart.Position) > 10 then return; end;
        if not CollectionService:HasTag(interactionPart, 'PostOfficeCollection') then return; end;

        local car = plr.Car.Value;

        if not car then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'You do not have a postal truck!');
            return;
        end;
        if not car:GetAttribute('Packages') then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'You do not have a postal truck!');
            return;
        end;
        if car:GetAttribute('Packages') == 12 then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'Your truck is full!');
            return;
        end;

        if plr.Character:FindFirstChild('Package') then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'You already have a package in your inventory! Place it in your truck before getting another one.')
            return;
        end;

        if plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild('Package') then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'You already have a package in your inventory! Place it in your truck before getting another one.')
            return;
        end;

        local packagePrefab = self.ServerAssets.Jobs.Package :: Tool;

        local packageClone = packagePrefab:Clone();
        packageClone.Parent = plr.Character;

        NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Package', `Place packages in your truck until it's full!`);
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('PlacePackageInTruck', function(plr: Player, interactionPart: BasePart)
        if plr:GetAttribute('CurrentJob') ~= 'Canada Post' then return; end;

        if plr:DistanceFromCharacter(interactionPart.Position) > 10 then return; end;
        if not CollectionService:HasTag(interactionPart, 'PostTruck') then return; end;

        local car = plr.Car.Value;

        if not car then return; end;
        if not car:GetAttribute('Packages') then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'You do not have a postal truck!');
            return;
        end;

        if not interactionPart:IsDescendantOf(car) then return; end;

        local package = plr.Character:FindFirstChild('Package');
        if not package then return; end;

        local packageCount = car:GetAttribute('Packages') or 0;

        if packageCount == 12 then _G.AeroError(plr, 'Your truck is full!') return; end;

        package:Destroy();

        car:SetAttribute('Packages', packageCount + 1);

        UpdatePackageVisibility(car);

        local destinationsFolder = car.Config.State.Destinations;
        local destinations = POST_DESTINATIONS:GetChildren();
        local chosenDestination = destinations[math.random(1, #destinations)] :: Model;

        local objectValue = Instance.new('ObjectValue');
        objectValue.Name = tostring(#destinationsFolder:GetChildren() + 1);
        objectValue.Value = chosenDestination;
        objectValue.Parent = destinationsFolder;

        if packageCount == 11 then
            car.Config.State.DeliveryStarted.Value = true;
            NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Delivery Started', 'Get in your truck to get directions to your first destination!');

            local currentDestination = Instance.new('ObjectValue');
            currentDestination.Name = 'CurrentDestination';
            local closestDestination = chosenDestination;

            for _,v in destinationsFolder:GetChildren() do
                if (v.Value.PrimaryPart.Position - car.PrimaryPart.Position).Magnitude < (closestDestination.PrimaryPart.Position - car.PrimaryPart.Position).Magnitude then
                    closestDestination = v.Value;
                end;
            end;

            currentDestination.Value = closestDestination;
            currentDestination.Parent = car.Config.State;
        else
            NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Package Placed', `Place {12 - (packageCount + 1)} more packages in your truck to start your deliveries!`);
        end;

        chosenDestination:AddPersistentPlayer(plr);
    end);

    NetworkService.Connect('TakePackageFromTruck', function(plr: Player, interactionPart: BasePart)
        if plr:GetAttribute('CurrentJob') ~= 'Canada Post' then return; end;

        if not CollectionService:HasTag(interactionPart, 'PostTruck') then return; end;

        local car = plr.Car.Value;

        if not car then return; end;
        if not car:GetAttribute('Packages') then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'You do not have a postal truck!');
            return;
        end;

        if plr.Character:FindFirstChild('Package') then return; end;
        if plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild('Package') then return; end;

        if not interactionPart:IsDescendantOf(car) then return; end;

        local packageCount = car:GetAttribute('Packages') or 0;
        if packageCount <= 0 then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'Your truck is empty!');
            return;
        end;

        local currentDestination = car.Config.State.CurrentDestination.Value;
        if (car.PrimaryPart.Position - currentDestination.PrimaryPart.Position).Magnitude > 100 then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'You are too far away from your destination!');
            return;
        end;

        local packagePrefab = self.ServerAssets.Jobs.Package :: Tool;
        local packageClone = packagePrefab:Clone();

        local destination = Instance.new('ObjectValue');
        destination.Name = 'Destination';
        destination.Value = currentDestination;
        destination.Parent = packageClone;

        packageClone.Parent = plr.Character;

        car:SetAttribute('Packages', packageCount - 1);
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('DeliverPackage', function(plr: Player, interactionPart: BasePart)
        local car = plr.Car.Value;

        if plr:GetAttribute('CurrentJob') ~= 'Canada Post' then return; end;

        if not car then return; end;
        if not car:GetAttribute('Packages') then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'You do not have a postal truck!');
            return;
        end;

        if not interactionPart:IsDescendantOf(POST_DESTINATIONS) then return; end;

        if plr:DistanceFromCharacter(interactionPart.Position) > 10 then return; end;

        local package = plr.Character:FindFirstChild('Package');
        if not package then return; end;
        local destination = package:FindFirstChild('Destination');
        if not destination then return; end;

        if destination.Value.PrimaryPart ~= interactionPart then return; end;

        package:Destroy();

        local startLocation = plr.StartLocation.Value;
        if not startLocation then return; end;

        local distance = (interactionPart.Position - startLocation.Position).Magnitude;

        local income = math.floor(Map(distance, 0, 8000, 250, 350));

        plr:SetAttribute('JobMoney', (plr:GetAttribute('JobMoney') or 0) + income);

        local destinationsFolder = car.Config.State.Destinations;
        local currentDestination = car.Config.State.CurrentDestination;

        for _,v in next, destinationsFolder:GetChildren() do
            if v.Value == interactionPart.Parent then
                v:Destroy();
                break;
            end;
        end;

        UpdatePackageVisibility(car);

        if #destinationsFolder:GetChildren() == 0 then
            --Delivery is over, they need to collect paycheque
            car.Config.State.DeliveryStarted.Value = false;
            currentDestination:Destroy();

            NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Deliveries Complete', 'You have completed your deliveries! Return to the post office to collect your paycheque.');
        else
            --still more to go
            NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Package Delivered', `You have delivered a package! You have {#destinationsFolder:GetChildren()} more to go!`);
            local destinationList = destinationsFolder:GetChildren();
            table.sort(destinationList, function(a, b)
                return (a.Value.PrimaryPart.Position - car.PrimaryPart.Position).Magnitude < (b.Value.PrimaryPart.Position - car.PrimaryPart.Position).Magnitude
            end);

            currentDestination.Value = destinationList[1].Value;
        end
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('CollectJobPay', function(plr: Player, interactionPart: BasePart)
        if plr:GetAttribute('CurrentJob') == nil then return; end;

        if plr:DistanceFromCharacter(interactionPart.Position) > 10 then return; end;
        if not CollectionService:HasTag(interactionPart, 'Job') then return; end;

        local jobMoney = plr:GetAttribute('JobMoney');
        if jobMoney == nil then return; end;

        plr:SetAttribute('JobMoney', nil);

        local ownsX2 = plr:GetAttribute('X2Income') == true;

        local income;

        if ownsX2 then
            income = math.floor(jobMoney * 1.5);
            NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Job Pay', `You have collected your paycheque of ${jobMoney}! You also have the increased income pass, so you earned ${income}!`, nil, 'Green');
        else
            income = jobMoney;
            NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Job Pay', `You have collected your paycheque of ${jobMoney}!`, nil, 'Green');
        end;
        MoneyService:AddBank(plr, income);
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('EndCivilianJob', function(plr: Player, interactionPart: BasePart)
        if typeof(interactionPart) ~= "Instance" then return; end;
        if not interactionPart:IsA("BasePart") then return; end;

        if plr:DistanceFromCharacter(interactionPart.Position) > 10 then return; end;

        local jobName = interactionPart:GetAttribute('JobName');
        if jobName == nil then return; end;

        local currentJob = plr:GetAttribute('CurrentJob');
        if currentJob ~= jobName then return; end;
        if currentJob == nil then return; end;

        local trove = JobTroves[plr];
        if not trove then return; end;

        local jobMoney = plr:GetAttribute('JobMoney');

        if jobMoney ~= nil then
            local ownsX2 = plr:GetAttribute('X2Income') == true;
            local income;

            if ownsX2 then
                income = math.floor(jobMoney * 1.5);
                NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Job Pay', `You have collected your paycheque of ${jobMoney}! You also have the increased income pass, so you earned ${income}!`, nil, 'Green');
            else
                income = jobMoney;
                NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Job Pay', `You have collected your paycheque of ${jobMoney}!`, nil, 'Green');
            end;
            MoneyService:AddBank(plr, income);
        end;

        trove:Destroy();
        JobTroves[plr] = nil;
    end)
end


function JobService:Init()
    MoneyService = self.Services.MoneyService;
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    NotificationService = self.Services.NotificationService;
    Trove = self.Shared.Trove;
    Map = self.Shared.Map;
end


return JobService

--[[
    JudgeService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53

-- Judge Service
-- Khizzer
-- January 11, 2022


local HttpService = game:GetService('HttpService');
local Players = game:GetService('Players');
local jsonContentType = Enum.HttpContentType.ApplicationJson;

local JudgeService = {Client = {}}
local RecordService;
local WarrantDataService;
local NetworkService;
local NotificationService;
local DeveloperCheck;
local CitationsModule;
local CrimesModule;
local PrisonService;
local CooldownService;
local ProfileDataService;
local WebUtil;
local MoneyService;

local Trello = require(game.ServerStorage.Aero.Modules.Trello);
local APP_KEY = 'ed26b9f15084fd2838d755c50f712ae5';
local TOKEN = 'ATTA5eb7ff54a3488a20e4690fb034b2d252d02dc8cac63e511e3a794fe4ce5b6b0c34BA7C9F';


local function FindCitationPrice(Value)
	return CitationsModule[Value]
end

local function FindArrestTime(value)
    return CrimesModule[value]
end

local function SendJudgeLog(name: string, userID: number, action: string, ...)
	local data = {
		embeds = {
			{
				title = 'Judiciary Log',
				color = 3769079,
				fields = {
					{
						name = 'Judge',
						value = name,
						inline = false
					},
					{
						name = 'Judge Profile',
						value = 'https://www.roblox.com/users/' .. userID .. '/profile',
						inline = false
					},
					{
						name = 'Action',
						value = action,
						inline = false
					},
					table.unpack(...)
				}
			}
		}
	};

	local ok1, err1 = pcall(HttpService.PostAsync, HttpService, 'https://webhook.lewisakura.moe/api/webhooks/995400839432786080/pYzxudUViFWYdQvp2uUpw9RIPAv4O_HWJhXTbiIYQL1SzEW5fW2mwxvauVCTUBqeglVp', HttpService:JSONEncode(data), jsonContentType);
    if ok1 then
        return true
    end

    warn(`Could not log judicial action: {err1}. Attempting bot.`)
    local succ, err = pcall(WebUtil.DiscordBotMessage, "995400742032642088", data)
    if succ then
        return true
    end
    warn(`Could not log judicial action via bot: {err}`)
    _G.AeroError(Players[name], "This action could not be logged and has been aborted. Please try again, attempt in another server, or report to a developer.")

    return false
end;

function JudgeService:Start()
    NetworkService.ConnectFunction('GetActiveWarrants', function(plr)
        if plr.Team ~= game.Teams['Provincial Court'] and not DeveloperCheck(plr) then return; end;
        return WarrantDataService:GetActiveWarrants();
    end)

	NetworkService.Connect('SUBMIT_WARRANT', function(plr, target: string, crimes: {string}, reason: string)
        if plr.Team ~= game.Teams['Provincial Court'] and not DeveloperCheck(plr) then return; end;
        local possibleUserId = Players:GetUserIdFromNameAsync(target);
        if not possibleUserId then
            NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Judicial System', 'Could not issue warrant. Username is invalid.', nil, 'Red');
            return;
        end;

        if not SendJudgeLog(plr.Name, plr.UserId, 'Issued Warrant', {
            {
                name = 'Target',
                value = target,
                inline = false
            },
            {
                name = 'Target Profile',
                value = 'https://www.roblox.com/users/' .. possibleUserId .. '/profile',
                inline = false
            },
            {
                name = 'Crimes',
                value = table.concat(crimes, '; '),
                inline = false
            },
            {
                name = 'Reason',
                value = reason,
                inline = false
            }
        }) then
            return
        end

        local username = Players:GetNameFromUserIdAsync(possibleUserId);
        WarrantDataService:AddWarrant(username, crimes, reason, possibleUserId);
        NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Judicial System', ('Warrant successfully issued for %s'):format(target), nil, 'Purple');
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('REMOVE_WARRANT', function(plr, UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER)
        if plr.Team ~= game.Teams['Provincial Court'] and not DeveloperCheck(plr) then return; end;
        local warrants = WarrantDataService:GetActiveWarrants();
        local warrant = warrants[UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER];
        if not warrant then
            NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Judicial System', 'Could not revoke warrant; warrant was not found in database.', nil, 'Red');
            return
        end;

        if not SendJudgeLog(plr.Name, plr.UserId, 'Removed Warrant', {
            {
                name = 'Target',
                value = warrant[1],
                inline = false
            },
            {
                name = 'Target Profile',
                value = 'https://www.roblox.com/users/' .. warrant[4] .. '/profile',
                inline = false
            },
            {
                name = 'Crimes',
                value = table.concat(warrant[2], '; '),
                inline = false
            },
            {
                name = 'Warrant Reason',
                value = warrant[3],
                inline = false
            }
        }) then
            return
        end

        WarrantDataService:RemoveWarrant(UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER);
        NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Judicial System', 'Warrant successfully removed', nil, 'Purple');
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('SUBMIT_FINE', function(plr, target: string, citations: {string}, reason: string, valueOverride: number?)
        if plr.Team ~= game.Teams['Provincial Court'] and not DeveloperCheck(plr) then return; end;
        local possibleUserId = Players:GetUserIdFromNameAsync(target);
        if not possibleUserId then
            NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Judicial System', 'Could not issue fine. Username is invalid.', nil, 'Red');
            return;
        end;

        local realUsername = Players:GetNameFromUserIdAsync(possibleUserId);

        if (valueOverride or 0) < 0 then return end;
		local citationsPrice = valueOverride or 0;
        if valueOverride == nil then
            for _,name in next, citations do
                local ct = FindCitationPrice(name)
                if ct then citationsPrice += ct end
            end;
        end

        if not SendJudgeLog(plr.Name, plr.UserId, 'Issued Fine', {
            {
                name = 'Target',
                value = target,
                inline = false
            },
            {
                name = 'Target Profile',
                value = 'https://www.roblox.com/users/' .. possibleUserId .. '/profile',
                inline = false
            },
            {
                name = 'Offences',
                value = table.concat(citations, '; '),
                inline = false
            },
            {
                name = 'Penalty',
                value = `${citationsPrice}` .. if valueOverride == nil then ' (Auto)' else '' ,
                inline = false,
            },
            {
                name = 'Reason',
                value = reason,
                inline = false
            }
        }) then
            return
        end

        --if #citations == 1 and citations[1] == "Administrative" then
            RecordService:AddCitation(plr.Name, 'COURT', target, citationsPrice, citations, reason);
        --end

        if Players:FindFirstChild(realUsername) then
            MoneyService:SubtractBank(Players[realUsername], citationsPrice)
        else
            ProfileDataService.AddGlobalUpdate(`Player_{possibleUserId}`, {
                Type = 'IssueFine';
                IssueFine = true;
                FineAmount = citationsPrice;
            })
        end;

        NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Judicial System', ('Fine successfully issued for %s'):format(target), nil, 'Purple');
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('JUDGE_ARREST', function(plr, target: string, crimes: {string}, reason: string, timeOverride: number?)
        if plr.Team ~= game.Teams['Provincial Court'] and not DeveloperCheck(plr) then return; end;
        local possibleUserId = Players:GetUserIdFromNameAsync(target);
        if not possibleUserId then
            NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Judicial System', 'Could not issue charge. Username is invalid.', nil, 'Red');
            return;
        end;

        local realUsername = Players:GetNameFromUserIdAsync(possibleUserId);

        if (timeOverride or 0) < 0 then return end;
		local prisonTime = timeOverride or 0;
        if timeOverride == nil then
            for _,name in next, crimes do
                local ct = FindArrestTime(name)
                if ct then prisonTime += ct end
            end;
        end

        if prisonTime > 0 then
            NotificationService.SendAll('Court Sentence', `{realUsername} has been sentenced to {math.floor(prisonTime / 60)} minutes.`, nil, 'Black');
            if Players:FindFirstChild(realUsername) then
                --instantly add it if theyre in game
                PrisonService.AddPrisonerSignal:Fire(Players[realUsername], prisonTime);
            else
                --If not in game use profileservice global updates to add next time they join
                local profileStore = ProfileDataService:GetProfileStore();
                local userId = Players:GetUserIdFromNameAsync(target);
                local profileKey = `Player_{userId}`;

                profileStore:GlobalUpdateProfileAsync(profileKey, function(globalUpdates)
                    globalUpdates:AddActiveUpdate({
                        IssuePrisonTime = true;
                        PrisonTime = prisonTime;
                    })
                end)
            end;
        end

        if not SendJudgeLog(plr.Name, plr.UserId, 'Issued Sentence', {
            {
                name = 'Target',
                value = target,
                inline = false
            },
            {
                name = 'Target Profile',
                value = 'https://www.roblox.com/users/' .. possibleUserId .. '/profile',
                inline = false
            },
            {
                name = 'Offences',
                value = table.concat(crimes, '; '),
                inline = false
            },
            {
                name = 'Sentence',
                value = `{prisonTime} seconds` .. if timeOverride == nil then ' (Auto)' else '',
                inline = false,
            },
            {
                name = 'Reason',
                value = reason,
                inline = false
            }
        }) then
            return
        end

        --if #crimes == 1 and crimes[1] == "Administrative" then
            RecordService:AddArrest(plr.Name, 'COURT', target, prisonTime, crimes, reason)
        --end

        NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Judicial System', ('Sentence successfully issued for %s'):format(target), nil, 'Purple');
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('CourtFile', function(plr, responses)
        if CooldownService:Check('CourtCaseFile', plr) then return; end;

        CooldownService:Create(plr, 'CourtCaseFile', 3600);
        -- local trelloAPI = Trello(APP_KEY, TOKEN);
        -- local lists = trelloAPI.getLists('AK7Fbhwj');
        -- local list = trelloAPI.getListObj(lists, {'Unfiltered Submissions'});
        -- trelloAPI.makeCard(list.id,plr.Name,responses);
        self.Services.TrelloService:SubmitJudicialCase(plr.Name, responses)
        NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Judicial System', 'Court case has been filed. Please check the courts trello to confirm.', nil, 'Purple');
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('JUDGE_REMOVE_RECORD', function(plr, target, recordType, UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER)
        if plr.Team ~= game.Teams['Provincial Court'] and not DeveloperCheck(plr) then return; end;

        if not SendJudgeLog(plr.Name, plr.UserId, 'Removed Record', {
            {
                name = 'Player',
                value = target,
                inline = false
            },
            {
                name = 'Record Type',
                value = recordType,
                inline = false
            },
            {
                name = 'Record ID',
                value = UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER,
                inline = false
            }
        }) then
            return
        end

        if recordType == 'Citation' then
            RecordService:RemoveCitation(target, UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER);
        else
            RecordService:RemoveArrest(target, UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER);
        end;
        NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Judicial System', 'Records removed.', nil, 'Purple');
    end);

    NetworkService.Connect('JUDGE_CLEAR_RECORDS', function(plr, target)
        if plr.Team ~= game.Teams['Provincial Court'] and not DeveloperCheck(plr) then return; end;

        if not SendJudgeLog(plr.Name, plr.UserId, 'Cleared Records', {
            {
                name = 'Target',
                value = target,
                inline = false
            }
        }) then
            return
        end

        RecordService:ClearRecords(target);
        NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Judicial System', 'Records cleared.', nil, 'Purple');
    end);
end


function JudgeService:Init()
    DeveloperCheck = self.Shared.DeveloperCheck;
    WarrantDataService = self.Modules.WarrantDataService;
    CooldownService = self.Shared.CooldownService;
    NotificationService = self.Services.NotificationService;
    ProfileDataService = self.Modules.ProfileDataService;
    WebUtil = self.Modules.WebUtil;

    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    NotificationService = self.Services.NotificationService;
	RecordService = self.Services.RecordService;
    CitationsModule = require(game.ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild('CitationsModule'));
    CrimesModule = require(game.ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild('CrimesModule'));
    PrisonService = self.Services.PrisonService;
    MoneyService = self.Services.MoneyService;
end


return JudgeService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/LicensePlateService.lua ---

--[[
    LicensePlateService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local HttpService = game:GetService('HttpService');
local Players = game:GetService('Players')

local LicensePlateService = {Client = {}};
local NetworkService;
local LicenseDataService;

local carIDs = {}

function LicensePlateService.Create()
    local licensePlate = {};
    local GUID = HttpService:GenerateGUID(false);
    for letter in GUID:gmatch('%a') do
        table.insert(licensePlate, letter:upper());
        if #licensePlate == 3 then break; end;
    end;
    for number in GUID:gmatch('%d') do
        table.insert(licensePlate, number);
        if #licensePlate == 6 then break; end;
    end;
    licensePlate = table.concat(licensePlate);

    if LicenseDataService:IsPlateTaken(licensePlate) then
        return LicensePlateService.Create();
    end;

    return licensePlate;
end;

function LicensePlateService:Start()
    NetworkService.ConnectFunction('LicenseDataLookup', function(plr, plate)
        plate = plate:upper();

        local owner;
        local carType;
        local color;

        local NotFoundMessage = `License plate: {plate} was not found in the database`

        for _,v in workspace.Cars:GetChildren() do
            if v:GetAttribute('LicensePlate') == plate then
                local phantom = v:GetAttribute('Phantom')
                local gcps = plr:GetAttribute('Division') == 'GCPS'
                if phantom and not gcps and not _G.Aero.Shared.INSETest(plr) then
                    task.wait();
                    _G.AeroError(plr, NotFoundMessage);
                    return false;
                end

                owner = v:GetAttribute('Owner');
                carType = v.Name;
                color = v:GetAttribute('Color');

                if phantom and gcps then
                    owner = `{owner} (Phantom)`
                elseif phantom and not gcps then
                    owner = 'INSET INFORMATION ONLY: CSIS vehicle'
                end

                return {
                    Owner = owner,
                    CarType = carType,
                    Color = color
                }
            end;
        end;

        local isTaken = LicenseDataService:IsPlateTaken(plate);
        if not isTaken then
            _G.AeroError(plr, NotFoundMessage);
            return false;
        end;

        local data = LicenseDataService:GetPlateData(plate);
        local username = Players:GetNameFromUserIdAsync(data.UserId);

        owner = username;
        carType = data.CarType;
        color = data.Color;

        return {
            Owner = owner,
            CarType = carType,
            Color = color
        }
    end)
end;

function LicensePlateService:Init()
    LicenseDataService = self.Modules.LicenseDataService;
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
end;

return LicensePlateService;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/LogsService.lua ---

--[[
    LogsService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Logs Service
-- Khizzer
-- August 25, 2023

local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage');
local LinkedList = require(ReplicatedStorage.Packages.LinkedList);

local NetworkService;

local MAX_LOGS = 5000;

local LogsService = {
    Client = {};
    Logs = {
        Commands = LinkedList.new();
        Kills = LinkedList.new();
        Joins = LinkedList.new();
        Leaves = LinkedList.new();
        Teams = LinkedList.new();
    }
}

function LogsService:AddLog(logType: string, logData)
    local logs = self.Logs[logType];
    if not logs then return warn(`Log type {logType} does not exist!`); end;

    local formattedTime = DateTime.now():FormatUniversalTime('LTS', 'en-us');

    logs:Push(`{formattedTime}: {logData}`);

    local count = 0;
    for _,v in logs do
        count += 1;
    end;

    if count > MAX_LOGS then
        logs:PeekEntry().remove();
    end;
end;

function LogsService:Start()
    NetworkService.ConnectFunction('RequestLogs', function(plr, logType)
        if ((plr:GetAttribute('AdminLevel') or 0) == 0) and not plr:GetAttribute('Developer') then return; end;

        local list = self.Logs[logType];

        if not list then return; end;

        local logs = {};
        for value, entry in list:IterReversed() do
            table.insert(logs, value);
        end;

        return logs;
    end)
end


function LogsService:Init()
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
end


return LogsService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/LookService.lua ---

--[[
    LookService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local Players = game:GetService('Players');

local NetworkService;

local LOOK_EVENT = 'Look';

local findFirstChild = workspace.FindFirstChild;
local osTime = os.time;

local Send;

local LookService = {Client = {}, LastFired = {}};

function LookService:Start()
    self:ConnectClientEvent('Look', function(plr, lookVectorX, lookVectorY)
        local plrChar = plr.Character;
        if not plrChar then return; end;
        local plrRootPartPos = findFirstChild(plrChar, 'HumanoidRootPart');
        plrRootPartPos = plrRootPartPos and plrRootPartPos.Position;
        if not plrRootPartPos then return; end;

        local lastFiredTime = self.LastFired[plr];
        if lastFiredTime then
            self.LastFired[plr] = osTime();
            if osTime() - lastFiredTime < 0.15 then return; end;
        end;

        for i, v in next, Players:GetPlayers() do
            if v ~= plr then
                local char = v.Character;
                local rootPart = char and char:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart');
                if rootPart and (rootPart.Position - plrRootPartPos).Magnitude < 100 then
                    self:FireClient('Look', v, plrChar, lookVectorX, lookVectorY);
                    --Send(v, LOOK_EVENT, plrChar, lookVectorX, lookVectorY);
                end;
            end;
        end;
    end);
end;

function LookService:Init()
    self:RegisterUnreliableEvent('Look');
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    Send = NetworkService.Send;
end;

return LookService;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/MessageRecorderService.lua ---

--[[
    MessageRecorderService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Message Record Service
-- Khizzer
-- March 12, 2024


type MessageRecorder = {
    Players: {Player: RBXScriptConnection};
    WebhookLink: string;
    ChannelID: string;
    MessageQueue: {string}
}

local WebUtil;

local MessageRecordService = {
    Client = {},
    Recorders = {}
}

function MessageRecordService:SendMessage(id, content)
    local recorder: MessageRecorder = self.Recorders[id];
    local json = {
        content = content,
        username = "Message Recorder",
        avatar_url = "https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/969943810299793448/8e56d5e6b9b309b891c2cd66ccd942b6.png?size=4096",
        allowed_mentions = {
            parse = {}
        }
    };

    local suc, res = pcall(function()
        WebUtil.SendWebhook(recorder.WebhookLink, recorder.ChannelID, json);
    end);

    if not suc then
        warn(res);
        return false
    end
    return true
end

function MessageRecordService:AddToQueue(id, message)
    local recorder: MessageRecorder = self.Recorders[id];
    table.insert(recorder.MessageQueue, message);
end

function MessageRecordService:CreateRecorder(id, webhookLink, channelId, plr)
    self.Recorders[id] = {
        Players = {};
        WebhookLink = webhookLink;
        ChannelID = channelId;
        MessageQueue = {};
    };

    local time = DateTime.now():FormatUniversalTime('HH:mm:ss', 'en-us')
    local err = WebUtil.DiscordBotMessage(channelId, {
        content = `> [{time}] {plr.Name} started a {id} message recorder.`,
        username = "Message Recorder",
        avatar_url = "https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/969943810299793448/8e56d5e6b9b309b891c2cd66ccd942b6.png?size=4096";
        allowed_mentions = {
            parse = {}
        }
    })
    if err then
        self:DeleteRecorder(id)
        return false
    end
    return true
end;

function MessageRecordService:AddPlayerToRecorder(player: Player, id: string)
    local recorder: MessageRecorder = self.Recorders[id];

    if not recorder then
        return;
    end;

    self.Recorders[id].Players[player] = player.Chatted:Connect(function(msg)
        msg = msg:gsub("&amp;", "&"):gsub("&lt;", "<"):gsub("&gt;", ">"):gsub('&quot;', '"'):gsub("&apos;", "'")
        local suc, res = pcall(function()

            msg = msg:gsub("%s+", " "):gsub("%*", "\\*"):gsub("%_", "\\_"):gsub(">", "\\>")

            local time = DateTime.now():FormatUniversalTime('HH:mm:ss', 'en-us')
            self:AddToQueue(id, `[{time}] **[{player.Name}]:** {msg}`);
            if #recorder.MessageQueue >= 10 then
                local ok = self:SendMessage(id, table.concat(recorder.MessageQueue, "\n"))
                if ok then
                    recorder.MessageQueue = {};
                end
            end;
        end)

        if not suc then
            warn(res);
        end;
    end);
end;

function MessageRecordService:RemovePlayerFromRecorder(player, id)
    if not self.Recorders[id] then
        return;
    end;

    if self.Recorders[id].Players[player] then
        self.Recorders[id].Players[player]:Disconnect();
        self.Recorders[id].Players[player] = nil;
    end;
end;

function MessageRecordService:DeleteRecorder(id)
    local recorder = self.Recorders[id]
    if not recorder then return; end;

    for i, v in recorder.Players do
        v:Disconnect();
        recorder.Players[i] = nil;
    end

    if #recorder.MessageQueue > 0 then
        self:SendMessage(id, table.concat(recorder.MessageQueue, "\n"))
    end;

    self.Recorders[id] = nil;
end;

--For PlayerService PlayerRemoving only
function MessageRecordService:CleanPlayer(player)
    for i,v in next, self.Recorders do
        if v.Players[player] then
            v.Players[player]:Disconnect();
            v.Players[player] = nil;
        end;
    end;
end;

function MessageRecordService:Start()
	task.defer(function()
        while true do
            task.wait(10);
            for id, v in next, self.Recorders do
                if #v.MessageQueue > 0 then
                    local ok = self:SendMessage(id, table.concat(v.MessageQueue, "\n"))
                    if ok then
                        v.MessageQueue = {};
                    end
                end;
            end;
        end
	end)

    -- I was going to make it only pick up players in a detector part
    -- and automatically update this every second, but... there aren't any
    -- detector parts. so....
    -- task.defer(function()
    --     while true do
    --         task.wait(1)
    --         for _, recorder in self.Recorders do

    --         end
    --     end
    -- end)
end


function MessageRecordService:Init()
	WebUtil = self.Modules.WebUtil;
end


return MessageRecordService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/MessageService.lua ---

--[[
    MessageService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Message Service
-- Khizzer
-- January 2, 2024

local MessagingService = game:GetService("MessagingService")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local ServerStorage = game:GetService("ServerStorage")

local Cmdr = require(ServerStorage.Packages.Cmdr);

local NetworkService;

local FilterStringAsync;
local GetChatForUserAsync;

local MessageService = {Client = {}}


function MessageService:Start()
	MessagingService:SubscribeAsync('remotemessage', function(message)
        local data = message.Data;

        if data then
            for _,v in next, Players:GetPlayers() do
                local filterResult: TextFilterResult? = FilterStringAsync(data, v.UserId, Enum.TextFilterContext.PrivateChat);

                if not filterResult then return; end;

                local filteredMessage: string? = GetChatForUserAsync(filterResult, v.UserId);

                if not filteredMessage then return; end;

                NetworkService.Send(v, 'ADMIN_MESSAGE', 'Developer Message', filteredMessage);
            end
        end
	end)

    MessagingService:SubscribeAsync('announceshutdown', function(message)
        self.Services.NetworkService.SendAll('ServerShutdownMessage', {Name = 'Remote Shutdown'});

        Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(player)
            player:Kick('This server is being shutdown by a developer. Please rejoin in approximately 2 minutes.');
        end);

        task.delay(2, function()
            for i = 60, 1, -1 do
                self.Services.NotificationService.SendAll('Shutdown Timer', `{i}`, nil, 'Purple');
                task.wait(1);
            end;
        end)
    end)

    MessagingService:SubscribeAsync('banplayer', function(message)
        local userId = message.Data;

        Cmdr.Registry:GetStore('Bans')[userId] = 'Trello Banned';

        local plr = Players:GetPlayerByUserId(userId);

        if plr then
            NetworkService.SendAll('Notification', 'Player Banned', `{plr.Name} has been banned from British Columbia games.`, nil, 'Purple');
            plr:SetAttribute('Moderated', true);
            plr:Kick('You have been banned from British Columbia games. Please refer to the Trello board for further details.');
        end;
    end)
end


function MessageService:Init()
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    FilterStringAsync = self.Modules.Filter.FilterStringAsync;
    GetChatForUserAsync = self.Modules.Filter.GetChatForUserAsync;
end


return MessageService

--[[
    MissileService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Missile Service
-- Khizzer
-- July 11, 2023
local Debris = game:GetService("Debris")

local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")

local DamageCharacter;

local MissileService = {Client = {}}

local MissilePrefab: Model?;

local missileSilo: Model = workspace:WaitForChild('MissileSilo');
local launchDoor: Part = missileSilo:WaitForChild('LaunchDoor');
local CLOSED_POSITION = launchDoor.Position;
local OPEN_POSITION = Vector3.new(-1985.589, -34.05, 146.208);
local FIRST_TARGET = missileSilo:WaitForChild('LaunchTarget');

local DEFAULT_TARGET = missileSilo:WaitForChild('DefaultTarget');

local openTween = TweenService:Create(launchDoor, TweenInfo.new(2), {Position = OPEN_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(launchDoor, TweenInfo.new(2), {Position = CLOSED_POSITION});

local function ReachedTarget(pos1, pos2)
    return (pos1 - pos2).Magnitude <= 4
end;

function MissileService:FireMissile(target: string | Player)
    local missile = MissilePrefab:Clone();

    local primaryPart = missile.Main;
    local force = missile.Force;

    local smoke = primaryPart.Smoke;
    local fire = primaryPart.Fire;
    local rocketPropulsion: RocketPropulsion = force.RocketPropulsion;

    missile.Parent = workspace;

    missile.ModelStreamingMode = Enum.ModelStreamingMode.PersistentPerPlayer;
    missile:AddPersistentPlayer(target == 'Default' and game.Players:FindFirstChildOfClass('Player') or target);

    --[[ if target == 'Default' then
        primaryPart:SetNetworkOwner(game.Players:FindFirstChildOfClass('Player'));
    else
        primaryPart:SetNetworkOwner(target);
    end; ]]

    rocketPropulsion.Target = FIRST_TARGET;

    launchDoor.OpenSmoke.Enabled = true;
    task.delay(1, function()
        launchDoor.OpenSmoke.Enabled = false;
        openTween:Play()
        openTween.Completed:Wait();
        smoke.Enabled = true;
        task.wait(3);
        rocketPropulsion:Fire();
        fire.Enabled = true;
        smoke.Enabled = false;
    end)

    repeat task.wait() until ReachedTarget(force.Position, FIRST_TARGET.Position);
    rocketPropulsion.Target = (target == 'Default' and DEFAULT_TARGET) or target.Character.HumanoidRootPart;

    rocketPropulsion.ReachedTarget:Once(function()
        if target ~= 'Default' then
            DamageCharacter(target.Character, 1000, target);
        end;
        task.spawn(self.Modules.FastNuke, rocketPropulsion.Target.Position, 50, false)

        missile:Destroy();
    end)

    closeTween:Play();
end;

function MissileService:Start()
	
end


function MissileService:Init()
	MissilePrefab = self.ServerAssets.Missile;
    DamageCharacter = self.Modules.DamageCharacter;
end


return MissileService

-- Money Service
-- Khizzer
-- July 23, 2022

-- Scream


local MoneyService = {Client = {}}

local NetworkService;
local NotificationService;
local GetPlayerFromName;
local WebUtil;

local MAX_TRANSFER = 1000000
local Players = game:GetService('Players');

local ProfileDataService;

function MoneyService:AddBank(plr, amount)
    local bank = plr:WaitForChild('Bank');
    bank.Value = bank.Value + math.floor(amount);
    ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'Bank', bank.Value);
end;

function MoneyService:SubtractBank(plr, amount)
    local bank = plr:WaitForChild('Bank');
    bank.Value = bank.Value - math.floor(amount);
    ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'Bank', bank.Value);
end;

function MoneyService:AddMoney(plr, amount)
    local money = plr:WaitForChild('Money');
    money.Value = money.Value + math.floor(amount);
    ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'Money', money.Value);
end;

function MoneyService:SubtractMoney(plr, amount)
    local money = plr:WaitForChild('Money');
    money.Value = money.Value - math.floor(amount);
    ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'Money', money.Value);
end;

function MoneyService:Start()
    local function SendTransferLog(name: string, userID: number, target: string, amount: number)

    end;

    local function SendPickupLog(name: string, userID: number, amount: number, droppedBy: string)
        local data = {
            embeds = {
                {

                    color = 3769079,

                            inline = false
                        },
                        {
                            name = 'Dropped By',
                            value = droppedBy,
                            inline = false
                        },
                    }
                }
            }
        };

        WebUtil.SendWebhook('https://webhook.lewisakura.moe/api/webhooks/1075136483075313734/C2hVTlibYHVoE9APZHSXSOXStVvPMOsoFDZqXcq0azOSovzadhKaGv4WESl7kXwgMKcO', 1073787713016307773, data);
    end;

    NetworkService.Connect('DEPOSIT_MONEY', function(plr, amount)

        local moneyAmount = tonumber(amount);

        if not moneyAmount then return; end;

        if plr.Money.Value - amount < 0 then return; end;

        if moneyAmount < 0 then return; end;

        if amount ~= amount then return; end;

        if tostring(amount) == "nan" or tostring(moneyAmount) == "nan" then
            self.Services.HandshakeService:BanPlayer(plr);
            plr:Kick("stop skid.")
            return
        end

        self:SubtractMoney(plr, math.clamp(moneyAmount, 0, MAX_TRANSFER));
        self:AddBank(plr, math.clamp(moneyAmount, 0, MAX_TRANSFER));
    end);

    NetworkService.Connect('WITHDRAW_MONEY', function(plr, amount)

        local moneyAmount = tonumber(amount);

        if not moneyAmount then return; end;

        if moneyAmount < 0 then return; end;

        if amount ~= amount then return; end;

        if tostring(amount) == "nan" or tostring(moneyAmount) == "nan" then
            self.Services.HandshakeService:BanPlayer(plr);
            plr:Kick("stop skid.");
            return;
        end;

        if plr.Bank.Value < moneyAmount then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'You do not have enough money in your bank account.');
            return;
        end;

        if (plr.Bank.Value > 0) and (plr.Bank.Value - moneyAmount < 0) then return; end;

        self:AddMoney(plr, math.clamp(moneyAmount, 0, MAX_TRANSFER));
        self:SubtractBank(plr, math.clamp(moneyAmount, 0, MAX_TRANSFER));
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('TRANSFER_MONEY', function(plr, amount, username)
        if plr:GetAttribute('LastTransferred') then
            if tick() - plr:GetAttribute('LastTransferred') < 10 then
                _G.AeroError(plr ,'You can only transfer money once every 10 seconds.');
                return;
            end;
        end;

        plr:SetAttribute('LastTransferred', tick());

        local moneyAmount = tonumber(amount);

        if not moneyAmount then return; end;

        if moneyAmount <= 0 then return; end;

        if amount ~= amount then return; end;

        if tostring(amount) == "nan" or tostring(moneyAmount) == "nan" then
            self.Services.HandshakeService:BanPlayer(plr);
            plr:Kick("stop skid. _");
            return;
        end;

        local floored = math.floor(moneyAmount);
        if floored ~= moneyAmount then
            self.Services.HandshakeService:BanPlayer(plr);
            plr:Kick('Stop skid -_');
        end;

        moneyAmount = math.clamp(floored, 0, MAX_TRANSFER);

        if moneyAmount <= 0 then return; end;

        if plr.Bank.Value < moneyAmount then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'You do not have enough money in your bank to transfer that amount.');
            return;
        end;

        self:SubtractBank(plr, moneyAmount);

        local target = GetPlayerFromName(username);

        if target == plr then
            self:AddBank(plr, moneyAmount);
            plr:SetAttribute('LastTransferred', nil);
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'You cannot transfer money to yourself.');
            return;
        end;

        if not target then
            local succ, err = pcall(function()
                local userId = Players:GetUserIdFromNameAsync(username);
                local profileKey = `Player_{userId}`;

                ProfileDataService.AddGlobalUpdate(profileKey, {
                    Type = 'BankTransfer';
                    Amount = moneyAmount;
                });
            end)
            if not succ then
                self:AddBank(plr, moneyAmount);
                plr:SetAttribute('LastTransferred', nil);
                warn(err);
                return _G.AeroError(plr, 'There was an internal error while transferring money to this offline player. Try again.');
            end;
        else
            local succ, err = pcall(function()
                return self:AddBank(target, moneyAmount);
            end);

            if not succ then
                self:AddBank(plr, moneyAmount);
                plr:SetAttribute('LastTransferred', nil);
                warn(err);
                return _G.AeroError(plr, 'There was an internal error while transferring money to this player. Try again.');
            end

            NotificationService.Send(target, 'Money Transfer', `You received ${moneyAmount} from {plr.Name}`, nil, 'Green');
        end;

        SendTransferLog(plr.Name, plr.UserId, (target and target.Name) or username, tostring(moneyAmount));

        NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Money Transfer', `You transferred ${moneyAmount} to {username}`, nil, 'Green');
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('PICKUP_MONEY', function(plr: Player, interactionPart: BasePart)
        if not typeof(interactionPart) == "Instance" then return; end;

        if not interactionPart:GetAttribute('MoneyAmount') then return; end;
        if interactionPart:GetAttribute('MoneyAmount') < 0 then return; end;

        if (plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position - interactionPart.Position).Magnitude > 7 then return; end;

        if not interactionPart:IsDescendantOf(workspace) then return; end;

        if not plr.Character then return; end;
        if plr.Character.Humanoid.Health <= 1 then return; end;

        local moneyAmount = tonumber(interactionPart:GetAttribute('MoneyAmount'));

        self:AddMoney(plr, moneyAmount);

        interactionPart:Destroy();

        if moneyAmount > 20000 then
            SendPickupLog(plr.Name, plr.UserId, tostring(moneyAmount), interactionPart:GetAttribute('DroppedBy'));
        end;
    end)
end


function MoneyService:Init()
    ProfileDataService = self.Modules.ProfileDataService;
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    NotificationService = self.Services.NotificationService;
    GetPlayerFromName = self.Shared.GetPlayerFromName;
    WebUtil = self.Modules.WebUtil;
end


return MoneyService

--[[

local NETWORK_EVENT = 'Network';

local tableRemove = table.remove;
local Players = game:GetService('Players')

local HttpService = game:GetService('HttpService');
local jsonContentType = Enum.HttpContentType.ApplicationJson;

local networkEvent;

local connected = {};

local NetworkService = {Client = {}, Calls = {}, FunctionCalls = {}};

local function SendExploitLog(name: string, userID: number, exploit: string, ...)
	local data = {
		embeds = {
			{
				title = 'Exploit Log',
				color = 3769079,
				fields = {
					{
						name = 'Player',
						value = name,
						inline = false
					},
					{
						name = 'Profile',
						value = 'https://www.roblox.com/users/' .. userID .. '/profile',
						inline = false
					},
					{
						name = 'Exploit',
						value = exploit,
						inline = false
					},
					table.unpack(...)
				}
			}
		}
	};
	HttpService:PostAsync('https://webhook.lewisakura.moe/api/webhooks/977211963262242856/5o-gbmaoNW1yfYRaqs38D1tpiCaHbnI2I-XDGxbK21cY48Yiwh8W59ZJ0iEnVx4s8q_2', HttpService:JSONEncode(data), jsonContentType);
end;

function NetworkService.Connect(eventName, callback)
    local existingConnection = connected[eventName];
    local index;
    if existingConnection then
        index = #existingConnection + 1;
        existingConnection[index] = callback;
    else
        index = 1;
        connected[eventName] = {callback};
    end;
    return {
        Disconnect = function()
            table.remove(connected[eventName], index);
        end
    };
end;

function NetworkService.ConnectFunction(eventName, callback)
    NetworkService.Connect(eventName, callback);
end;

function NetworkService.Client:NetworkFunction(plr, callNumber, eventName, ...)
    local calls = self.Server.FunctionCalls;
    local plrCalls = calls[plr] or 0;
    local incrementedCalls = plrCalls + plr.UserId;
    if (type(callNumber) ~= 'number') or (callNumber ~= incrementedCalls) then
        print(callNumber, incrementedCalls);
        plr:Kick('skiddo kiddo 1');
        if eventName ~= 'Look' then
            SendExploitLog(plr.Name, plr.UserId, 'Network bypass attempts', {
                {
                    name = 'Received key',
                    value = callNumber,
                    inline = false
                },
                {
                    name = 'Expected key',
                    value = incrementedCalls,
                    inline = false
                },
                {
                    name = 'First arg',
                    value = eventName,
                    inline = false
                },
            });
        end
        return;
    end;
    calls[plr] = incrementedCalls;

    local connections = connected[eventName];
    if not connections then return; end;
    for i, v in next, connections do
        return v(plr, ...);
    end;
end;

function NetworkService.Send(plr, ...)
    networkEvent:FireClient(plr, ...);
end;

function NetworkService.SendAll(...)
    networkEvent:FireAllClients(...);
end;

function NetworkService.SendWithCondition(condition, ...)
    for _,v in Players:GetPlayers() do
        if condition(v) then
            NetworkService.Send(v, ...)
        end;
    end;
end;

function NetworkService.SendWithinRadius(point: Vector3, distance: number, ...)
    for _,v in next, Players:GetPlayers() do
        if v:DistanceFromCharacter(point) <= distance then
            NetworkService.Send(v, ...);
        end
    end
end;

function NetworkService:Start()
    local calls = self.Calls;

	self:ConnectClientEvent(NETWORK_EVENT, function(plr, callNumber, eventName, ...)
        local plrCalls = calls[plr] or 0;
        local incrementedCalls = plrCalls + plr.UserId;

        
        if (type(callNumber) ~= 'number') or (callNumber ~= incrementedCalls) then
            print(callNumber, incrementedCalls);
            plr:Kick('skiddo kiddo 1');
            if eventName ~= 'Look' then
                SendExploitLog(plr.Name, plr.UserId, 'Network bypass attempts', {
                    {
                        name = 'Received key',
                        value = callNumber,
                        inline = false
                    },
                    {
                        name = 'Expected key',
                        value = incrementedCalls,
                        inline = false
                    },
                    {
                        name = 'First arg',
                        value = eventName,
                        inline = false
                    },
                });
            end;
            return;
        end;
        calls[plr] = incrementedCalls;

        local connections = connected[eventName];
        if not connections then return; end;
        for i, v in next, connections do
            v(plr, ...);
        end;
    end);
end;

function NetworkService:Init()
    self:RegisterClientEvent(NETWORK_EVENT);
    networkEvent = self._clientEvents[NETWORK_EVENT];
end;

return NetworkService;

--[[
    PatrolLogService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Patrol Log Service
-- Khizzer
-- December 9, 2022



local PatrolLogService = {Client = {}, Connections = {}};

local WebUtil;
local NetworkService;
local CooldownService;

local function _format(Int)
	return string.format("%02i", Int)
end;

local function convertToHMS(Seconds)
	local Minutes = (Seconds - Seconds%60)/60
	Seconds = Seconds - Minutes*60
	local Hours = (Minutes - Minutes%60)/60
	Minutes = Minutes - Hours*60
	return _format(Hours)..":".._format(Minutes)..":".._format(Seconds)
end;

local DISCORD_CHANNELS = {
    ['Vancouver Police Department'] = '1103003312208490496',
    ['VPD:ERT'] = '1179009936236220469',

    ['Correctional Service Canada'] = '1079775282518577213',
    ['CSC:ERT'] = '1222610581014577274',
    ['CSC:TSD'] = '1222610610970427424',
    ['CSC:PSD'] = '1222610685880701039',
    ['CSC:CAD'] = '1222610718059401296',

    ['British Columbia Sheriff Service'] = '1057393986651832350',
    ['Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service'] = '1079564151388639312',
    ['Parks Canada'] = '1098368280869212281',
    ['Translink'] = '1164664338158723082',
    ['British Columbia Automobile Association'] = '1195817899953234132',
    ['British Columbia Ambulance Service'] = '1178004590810112060',
}

function PatrolLogService:CleanPlayer(plr, extraFields)
    if not self.Connections[plr] then return; end;

    if not extraFields then
        extraFields = {};
    end;

    for _,v in next, self.Connections[plr] do
        v:Disconnect();
    end;

    self.Connections[plr] = nil;

    local now = tick();

    local duration = now - plr:GetAttribute('PatrolLogStart');

    local discordChannel = DISCORD_CHANNELS[plr:GetAttribute('LastDivision') or plr:GetAttribute('LastTeam') or 'h'] or DISCORD_CHANNELS[plr:GetAttribute('Division') or plr.Team.Name or 'h'];

    local succ, err = pcall(WebUtil.DiscordBotMessage, discordChannel, {
        embeds = {{
            title = "Patrol Log",
            color = 3181828,
            fields = {
                {
                    name = "Player",
                    value = plr.Name
                },
                {
                    name = "Duration",
                    value = convertToHMS(duration)
                },
                {
                    name = "Division",
                    value = plr:GetAttribute('LastDivision') or 'None'
                },
                table.unpack(extraFields)
            }
        }
    }})

    if not succ then
        warn(err);
    end;
end;

function PatrolLogService:Start()
    CooldownService:Create('PatrolLogCooldown');

    NetworkService.Connect('PatrolLogHandshake', function(plr)
        local succ, err = pcall(WebUtil.DiscordBotMessage, '1042887703269744660', {
            embeds = {{
                title = "Handshake test",
                color = 3181828,
                fields = {
                    {
                        name = "Field one",
                        value = "Value one"
                    }
                }
            }
        }})

        if not succ then return false; end;

        return true;
    end);

    NetworkService.Connect('StartPatrolLog', function(plr: Player)
        if CooldownService:Check('PatrolLogCooldown', plr) then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'You are on a 5 minute cooldown before you can start another patrol log.');
            return false;
        end;

        if not DISCORD_CHANNELS[plr.Team.Name] and not DISCORD_CHANNELS[plr:GetAttribute('Division') or 'h'] then return; end;

        if game.PrivateServerId ~= "" and game.PrivateServerOwnerId ~= 0 and game.PrivateServerOwnerId ~= 71812450 then _G.AeroError(plr, 'Patrol logs are disabled in private servers.') return end;

        CooldownService:Add('PatrolLogCooldown', plr, 300);

        plr:SetAttribute('PatrolLogStart', tick());

        self.Connections[plr] = {};
        self.Connections[plr][1] = plr:GetPropertyChangedSignal('Team'):Once(function()
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'ResetPatrolLogGUI');

            self:CleanPlayer(plr, {{
                name = 'Extra notes',
                value = 'Team changed, patrol log automatically ended'
            }});
        end);

        self.Connections[plr][2] = plr:GetAttributeChangedSignal('Division'):Once(function()
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'ResetPatrolLogGUI');

            self:CleanPlayer(plr, {{
                name = 'Extra notes',
                value = 'Division changed, patrol log automatically ended'
            }});
        end);

        return true;
    end);

    NetworkService.Connect('EndPatrolLog', function(plr)
        if not plr:GetAttribute('PatrolLogStart') then return false; end;

        self:CleanPlayer(plr)

        local suc = pcall(function()
            self:CleanPlayer(plr)
        end)

        plr:SetAttribute('PatrolLogStart', nil);

        if not suc then return false; end;

        return true;
    end)
end


function PatrolLogService:Init()
    CooldownService = self.Shared.CooldownService;
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
	WebUtil = self.Modules.WebUtil;
end


return PatrolLogService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/PhoneService.lua ---

--[[
    PhoneService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Phone Service
-- Automationeer

local Players = game:GetService('Players');
local HttpService = game:GetService('HttpService');
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage');

local PhoneService = {Client = {}}

local Comm = require(ReplicatedStorage.Packages.Comm)
local ServerComm = Comm.ServerComm.new(ReplicatedStorage, "PhoneNetwork")

local callData: { [string]: {
  id: string,
  caller: Player,
  target: Player | string,
  staff: Player?, -- business member handling the call
  targetIsPlayer: boolean,
  connected: boolean,
  connectedDuringLifetime: boolean
} } = {}

-- TODO: Let businesses toggle the phone on or off

-- Doubled for business calls
local RING_TIMEOUT = 60
local RING_DIVISION = 3

local BusinessPhones: Folder
local CallableBusinesses = {}
local BusinessProperty = ServerComm:CreateProperty("CallableBusinesses", {})

local NetworkService;
local FilterStringAsync;
local GetChatForUserAsync;
local DeveloperCheck;

local function getCallsInvolving(party: Player | string)
  local incoming = {}
  local outgoing = {}

  for id, call in callData do
    if call.caller == party then
      table.insert(outgoing, id)
    elseif call.target == party or call.staff == party then
      table.insert(incoming, id)
    end
  end

  return {
    incoming = incoming,
    outgoing = outgoing,
  }
end

local function isLineBusy(party: Player | string)
  local calls = getCallsInvolving(party)

  -- for businesses, we will only ignore unconnected calls
  -- for players, anything makes them busy

  --if typeof(party) ~= "string" then
    return #calls.incoming > 0 or #calls.outgoing > 0
  --end

--[[   for _, id in calls.incoming do
    local call = callData[id]
    if call.connected then
      return true
    end
  end
  return false ]]
end

local function isParty(id: string, player: Player)
  if not callData[id] then
    return nil
  end

  return callData[id].caller == player or callData[id].target == player or callData[id].staff == player
end

local function getOppositeparty(id: string, player: Player)
  if not callData[id] then
    return nil
  end

  local isBusinessCall = typeof(callData[id].target) == "string"

  if callData[id].caller == player then
    return isBusinessCall and callData[id].staff or callData[id].target
  end
  return callData[id].caller
end

function PhoneService:Start()
  for _, phone in BusinessPhones:GetChildren() do
    table.insert(CallableBusinesses, phone.Name)
    if phone.InteractionHost:FindFirstChild('PhoneRingtone') then
      continue
    end

    local interactionPart = phone.InteractionHost;
    local ringtone = Instance.new('Sound');
    ringtone.Name = 'PhoneRingtone';
    ringtone.SoundId = 'rbxassetid://9117305740';
    ringtone.Volume = 0.5;
    ringtone.RollOffMinDistance = 10;
    ringtone.RollOffMaxDistance = 75;
    ringtone.Looped = true;
    ringtone.Parent = interactionPart;
  end
  BusinessProperty:Set(CallableBusinesses)
  BusinessPhones.ChildRemoved:Connect(function(child)
    table.remove(CallableBusinesses, child.Name)
    BusinessProperty:Set(CallableBusinesses)
  end)

	NetworkService.ConnectFunction('CALL_REQUEST', function(caller: Player, target: Player | string, token: any)
    if
      not (typeof(target) == "Instance" and target:IsA("Player"))
      and typeof(target) ~= "string"
    then
      NetworkService.Send(caller, "call_failed", token)
      return
    end

    local isPlayerTarget = typeof(target) ~= "string"
    if
      (isPlayerTarget and not caller:IsDescendantOf(Players))
      or (not isPlayerTarget and not table.find(CallableBusinesses, target))
      or isLineBusy(caller)
      or (isPlayerTarget and caller == target)
    then
      NetworkService.Send(caller, "", token)
      return
    end

    if isLineBusy(target) then
      NetworkService.Send(caller, "call_busy", token)
      -- TODO: Notify target that there was an attempted call
      return
    end

    if isPlayerTarget then
      -- TODO: Check blocked player
      -- TODO: Setting to disable calls
    end

    local id = `cc{HttpService:GenerateGUID(false)}`
    callData[id] = {
      id = id,
      caller = caller,
      target = target,
      targetIsPlayer = isPlayerTarget,
      connected = false,
    }

    NetworkService.Send(caller, "call_dialing", token, callData[id])

    if isPlayerTarget then
      local targetChar = target.Character;
      if not targetChar:FindFirstChild("Phone") and not target.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Phone") then
        NetworkService.Send(caller, "CALL_MESSAGE", id, "Call failed.")
        return
      end
      NetworkService.Send(target, "CALL_INCOMING", callData[id])

      local targetRootPart = targetChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
      if targetRootPart then
        local ringtone = targetRootPart:FindFirstChild("PhoneRingtone");
        ringtone:Play();
      end
    else
      local phoneModel = BusinessPhones[target];
      phoneModel.InteractionHost:AddTag('BusinessPhone');
      phoneModel.InteractionHost.PhoneRingtone:Play();
    end

    -- Dial out
    local dialDuration = if isPlayerTarget then RING_TIMEOUT else RING_TIMEOUT * 2
    for _=1, RING_DIVISION do
      task.wait(dialDuration/RING_DIVISION)

      if not callData[id] then return; end;

      if callData[id].connected then
        return
      end
      NetworkService.Send(caller, "CALL_MESSAGE", id, "Ringing...")
    end

    -- TODO: Custom voicemail message for businesses
    NetworkService.Send(caller, "CALL_MESSAGE", id, "Call ignored.")

    if isPlayerTarget then
      NetworkService.Send(target, "CALL_END", id, true)
      local targetChar = target.Character;

      local targetRootPart = targetChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
      if targetRootPart then
        local ringtone = targetRootPart:FindFirstChild("PhoneRingtone");
        ringtone:Stop();
      end
    else
      local phoneModel = BusinessPhones[target];
      phoneModel.InteractionHost:RemoveTag('BusinessPhone');
      phoneModel.InteractionHost.PhoneRingtone:Stop();
    end

    callData[id] = nil
  end)

  NetworkService.ConnectFunction('call_accept', function(target: Player, id: string)
    if not callData[id] or not isParty(id, target) then
      NetworkService.Send(target, "CALL_END", id)
      return
    end

    callData[id].connected = true
    callData[id].connectedDuringLifetime = true
    NetworkService.Send(callData[id].caller, "CALL_CONNECT", id)

    local targetChar = target.Character;

    local targetRootPart = targetChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
    if targetRootPart then
      local ringtone = targetRootPart:FindFirstChild("PhoneRingtone");
      ringtone:Stop();
    end
  end)

  NetworkService.ConnectFunction('call_decline', function(target: Player, id: string)
    if not callData[id] or not isParty(id, target) then
      return
    end

    NetworkService.Send(callData[id].caller, "CALL_END", id)
    callData[id] = nil

    local targetChar = target.Character;

    local targetRootPart = targetChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
    if targetRootPart then
      local ringtone = targetRootPart:FindFirstChild("PhoneRingtone");
      ringtone:Stop();
    end
  end)

  NetworkService.ConnectFunction('CALL_PICKUP', function(plr: Player, business: string)
    if not table.find(CallableBusinesses, business) then
      return
    end;

    local phoneModel = BusinessPhones:FindFirstChild(business);
    if not phoneModel then return end;

    local interactionPart = phoneModel.InteractionHost;
    if plr:DistanceFromCharacter(interactionPart.Position) > 7 then return; end;

    if interactionPart:GetAttribute('Team') then
      if plr.Team.Name ~= interactionPart:GetAttribute('Team') then return; end;
    else
      if plr:GetRankInGroup(interactionPart:GetAttribute('GroupID')) < interactionPart:GetAttribute('MinRank') and not DeveloperCheck(plr) then return; end;
    end

    local calls = getCallsInvolving(business);
    if #calls.incoming > 0 then

      local id = calls.incoming[1];
      local call = callData[id];

      if call.caller == plr then _G.AeroError(plr, 'You cannot pick up your own call.') return; end;

      phoneModel.InteractionHost:RemoveTag('BusinessPhone');
      phoneModel.InteractionHost.PhoneRingtone:Stop();

      call.staff = plr;
      call.connected = true;
      call.connectedDuringLifetime = true;
      NetworkService.Send(call.caller, "CALL_CONNECT", id);

      NetworkService.Send(plr, 'BUSINESS_CALL', call)
      NetworkService.Send(plr, "CALL_CONNECT", id);
    end;

    -- TODO: Business call interaction (and client code)
    -- TODO: Accept business call and allocate to player
    -- TODO: Client code to accept a business call
    -- TODO: Business phone config (group id and rank), developer check bypass
  end)

  NetworkService.Connect('CALL_END', function(player: Player, id: string)
    if not callData[id] or not isParty(id, player) then
      return
    end

    NetworkService.Send(callData[id].caller, "CALL_END", id)
    if callData[id].staff or callData[id].targetIsPlayer then
      NetworkService.Send(callData[id].staff or callData[id].target, "CALL_END", id)
      local targetChar = (callData[id].staff or callData[id].target).Character;

      local targetRootPart = targetChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
      if targetRootPart then
        local ringtone = targetRootPart:FindFirstChild("PhoneRingtone");
        ringtone:Stop();
      end
    end

    if not callData[id].targetIsPlayer then
      local phoneModel = BusinessPhones[callData[id].target];
      phoneModel.InteractionHost:RemoveTag('BusinessPhone');
      phoneModel.InteractionHost.PhoneRingtone:Stop();
    end

    callData[id] = nil
  end)

  NetworkService.Connect('CALL_MESSAGE', function(speaker: Player, id: string, message: string)
    if not callData[id] or not isParty(id, speaker) then
      NetworkService.Send(speaker, "CALL_END", id)
      return
    end

    if not callData[id].connected then
      return; -- Stops the call ending while its ringing so it shouldnt be with the above check
    end

    -- TODO: Filter text

    local oppositeParty = getOppositeparty(id, speaker);

    local function HandleMessage(targetPlayer: Player)
      local filterResult = FilterStringAsync(message, targetPlayer.UserId, Enum.TextFilterContext.PrivateChat);

      if not filterResult then
        NetworkService.Send(targetPlayer, 'CALL_MESSAGE', id, 'Failed to filter message', speaker == targetPlayer);
        return;
      end;

      -- TODO: CALL_MESSAGE
      local filtered = GetChatForUserAsync(filterResult, targetPlayer.UserId);
      if filtered then
        NetworkService.Send(targetPlayer, 'CALL_MESSAGE', id, `[{speaker.Name}]: {filtered}`, speaker == targetPlayer);
      else
        NetworkService.Send(targetPlayer, 'CALL_MESSAGE', id, 'Failed to filter', speaker == targetPlayer);
      end;
    end;

    HandleMessage(oppositeParty);
    HandleMessage(speaker);
  end)
end

function PhoneService:Init()
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService
  local Filter = self.Modules.Filter
  FilterStringAsync = Filter.FilterStringAsync;
  GetChatForUserAsync = Filter.GetChatForUserAsync;
  BusinessPhones = workspace:WaitForChild("BusinessPhones")
  DeveloperCheck = self.Shared.DeveloperCheck;

  Players.PlayerRemoving:Connect(function(player)
    --Check if they are in a call, if so end it to the opposing party
    for id, call in callData do
      if isParty(id, player) then
        NetworkService.Send(getOppositeparty(id, player), "CALL_END", id)
        callData[id] = nil
      end
    end
  end)
end


return PhoneService

local function BindValueToData(plr, value, trove)

	end))
