local function strSw(str: string, s: string)
	return str:sub(1, #s) == s
end

--Runs any migrations if the player has data before ProfileService was fully added
function PlayerService:_handleDataFixes(plr)
	local inventoryReset = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'InventoryReset');
	if not inventoryReset then
		local boughtCars = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'BoughtCars');
		for _,v in next, boughtCars or {} do
			if v.Inventory then
				v.Inventory = {};
			end;
		end;
		ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'BoughtCars', boughtCars);
		ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'InventoryReset', true);
	end;

	if not ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'MigratedBackpackLayouts') then
		ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'BackpackLayouts', GetData(plr, 'BackpackLayouts') or BACKPACK_TEMPLATE);
		ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'MigratedBackpackLayouts', true);
	else
		local l = false
		local layouts = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'BackpackLayouts')
		for _, layout in layouts do
			for i, tool in layout.Tools do
				if tool == '[LE] Sniper Rifle' then
					layout.Tools[i] = 'LE | Sniper Rifle'
					l = true
				end
			end
		end
		if l then ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'BackpackLayouts', layouts) end
	end;

	local fixedCarIds = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'FixedCarIds');

	local IDS_TO_FIX = {
		-- ['5005'] = 11;
		-- ['5010'] = 12;
		-- ['5009'] = 13;
		-- ['5008'] = 14;
		-- ['5006'] = 15;
		-- ['5007'] = 16;
		-- ['8575453755'] = 17;
		-- ['5432642'] = 18;
	}

	if not fixedCarIds then
		local boughtCars = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'BoughtCars') or {};
		for _,v in next, boughtCars do
			if typeof(v.ID) == 'string' then
				v.ID = tonumber(v.ID);
			end;
			if IDS_TO_FIX[tostring(v.ID)] then
				v.ID = IDS_TO_FIX[tostring(v.ID)];
			end;
		end;
		ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'BoughtCars', boughtCars);
		ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'FixedCarIds', true);
	end

	if not ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'MigratedRecords') then
		ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'ArrestRecord', GetData(plr, 'ArrestRecord') or {});
		ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'CitationRecord', GetData(plr, 'CitationRecord') or {});
		ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'MigratedRecords', true);
	end

	local renamedTools = {
		['Badge'] = 'CIU Badge',
		['Hunting rifle'] = 'Hunting Rifle',
		['SW5946'] = 'LE | SW5946',
		['[LE] Sniper Rifle'] = 'LE | Sniper Rifle'
	}

	local cars = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'BoughtCars') or {}
	local f = false
	for _, car in cars do
		for _, item in car.Inventory or {} do
			if renamedTools[item.Name] then
				item.Name = renamedTools[item.Name]
				f = true
			end

			local attr = item.Attributes or {}

			if attr.GunSlingName == "C8 CAF" then
				attr.Variant = "HoloSight"
				attr.GunSlingName = "C8 HS"
				f = true
			elseif attr.GunSlingName == "C8 CSOR" then
				attr.Variant = "ACOG"
				attr.GunSlingName = "C8 ACOG"
				f = true
			end

			if not attr.ToolSource then continue end
			if strSw(attr.ToolSource, "Inserted")
				or strSw(attr.ToolSource, "Purchased")
				or strSw(attr.ToolSource, "Spawned")
				or string.find(attr.ToolSource, " (NSEC)")
				or string.find(attr.ToolSource, " (GCPS)")
				or string.find(attr.ToolSource, " - ")
				then continue
			end
			if ServerStorage:FindFirstChild(`LE | {item.Name}`) then
				item.Name = `LE | {item.Name}`
				f = true
			end
		end
	end
	if f then ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'BoughtCars', cars) end

	local tools = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'CivilianTools') or {}
	local h = false
	for _, item in tools or {} do
		if renamedTools[item.Name] then
			item.Name = renamedTools[item.Name]
			h = true
		end
	end
	if h then ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'CivilianTools', tools) end
end;

local function playerHasFlag(plr: Player, criteria, groups)
	if table.find(criteria.Usernames, plr.Name) then
		return true
	end

	if table.find(criteria.UserIds, tostring(plr.UserId)) then
		return true
	end

	-- sighs
	for groupId, rank in groups do
		local rankRequire = criteria.Groups[groupId]
		if not rankRequire then
			break
		end

		if rank == rankRequire then
			return true, groupId
		-- if rank requirement is negative (<0) then it means greater or less than
		elseif rankRequire < 0 then
			if rank >= math.abs(rankRequire) then
				return true, groupId
			end
		end
	end

	return false
end

function PlayerService:HandleFlags(plr: Player)
	local flagData = TrelloService:GetFlagData(true)
	local groups = {}
	local groupNames = {}
	local adminLevel = 0

	for _, group in GroupService:GetGroupsAsync(plr.UserId) do
		groups[group.Id] = group.Rank
		groupNames[group.Id] = group.Name
	end

	for flag, criteria in flagData do
		local hasFlag, grp = playerHasFlag(plr, criteria, groups)

		if hasFlag and flag == "Banned" and not DeveloperCheck(plr) then
			plr:SetAttribute("Moderated", true)
			if grp then
				plr:Kick(`You are in banned group {groupNames[grp]} ({grp}). You must leave this group in order to play British Columbia games; please refer to the Trello board for further details.`)
			else
				plr:Kick("You are currently banned from British Columbia games. Please refer to the Trello board for further details.")
			end
			return false
		elseif hasFlag then
			plr:SetAttribute(flag, true)
			if AdminLevels[flag] and AdminLevels[flag] > adminLevel then
				adminLevel = AdminLevels[flag]
			end
		else
			plr:SetAttribute(flag, nil)
		end
	end

	plr:SetAttribute("AdminLevel", adminLevel)

	return true
end

function PlayerService:PlayerAdded(plr: Player)
	-- if not _G.Adonis then repeat task.wait() until _G.Adonis; end;
	LogsService:AddLog('Joins', `{plr.Name} joined`);
	plr:SetAttribute("Joined", os.time())

	if plr.AccountAge < MINIMUM_ACCOUNT_AGE and (not RunService:IsStudio()) then
		plr:Kick('You must be at least ' .. MINIMUM_ACCOUNT_AGE .. ' days old to play.');
		return;
	end;
	local succ, isDeveloper = pcall(DeveloperCheck, plr);
	if not succ then
		plr:Kick(FAILED_DATA_LOAD_MSG);
		return;
	end;

	-- handle bans and other permissions
	if self:HandleFlags(plr) == false then
		return
	end
	plr:SetAttribute('Developer', isDeveloper);

	if _G.ServerLocked and not (plr:GetAttribute("AdminLevel") > 0) and not isDeveloper and not _G.Whitelist[plr.UserId] then
		plr:SetAttribute("Moderated", true)
		plr:Kick("This server is locked.")
		return
	end

		task.wait(5); -- 5 second buffer to allow for patrol logs to be created, might just redo patrol log system this is kinda hacky

	sessionStorage.Name = plr.UserId;
	sessionStorage.Parent = playerSessionStorage;

	local trunkStorage = newInstance('Folder');
	trunkStorage.Name = 'Trunk';
	trunkStorage.Parent = sessionStorage;

	deathToolStorage.Name = 'DeathToolStorage';
	deathToolStorage.Parent = sessionStorage;

	boughtCarsStorage.Name = 'BoughtCars';

	boughtGamepassesStorage.Name = 'BoughtGamepasses';

	local money = newInstance('IntValue');
	money.Name = 'Money';

	self:_handleDataFixes(plr);

	local moneyData = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'Money');
	money.Value = moneyData
	money.Parent = plr;

	local bank = newInstance('IntValue');
	bank.Name = 'Bank';
	local bankData = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'Bank');

	if bankData < 0 then
		bankData = 0;
	end;

	bank.Value = bankData
	bank.Parent = plr;

	local prisonTime = newInstance('IntValue');
	prisonTime.Name = 'PrisonTime';
	local prisonTimeData = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'PrisonTime');
	prisonTime.Value = prisonTimeData or 0;
	prisonTime.Parent = plr;


	local car = newInstance('ObjectValue');
	car.Name = 'Car';

	boat.Name = 'Boat';
	boat.Parent = plr;

	motorbike.Name = 'Motorbike';
	motorbike.Parent = plr;

	transmissionKey.Name = 'TransmissionKey';

	BindValueToData(plr, transmissionKey, playerTrove);
	BindValueToData(plr, channelCycleKey, playerTrove);

	backpackLayouts.Name = 'BackpackLayouts';
	backpackLayouts.Parent = plr;

	local backpackData = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'BackpackLayouts');

	for i = 1, 20 do
		local layoutData = backpackData[`Layout{i}`];
		local layoutNumber = newInstance('IntValue');
		layoutNumber.Parent = backpackLayouts;
		layoutNumber.Name = tostring(i);
		layoutNumber:SetAttribute('Name', if layoutData then layoutData.Name else `Layout {i}`);

			if layoutData and layoutData.Tools[i2] then
				layoutNumber:SetAttribute('Slot'..tostring(i2), layoutData.Tools[i2])

	end;

	local SpeedingFine = GetPlayerData(plr, 'SpeedingFine');
	if SpeedingFine then
		plr:SetAttribute('SpeedingFine', SpeedingFine);
	end;

	local houseData = Instance.new('Folder');
	houseData.Name = 'House';
	houseData.Parent = sessionStorage;

	local boughtValue = Instance.new('BoolValue');
	boughtValue.Name = 'Bought'
	boughtValue.Parent = houseData;
	boughtValue.Value = GetPlayerData(plr, 'BoughtHouse') or false;

	local boughtTimeValue = Instance.new('IntValue');
	boughtTimeValue.Name = 'BoughtAt';
	boughtTimeValue.Parent = houseData;
	boughtTimeValue.Value = GetPlayerData(plr, 'BoughtHouseAt') or 0;
	--NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Elections', 'An election is currently ongoing! Go to the courthouse to vote!', nil, 'Purple');

	local firstTime = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'FirstTimeJoining');
	if firstTime == true then
		plr:SetAttribute('TutorialPrompt', true);
	end;

	if not plr:IsDescendantOf(Players) then return; end;
	plr:LoadCharacter();

	if prisonTimeData then
		if prisonTimeData > 1 then
			PrisonService.AddPrisonerSignal:Fire(plr, prisonTimeData);
		else
			local civilianToolData = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'CivilianTools');
			for _,v in next, civilianToolData do
				if workspace:GetAttribute('DoNotLoad') then break; end;

				local attributes = v.Attributes;
				local name = v.Name;

				local tool = ServerStorage:FindFirstChild(name);
				if tool and tool.Name ~= "Phone" then
					local newTool = tool:Clone();
					newTool.Parent = plr.Backpack;
					for attrName, attrValue in next, attributes do
						newTool:SetAttribute(attrName, attrValue);
					end;

					newTool:SetAttribute('DoNotSave', nil);
				end;
			end;
		end;
	end;

	plr:SetAttribute("LifeStart", os.time());
	LeaderboardService:Joined(plr);
	NotificationService.SendAll('Player Joined', plr.Name, plrImage, 'Yellow');

	local ok, err = pcall(function()
		if RunService:IsStudio() or game.PlaceId ~= 7197780083 then return end
		if plr:GetAttribute('Developer') then
			moneyLeaderboard:SetAsync(tostring(plr.UserId) .. 'D', ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'Bank') + ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'Money'));
			moneyLeaderboard:RemoveAsync(tostring(plr.UserId))
		else
			moneyLeaderboard:RemoveAsync(tostring(plr.UserId).. 'D')
			moneyLeaderboard:SetAsync(tostring(plr.UserId), ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'Bank') + ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'Money'));
		end
	end)
	if not ok then
		warn(`Could not update money leaderboard for {plr.Name}: {err}`)
	end
	ok, err = pcall(function()
		if RunService:IsStudio() or game.PlaceId ~= 7197780083 then return end
		sessionLogs:UpdateAsync(plr.UserId, function(data)
			if not data then data = {} end
			data[#data + 1] = { os.time(), tostring(game.JobId), #Players:GetPlayers() }
			return data
		end)
	end)
	if not ok then
		warn(`Could not log join event for {plr.Name}: {err}`)
	end

	if game.PrivateServerId ~= "" and game.PrivateServerOwnerId ~= 0 and game.PrivateServerOwnerId ~= 71812450 then return end;
	IncomeService:PlayerAdded(plr);
end;

function PlayerService:PlayerRemoving(plr: Player)
	LogsService:AddLog('Leaves', `{plr.Name} left`);
	local time = plr:GetAttribute('Joined')

	-- TODO: New tool saving system
	if not workspace:GetAttribute('DoNotLoad') then
		if (not plr:GetAttribute('LastTeam') or plr:GetAttribute('LastTeam') == 'Civilian') and plr:GetAttribute('Division') == nil then
			if CombatService:IsInCombat(plr) and (not shuttingDown) and (not plr:GetAttribute("Moderated")) then --Not shutting down, they left in combat
				CombatService:ResetCombat(plr);
				ToolService:ResetSavedCivilianTools(plr);
			elseif not CombatService:IsInCombat(plr) and (not shuttingDown) then --Not shutting down, they left normally
				ToolService:SaveCivilianTools(plr);
			elseif shuttingDown or plr:GetAttribute("Moderated") then --The game is shutting down, save tools anyway.
				ToolService:SaveCivilianTools(plr);
			end;
			if plr:GetAttribute('Ragdoll') then
				ToolService:ResetSavedCivilianTools(plr);
			end;
		end;
	end;

	self.Services.CarService.ClearCars(plr)

	if plr:GetAttribute('PatrolLogStart') then
		task.spawn(function()
			PatrolLogService:CleanPlayer(plr, {{
				name = 'Extra notes',
				value = 'Player left the game'
			}});
		end)
	end

	self.Services.MessageRecorderService:CleanPlayer(plr);

	--[[ local sessionStorage = playerSessionStorage:FindFirstChild(plrUserId);
	sessionStorage.Name = '_'..sessionStorage.Name; ]]

	if plr:GetAttribute('HandcuffedBy') ~= nil then
		local officer = plr:GetAttribute('HandcuffedBy');
		local officerPlayer = game.Players:FindFirstChild(officer);

		if officerPlayer then
			NetworkService.Send(officerPlayer, 'OfficerCuffAnimation', false);
			if officerPlayer.Character.Torso:FindFirstChildOfClass('WeldConstraint') then
				officerPlayer.Character.Torso:FindFirstChildOfClass('WeldConstraint'):Destroy();
      end;
		end;

		if (not shuttingDown) and (not plr:GetAttribute("Moderated")) then
			local jailTime
			if plr:GetAttribute('InZipties') then
				jailTime = 300
			elseif plr.Team.Name ~= "Prisoner" then
				local lastLTAA = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'LastLTAA')
				local timesLTAA = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'TimesLTAA')
				-- LTAA cooldown (1 day for every LTAA)
				if os.time() - lastLTAA > (math.clamp(timesLTAA, 5, 30) * 86400) then
					timesLTAA = 0
				end

				-- LTAAs start at 1800 seconds (30 mins) and increase by 900 seconds (15 mins)
				-- for every LTAA, up to a cap of 8 hours (28800 seconds)
				jailTime = math.min(1800 + (timesLTAA * 900), 28800)
				ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'LastLTAA', os.time())
				ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'TimesLTAA', timesLTAA + 1)
			else
				jailTime = (15 * 60)
			end

			ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'PrisonTime', (ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'PrisonTime') or 0) + jailTime);
			if jailTime > 1800 then
				local minutes = math.ceil(jailTime / 60)
				NotificationService.SendAll('Left to Avoid Arrest', `{plr.Name} has been imprisoned for {minutes} minutes.`, nil, 'Black');
			else
				NotificationService.SendAll('Left to Avoid Arrest', `{plr.Name} has been automatically imprisoned.`, nil, 'Black');
			end
		end
	end;

	task.spawn(function()
		ProfileDataService:RemoveProfile(plr);
	end)

	local prisoner = PrisonService:GetPrisoner(plr);
	if prisoner then
		for i,v in PrisonService.Prisoners do
			if v.Username == plr.Name then
				table.remove(PrisonService.Prisoners, i);
			end;
		end;
	end;

	local callsigns = CallsignService.Callsigns;
	if callsigns[plr] then
		callsigns[plr] = nil;
	end;

	local lookEventLastFired = LookService.LastFired;
	if lookEventLastFired[plr] then
		lookEventLastFired[plr] = nil;
	end;

	local carSpawnerLastSpawned = CarSpawnerService.LastSpawned;
	if carSpawnerLastSpawned[plr] then
		carSpawnerLastSpawned[plr] = nil;
	end;

	if networkCalls[plr] then
		networkCalls[plr] = nil;
	end;

	if self.Services.FirefighterService.HiddenHats[plr] then
		for _,v in next, self.Services.FirefighterService.HiddenHats[plr] do
			v:Destroy()
		end;
		self.Services.FirefighterService.HiddenHats[plr] = nil;
	end

--[[ 	local gang = GangService:GetGangFromPlayer(plr);
	if gang then
		if gang.Leader == plr.Name then
			GangService:DisbandGang(gang.Name);
		else
			GangService:RemovePlayer(plr.Name);
		end;
	end; ]]

--[[ 	if sessionStorage then
		sessionStorage:Destroy();
	end; ]]

	local ok, err = pcall(function()
		if not time then return end
		if RunService:IsStudio() or game.PlaceId ~= 7197780083 then return end
		igt:IncrementAsync(plr.UserId, os.time() - time)
	end)
	if not ok then
		warn(`Could not update time leaderboard for {plr.Name}: {err}`)
	end
	ok, err = pcall(function()
		if RunService:IsStudio() or game.PlaceId ~= 7197780083 then return end
		sessionLogs:UpdateAsync(plr.UserId, function(data)
			if
				not data
				or data[#data][4]
				or data[#data][2] ~= tostring(game.JobId)
			then
				return data
			end
			data[#data][4] = os.time()
			data[#data][5] = #Players:GetPlayers()
			return data
		end)
	end)
	if not ok then
		warn(`Could not log leave event for {plr.Name}: {err}`)
	end

	LeaderboardService:Left(plr);
	local suc, plrImage = pcall(getUserThumbnailAsync, Players, plr.UserId, thumbnailType, thumbnailSize);
	if not suc then plrImage = nil; end;
	NotificationService.SendAll('Player Left', plr.Name, plrImage, 'Yellow');
end;

function PlayerService:Start()
	Character.SetToolModule(Tool);

	for _,v in next, game.ServerStorage:GetChildren() do
		if v:IsA('Tool') then
			v:SetAttribute('DoNotSave', true);
		end;
	end;

    for _,v in next, game.ReplicatedStorage.Cars:GetDescendants() do
        if v:IsA('IntValue') and v.Name == 'ID' then
            local car = v.Parent.Parent.Parent;
            local carName = car.Name;
            if carIDs[v.Value] then
							if carName ~= carIDs[v.Value] then
                warn('Duplicate car ID found: '..v.Value..' for '..carName..' and '..carIDs[v.Value]);
							end
            else
                carIDs[v.Value] = carName;
            end;
        end;
    end;

	for i, v in next, Players:GetPlayers() do
		coroutineWrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				self:PlayerAdded(v);
			end);
		end)();
	end;

	Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(plr)
		task.spawn(function()
			self:PlayerAdded(plr);
		end)
	end);

	Players.PlayerRemoving:Connect(function(plr)
		task.spawn(function()
			self:PlayerRemoving(plr);
		end)
	end);

	local function onShutdown(player)
		local jobMoney = player:GetAttribute('JobMoney')
		if jobMoney then
			MoneyService:AddBank(player, jobMoney);
			NotificationService.Send(player, 'Shutdown Job Money', `You have been given your job money of ${jobMoney}.`, nil, 'Green');
			player:SetAttribute('JobMoney', nil);
			player:LoadCharacter();
		end;

		local duffelBag = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild('Duffel Bag')
		if duffelBag and duffelBag:GetAttribute('Money') then
			duffelBag:Destroy()
			MoneyService:AddMoney(player, duffelBag:GetAttribute('Money'))
		end
		if player:FindFirstChild('Backpack') then
			for _, x in player.Backpack:GetChildren() do
				if x.Name == 'Duffel Bag' and x:GetAttribute('Money') then
					x:Destroy()
					MoneyService:AddMoney(player, duffelBag:GetAttribute('Money'))
				end
			end
		end

		self:PlayerRemoving(player)
	end

	game:BindToClose(function()
		shuttingDown = true;
		if RunService:IsStudio() then return end
		NetworkService.SendAll('PermanentAdminMessage', 'Server Restart', `This server is now being restarted. All players will be marked as having left and in a few moments your screen will briefly go black as you are automatically rejoined.`);

		for _, player in Players:GetPlayers() do
			task.spawn(onShutdown, player)
		end

		while 0 ~= 1 do
			task.wait(0.5)
		end
	end);

	self.Services.NetworkService.Connect('UpdateSetting', function(plr, settingName, newSetting)
		local settingsFolder = plr:FindFirstChild('Settings');

		ProfileDataService.SetCategorisedData(plr, 'Settings', settingName, newSetting);
		settingsFolder:SetAttribute(settingName, newSetting);
	end);

	self.Services.NetworkService.Connect('TutorialAcknowledged', function(plr)
		ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'FirstTimeJoining', false)
	end)
end;

function PlayerService:Init()
	Players.CharacterAutoLoads = false;
	local services = self.Services;

	DataService = self.Modules.DataService;
	GetData, SetData--[[, RemoveData]] = DataService.Get, DataService.Set--[[, DataService.Remove]];

	PrisonService = self.Services.PrisonService;
	LeaderboardService = services.LeaderboardService;
	NotificationService = services.NotificationService;
	MoneyService = services.MoneyService;
	CallsignService = services.CallsignService;
	LookService = services.LookService;
	CarSpawnerService = services.CarSpawner.CarSpawnerService;
	Tool = self:WrapModule(require(script:WaitForChild('Tool')));
	Character = self:WrapModule(require(script:WaitForChild('Character')));
	BoughtGamepasses = self:WrapModule(require(script:WaitForChild('BoughtGamepasses')));
	NetworkService = services.NetworkService;
	networkCalls = NetworkService.Calls;
	GangService = self.Services.GangService;
	DeveloperCheck = self.Shared.DeveloperCheck;
	ProfileDataService = self.Modules.ProfileDataService;
	PatrolLogService = services.PatrolLogService;
	IncomeService = services.IncomeService;
	CombatService = services.CombatService;
	ToolService = services.ToolService;
	TrelloService = services.TrelloService;
	LogsService = services.LogsService;
	Trove = self.Shared.Trove;
end;

return PlayerService;

--[[
    BoughtGamepasses (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → PlayerService
    Parent: PlayerService
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script

-- Bought Gamepasses
-- Khizzer
-- January 23, 2022

local MarketplaceService = game:GetService('MarketplaceService');

local BoughtGamepasses = {}
local DeveloperCheck;
local ProfileDataService;
local Gamepasses;

local generalGamepasses;
local gearGamepasses;

function BoughtGamepasses.Load(plr: Player)
    local function SetupGamepass(dataName: string, gamepassId: number, isGear: boolean)
        local data = ProfileDataService.GetCategorisedData(plr, if isGear then 'GearGamepasses' else 'RegularGamepasses' , dataName);

        local attributeName = if isGear then dataName:gsub("%s+", "") else dataName;

        plr:SetAttribute(attributeName, data);
        plr:GetAttributeChangedSignal(attributeName):Connect(function()
            ProfileDataService.SetCategorisedData(plr, if isGear then 'GearGamepasses' else 'RegularGamepasses', dataName, plr:GetAttribute(attributeName));
        end);
    
        if not plr:GetAttribute(attributeName) then
            pcall(function()
                local ownsGamepass = MarketplaceService:UserOwnsGamePassAsync(plr.UserId, gamepassId);
                plr:SetAttribute(attributeName, ownsGamepass);
    
                if not ownsGamepass then
                    plr:SetAttribute(attributeName, DeveloperCheck(plr));
                end;
            end)
        end
    end

    for attribute, tbl in generalGamepasses do
        local succ, err = pcall(function()
            SetupGamepass(attribute, tbl.Gamepass, false);
        end);

        if not succ then _G.AeroError(plr, 'Failed to load gamepasses. Try rejoining.') warn(err) end;
    end;

    for gamepassName, tbl in next, gearGamepasses do
        local succ, err = pcall(function()
            SetupGamepass(gamepassName, tbl.Gamepass, true);
        end)

        if not succ then _G.AeroError(plr, 'Failed to load gamepasses. Try rejoining.') warn(err) end;
    end;
end;

function BoughtGamepasses:Start()
    generalGamepasses = Gamepasses.RegularGamepasses;
    gearGamepasses = Gamepasses.GearGamepasses;
end

function BoughtGamepasses:Init()
    Gamepasses = self.Shared.Constants.Gamepasses;
    DeveloperCheck = self.Shared.DeveloperCheck;
    ProfileDataService = self.Modules.ProfileDataService;
end


return BoughtGamepasses

local newInstance = Instance.new;

local function CreateAttachment(name, parent, position)
    local attachment = newInstance('Attachment');
    attachment.Name = name;
    attachment.Position = position;
    attachment.Parent = parent;
    return attachment;
end;

local TEAMS_CAN_BE_CUFFED = {'Civilian', 'Prisoner', 'Legislative Assembly', 'Provincial Court'}

local attachments = {
    ['Neck'] = {'NeckAttachment', 'NeckAttachment2'},
    ['Right Shoulder'] = {'RightCollarAttachment', 'RightShoulderAttachment'},
    ['Left Shoulder'] = {'LeftCollarAttachment', 'LeftShoulderAttachment'},
    ['Right Hip'] = {'RightHipAttachment', 'RightLegAttachment'},
    ['Left Hip'] = {'LeftHipAttachment', 'LeftLegAttachment'}
};

local Character = {Client = {}};

function Character:_characterAdded(char: Model, plr: Player, trunkStorage, plrImage)
    if not char then return; end;
    char:SetAttribute("GUID", HttpService:GenerateGUID(false))
    plr:SetAttribute("CharacterGUID", char:GetAttribute("GUID"))

    if plr.Team.Name == 'Civilian' then
        if plr:GetAttribute('GiveBackCivilianTools') then
            plr:SetAttribute('GiveBackCivilianTools', nil);
            ToolService:LoadCivilianTools(plr);
        end
    end

    TODAYS_DATE = DateTime.now():FormatUniversalTime('L', 'en-us');

    local phoneRingtone = Instance.new('Sound');
    phoneRingtone.Name = 'PhoneRingtone';
    phoneRingtone.SoundId = 'rbxassetid://9113750564';
    phoneRingtone.Volume = 0.5;
    phoneRingtone.Looped = true;
    phoneRingtone.RollOffMinDistance = 10;
    phoneRingtone.RollOffMaxDistance = 50;

    local muffle = Instance.new('EqualizerSoundEffect');
    muffle.Name = 'Muffle';
    muffle.HighGain = -20;
    muffle.MidGain = -20;
    muffle.LowGain = 0;
    muffle.Enabled = true;
    muffle.Parent = phoneRingtone;

    phoneRingtone.Parent = char.HumanoidRootPart;

    task.defer(pcall, function()
        if plr:GetAttribute('Division') ~= nil then
            local divisionName = plr:GetAttribute('Division');
            local teamName = plr.Team.Name;
            local divisionFolder = DivisionStorage[teamName][divisionName];
            for _,v in next, divisionFolder.Tools:GetChildren() do
                if v:GetAttribute('MinimumRank') then
                    if plr:GetRankInGroup(divisionFolder:GetAttribute('GroupID')) >= v:GetAttribute('MinimumRank') or DeveloperCheck(plr) then
                        local tool = v:Clone();
                        tool.Parent = plr.Backpack;
                        tool:SetAttribute('ToolSource', `{plr.Name} ({divisionName}) ({TODAYS_DATE})`);
                        tool:SetAttribute('UserName', plr.Name)
                    end;
                end;
            end
        else
            for i,v in next, plr.Team:GetChildren() do
                if v:IsA('Tool') then
                    if v:GetAttribute('MinimumRank') then
                        if (plr:GetRankInGroup(plr.Team:GetAttribute('GroupID')) >= v:GetAttribute('MinimumRank')) or DeveloperCheck(plr) then
                            local tool = v:Clone();
                            tool.Parent = plr.Backpack;
                            tool:SetAttribute('ToolSource', `{plr.Name} ({plr.Team.Name}) ({TODAYS_DATE})`);
                            tool:SetAttribute('UserName', plr.Name)
                        end;
                    end;
                elseif v:IsA('Shirt') then
                    local old = plr.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass('Shirt');
                    if old then old:Destroy(); end;
                    local shirt = Instance.new('Shirt');
                    shirt.Parent = plr.Character;
                    shirt.ShirtTemplate = v.ShirtTemplate;
                elseif v:IsA('Pants') then
                    local old = plr.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass('Pants');
                    if old then old:Destroy(); end;
                    local pants = Instance.new('Pants');
                    pants.Parent = plr.Character;
                    pants.PantsTemplate = v.PantsTemplate;
                end;
            end;
        end;
    end)

    plr:SetAttribute('Ragdoll', nil);

    local humanoid = char:WaitForChild('Humanoid') :: Humanoid;
    local rootPart = char:WaitForChild('HumanoidRootPart');
    local torso = char:WaitForChild('Torso');

    CollectionService:AddTag(rootPart, 'HRT')
    for _,v in next, TEAMS_CAN_BE_CUFFED do
        if string.find(plr.Team.Name, v) then
            CollectionService:AddTag(rootPart, 'HumanoidRootPart');
        end;
    end;

    if not WhitelistedTeams.CheckLEO(plr) and WhitelistedTeams.CheckEmergencyServices(plr) then
        humanoid.Health = math.huge;
        humanoid.MaxHealth = math.huge;
    end;

    local ballConstraints = {};

    if plr:GetAttribute('Division') ~= nil then
        task.delay(0.3, function()
            local divisionName = plr:GetAttribute('Division');
            if DivisionSpawns:FindFirstChild(divisionName) then
                local spawns = DivisionSpawns[divisionName]:GetChildren();
                local randomSpawn = spawns[math.random(1, #spawns)]
                char:PivotTo(CFrame.new(randomSpawn.Position))
            end
        end)
    end;

    local boughtGearGamepasses = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'GearGamepasses');

    for toolName, isBought in next, boughtGearGamepasses do
        if not isBought then continue; end;
        if plr.Team == game.Teams.Civilian then
            if game.ServerStorage:FindFirstChild(toolName) then
                local _tool = game.ServerStorage[toolName];
                local toolClone = _tool:Clone();
                toolClone.Parent = plr.Backpack;
                toolClone:SetAttribute("DoNotSave", true);
                toolClone:SetAttribute("ToolSource", `Game pass item for {plr.Name}`)
                if toolClone.Name == "PAL" then
                    toolClone:SetAttribute("DoNotRemove", true);
                end
            end
        end;
    end;

    for i, v in next, trunkStorage:GetChildren() do
        v:Destroy();
    end;

    char.ChildAdded:Connect(function(child)
        if child:IsA('Tool') then
            Tool.WeldTool(child);
        end;
    end);

    CarService.ClearCars(plr)

    if self.Services.FirefighterService.HiddenHats[plr] then
        for _,v: Accessory in next, self.Services.FirefighterService.HiddenHats[plr] do
            v:Destroy();
        end;
        self.Services.FirefighterService.HiddenHats[plr] = {};
    end

    humanoid.Died:Connect(function()
        if not humanoid:GetAttribute('SurpressNotifications') then
            NotificationService.SendAll('Player Died', plr.Name, plrImage, 'Red');
        end
	end);

    local socketContainer = newInstance('Folder');
    socketContainer.Name = 'SocketContainer';
    socketContainer.Parent = char;

    CreateAttachment('NeckAttachment2', char:WaitForChild('Head'), Vector3.new(0, -0.5, 0));
    CreateAttachment('RightHipAttachment', torso, Vector3.new(0.5, -1, 0));
    CreateAttachment('LeftHipAttachment', torso, Vector3.new(-0.5, -1, 0));
    CreateAttachment('LeftLegAttachment', char:WaitForChild('Left Leg'), Vector3.new(0, 1, 0));
    CreateAttachment('RightLegAttachment', char:WaitForChild('Right Leg'), Vector3.new(0, 1, 0));

    for i, v in next, torso:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('Motor6D') then
            local socket = newInstance('BallSocketConstraint')
            socket.Attachment0 = torso[attachments[v.Name][1]];
            socket.Attachment1 = char:FindFirstChild(attachments[v.Name][2], true);
            socket.Parent = socketContainer;
            socket.Enabled = false;
            ballConstraints[#ballConstraints+1] = socket;
            --v:Destroy();
        end;
    end;

    local function Ragdoll(state: boolean)
        for _, v: BallSocketConstraint in next, ballConstraints do
            v.Enabled = state;
        end;
        for i, v in next, torso:GetChildren() do
            if v:IsA('Motor6D') then
                v.Enabled = not state;
            end;
        end;
    end;

    humanoid.HealthChanged:Connect(function(health)
        if health <= 1 then
            if not char.Parent then return; end;
            Ragdoll(true);
            if health > 0 then
                humanoid:SetAttribute('PlayerTeam', plr.Team.Name)
                for _, tool in plr.Backpack:GetChildren() do
                    -- Move to death storage
                end
                -- Also move tools in character
                if not humanoid:GetAttribute('SurpressNotifications') then
                    NotificationService.SendAll('Player Downed', plr.Name, plrImage, 'Red');
                end
            end
            NetworkService.Send(plr ,'SetInventoryEnabled', false);
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'SetDownedGUI', true)

            local rootPartCFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame;

            local plrMoney = plr.Money.Value;

            if plrMoney > 0 and not char:GetAttribute("DroppedMoney") then
                local dropAmount = math.floor(math.random(1, plr.Money.Value/2));
                char:SetAttribute("DroppedMoney", true)
                if dropAmount >= 1 then
                    local moneyDrop = MONEY_PART:Clone();
                    moneyDrop.Parent = workspace;
                    moneyDrop.CFrame = rootPartCFrame * CFrame.new(0, 0, -1);
                    moneyDrop.Velocity = (-rootPartCFrame.RightVector * math.random(6, 8)) + (-rootPartCFrame.UpVector * math.random(1.2, 1.5)) + UP_VELOCITY;
                    moneyDrop.RotVelocity = Vector3.new(math.random(8), math.random(8), math.random(8));
                    moneyDrop:SetAttribute('MoneyAmount', dropAmount);
                    moneyDrop:SetAttribute('DroppedBy', plr.Name);
                    MoneyService:SubtractMoney(plr, dropAmount);
                end
            end
        elseif health > 1 then
            if not char.Parent then return; end;
            Ragdoll(false);
        end;
        if humanoid.Health == 1 and rootPart.Parent then
            CollectionService:AddTag(rootPart.Parent.Head, 'Revive');
        elseif humanoid.Health ~= 1 and rootPart.Parent then
            CollectionService:RemoveTag(rootPart.Parent.Head, 'Revive');
        end;
    end);

	if typeof(plr:GetAttribute("DisplayName")) == "string" then
        char.Humanoid.DisplayName = plr:GetAttribute("DisplayName");
    else
        char.Humanoid.DisplayName = plr.Name;
    end

--[[     for _,v in next, char:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('BasePart') then
            v.CollisionGroup = 'Character';
        end;
    end; ]]

    local accessoryRemovedConnection = char.ChildRemoved:Connect(function(child)
        local childIsAccessory = child:IsA('Accessory');
        local childIsTool = child:IsA('Tool');
        if (childIsAccessory or childIsTool) and (child.Parent == workspace) then
            plr:Kick(`Status 9024, please report this to a developer, mention: ({child.Name})`);
            warn(`{plr.Name} removed {child.Name} from their character.`)
            child:Destroy();
        end;
    end);

    local humanoidRemovedConnection = char.ChildRemoved:Connect(function(child)
        if humanoid == child then
            warn(plr,"'s humanoid was removed");
            plr:LoadCharacter();
        end
        if humanoid and humanoid.RootPart == child then --char:BreakJoints()
            warn(plr,"'s humanoidrootpart was removed whilst being alive? This may be lag or an exploiter.")
        end;
    end);

    char.Destroying:Connect(function()
        accessoryRemovedConnection:Disconnect()
        humanoidRemovedConnection:Disconnect()
    end)

    plr.CharacterAppearanceLoaded:Wait();

    for _,v in char:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('CharacterMesh') then
            if not table.find(WHITELISTED_MESHES, v.MeshId) then
                v:Destroy();
            end
        end;
    end;

    char:SetAttribute("Spawned", os.time())
end;


function Character.SetToolModule(toolModule)
    Tool = toolModule;
end;

function Character:Setup(plr: Player, trunkStorage, plrImage)
    self:_characterAdded(plr.Character, plr, trunkStorage, plrImage);

    plr.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(char)
        self:_characterAdded(char, plr, trunkStorage, plrImage);
    end);
end;

function Character:Start()
    NetworkService.Connect('ToggleNameHide', function(plr: Player)
        if plr.Team.Name ~= 'Civilian' and plr.Team.Name ~= 'Prisoner' and plr:GetAttribute('Division') ~= 'POU' and plr:GetAttribute('Division') ~= 'GCPS' then return; end;

        local humanoid = plr.Character:WaitForChild('Humanoid');
        if humanoid.DisplayName == " " then
            humanoid.DisplayName = if typeof(plr:GetAttribute("DisplayName")) == "string" then plr:GetAttribute("DisplayName") else plr.Name
        else
            humanoid.DisplayName = " "
        end;
    end)
end;

function Character:Init()
	NotificationService = self.Services.NotificationService;
	CarService = self.Services.CarService;
    DeveloperCheck = self.Shared.DeveloperCheck;
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    WhitelistedTeams = self.Shared.Constants.WhitelistedTeams;
    MONEY_PART = self.ServerAssets.MoneyPart;
    MoneyService = self.Services.MoneyService;
    ToolService = self.Services.ToolService;
    ProfileDataService = self.Modules.ProfileDataService;
end;

return Character;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/PlayerService_contents/Tool.lua ---

--[[
    Tool (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → PlayerService
    Parent: PlayerService
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local ServerStorage = game:GetService("ServerStorage")
local newInstance = Instance.new;

local Tool = {Client = {}};

function Tool.WeldTool(tool: Tool)
    if tool:GetAttribute('IsWelded') then return; end;
    tool:SetAttribute('IsWelded', true);
    local handle = tool:FindFirstChild('Handle');
    if not handle then return; end;
    local handleCFrame = handle.CFrame;


    for i, v in next, tool:GetDescendants() do
        if (v:IsA('BasePart') or v:IsA('Seat')) and not v:GetAttribute('NoWeld') then
            local weld = newInstance('Weld');
            weld.Part0 = v;
            weld.Part1 = handle;
            weld.C0 = v.CFrame:Inverse() * handleCFrame;
            weld.Parent = v;
            v.Anchored = false;
        end;
    end;
end;


function Tool:SetupBackpack(backpack: Backpack)
    if not backpack then return; end;

    for _, v in next, backpack:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('Tool') then
            self.WeldTool(v);
            v.CanBeDropped = false;
        end;
    end;

    backpack.ChildAdded:Connect(function(child)
        if child:IsA('Tool') then
            self.WeldTool(child);
            child.CanBeDropped = false;
        end;
    end);

end;

function Tool:Setup(plr)
    self:SetupBackpack(plr:FindFirstChild('Backpack'));

    plr.ChildAdded:Connect(function(child)
        if child:IsA('Backpack') then
            self:SetupBackpack(child);

            if plr.Team.Name ~= 'Prisoner' then
                local phone = ServerStorage.Phone:Clone()
                phone:SetAttribute("DoNotSave", nil)
                phone.Parent = child;
            end
        end;
    end);
end;

function Tool:Start()

end;

function Tool:Init()

end;

return Tool;

--[[
    PrisonService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Prison Service
-- Khizzer, LG
-- June 20, 2021

local Notifications;
local ToolService;
local Signal;
local NetworkService;
local ProfileDataService;

local MarketplaceService = game:GetService('MarketplaceService')
local Prisoner;

local PrisonService = {Client = {}, Prisoners = {}, AddPrisonerSignal = nil}

local releaseGUIPrefab = game:GetService('ServerStorage'):WaitForChild('Character'):WaitForChild('ReleaseGUI');

function PrisonService:GetPrisoner(plr)
    for _,v in self.Prisoners do
        if v.Player == plr then
            return v;
        end;
    end;
    return;
end;

function PrisonService:Start()
    self.AddPrisonerSignal = Signal.new();

    self.AddPrisonerSignal:Connect(function(target, time)
        local prisoner = self:GetPrisoner(target);
        if prisoner then
            prisoner:SetTime(prisoner.Time + time)
            target:SetAttribute('HandcuffedBy', nil);
            target:SetAttribute('GrabbedBy', nil);
            target:SetAttribute('Division', nil);
            target:LoadCharacter();
            return
        end

        ToolService:ResetSavedCivilianTools(target);

        local inmate = Prisoner.new(target, time)
        inmate:SetTime(time);

        self.Prisoners[#self.Prisoners + 1] = inmate;
        task.delay(0.5, target.LoadCharacter, target);
        target:SetAttribute('HandcuffedBy', nil);
        target:SetAttribute('GrabbedBy', nil);
        target:SetAttribute('Division', nil);
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('Bail', function(plr)
        local prisoner = self:GetPrisoner(plr);
        if not prisoner then return end;
        if prisoner.Time >= 1500 then return end;

        local devProductID;

        if prisoner.Time > 0 and prisoner.Time < 300 then
            devProductID = 1736534827
        elseif prisoner.Time >= 300 and prisoner.Time < 600 then
            devProductID = 1736534814
        elseif prisoner.Time > 600 then
            devProductID = 1736534810;
        end;

        if devProductID == nil then _G.AeroError(plr, 'Error prompting bail, time is invalid. Report this to a developer') return end;

        local lastPurchasedBail: number = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'LastPurchasedBail');
        --check if lastpurchasedbail from now is less than 24 hours
        if os.time() - lastPurchasedBail < 86400 then
            local hoursRemaining = math.floor((86400 - (os.time() - lastPurchasedBail)) / 3600);
            if hoursRemaining >= 1 then
                _G.AeroError(plr, `You have already purchased bail in the last 24 hours. Please wait {hoursRemaining} hours.`);
            else
                local minutesRemaining = math.floor((86400 - (os.time() - lastPurchasedBail)) / 60);
                _G.AeroError(plr, `You have already purchased bail in the last 24 hours. Please wait {minutesRemaining} minutes.`);
            end
            return;
        end;
        if os.time() - lastPurchasedBail < 259200 then
            print('Purchased bail in the previous 72 hours')
        end

        MarketplaceService:PromptProductPurchase(plr, devProductID)
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('PrisonRelease', function(plr)
        if plr:GetAttribute('Releasing') then return end
        if plr.Team.Name ~= "Prisoner" then return end

        local inmate = self:GetPrisoner(plr);
        if not inmate then
            _G.AeroError(plr, "You cannot be released. Try rejoining.")
            return
        end

        if inmate.Time > 0 then
            _G.AeroError(plr, "Your sentence has not expired.")
            return
        end

        if plr:GetAttribute('HandcuffedBy') then
            _G.AeroError(plr, "You are currently handcuffed.")
            return
        end

        local char = plr.Character
        local humanoid = char and char:FindFirstChildOfClass('Humanoid')
        local head = char and char:FindFirstChild('Head')
        if not humanoid and not head then
            _G.AeroError(plr, "Character not valid.")
            return
        end

        if humanoid.Health <= 1 then
            _G.AeroError(plr, "You are downed or dead.")
            return
        end

        if workspace:FindFirstChild('PrisonRadius') then
            local inPrison = false
            for _, x in workspace:GetPartsInPart(workspace.PrisonRadius) do
                if x:IsDescendantOf(plr.Character) then
                    inPrison = true
                end
            end
            if not inPrison then
                _G.AeroError(plr, "You either have escaped or are not in a prisoner area.")
                return
            end
        end

        plr:SetAttribute('Releasing', true)

        if humanoid.Sit then
            humanoid.Jump = true
            task.wait(0.1)
        end

        humanoid.WalkSpeed = 0
        humanoid.JumpPower = 0

        local releaseGUI = releaseGUIPrefab:Clone()
        local timeLabel = releaseGUI.ReleaseLabel.TimeLabel
        releaseGUI.Parent = head
        releaseGUI.Adornee = head

        for i = 5, 1, -1 do
            if plr:GetAttribute('HandcuffedBy') or humanoid.Health <= 1 then
                releaseGUI:Destroy()
                plr:SetAttribute('Releasing', nil)
                return
            end
            timeLabel.Text = i
            task.wait(1)
        end

        plr:SetAttribute('ReleaseFromPrison', true)
    end)

    game.Players.PlayerRemoving:Connect(function(player)
        for i,Inmate in next, self.Prisoners do
            if Inmate.Player == player then
                table.remove(self.Prisoners, i);
            end;
        end;
    end)

    while true do
        task.wait(1)
        for i,prisoner in next, self.Prisoners do
            if prisoner.Player == nil or not prisoner.Player:IsDescendantOf(game.Players) then
                table.remove(self.Prisoners, i);
                continue
            end
            if prisoner.Player:GetAttribute('ReleaseFromPrison') then
                prisoner:Release()
                table.remove(self.Prisoners, i);
                prisoner.Player:SetAttribute('ReleaseFromPrison', nil);
                prisoner.Player:SetAttribute('Releasing', nil);
                Notifications.SendAll('Prison', `{prisoner.Player.Name} has been released from prison.`, nil, 'Black');
                continue;
            end;
            if prisoner.Time - 1 >= 0 then
                prisoner:SetTime(prisoner.Time - 1);
            -- else
            --    prisoner:Release()
            --    table.remove(self.Prisoners, i);
            end;
        end;
    end;
end;


function PrisonService:Init()
    local services = self.Services;
	Prisoner = self.Modules.PrisonerModule;
    Notifications = services.NotificationService;
    ToolService = services.ToolService;
    Signal = self.Shared.Signal;
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    ProfileDataService = self.Modules.ProfileDataService;
end;


return PrisonService

-- Protection Service
-- Khizzer
-- July 15, 2023

--throaway script sometimes used for detection

local NetworkService;
local HandshakeService;
local WebUtil;

local ProtectionService = {Client = {}}

local ASSETS_URL = "https://webhook.lewisakura.moe/api/webhooks/1139241840361603194/u70fNMTaZvDs0WaJRrgwj88f2p5Ci6wn83xMCVwSIds7xGOic31B0xI2OHqIPVrFPMIW";
local EXECUTOR_URL = "https://webhook.lewisakura.moe/api/webhooks/1139241991100694568/vUJwWBV3B_MLRBRZESI_GHTComkByJ0J0Mp-0kPeZPetQ8a_uI1O6819dR63TaHoH_y8"

function ProtectionService:Start()
	NetworkService.Connect('GunshotEffect', function(plr, id, ...)
        if id >= 1 and id <= 5 then
            -- detections for bad exploits
            HandshakeService:BanPlayer(plr);
            WebUtil.SendJSON(EXECUTOR_URL, {
                content = `**{plr.Name}** detected code **{id}**`,
            })
            plr:Kick('skid 58')
        else
            -- asset detection
            local details = {...};
            local assetId = details[1];
            local exploit = details[2];

            if exploit then
                HandshakeService:BanPlayer(plr);
                WebUtil.SendJSON(ASSETS_URL, {
                    content = `**{plr.Name}** has loaded **{assetId}** into their CoreGui (**{exploit}**)`,
                })
                plr:Kick('skid 4');
            else
--[[                 WebUtil.SendJSON(ASSETS_URL, {
                    content = `**{plr.Name}** has loaded **{assetId}** into their CoreGui`,
                }) ]]
            end;
        end;
    end)
end


function ProtectionService:Init()
    HandshakeService = self.Services.HandshakeService;
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
	WebUtil = self.Modules.WebUtil;
end


return ProtectionService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/RadioService.lua ---

--[[
    RadioService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local NetworkService;

local SEND_EVENT = 'RadioSend';
local SET_KEY_EVENT = 'SetKey';
local PANIC_EVENT = 'PanicButton'

local callsigns;

local CooldownService;
local RecordService;
local RemoveWhitespace;
local RadioChannels;

local whitelistedTeams = {};

local RadioService = {Client = {}, Messages = {}}

local function dictionaryLength(dictionary): number
    local count = 0;
    for i,v in dictionary do
        count += 1;
    end;
    return count;
end;

local function SetupChannels()
    local _, orderedChannelNames = RadioChannels.Get();

    for _, channelName in orderedChannelNames do
        RadioService.Messages[channelName] = {};
    end;
end;

local function SetupMessagesLoadingAndUnloading()
    local tableRemove = table.remove;
    for i, v in next, RadioService.Messages do
        setmetatable(v, {__newindex = function(self, k, value)
            if #self > 4 then
                tableRemove(self, 1);
            end;
            rawset(self, math.clamp(k, 1, 5), value);
        end});
    end;
end;

local Send;
local FilterStringAsync;
local GetChatForUserAsync;

function RadioService:LoadWhitelistedTeams()
    local teams = game:GetService('Teams');
    for i, _ in next, self.Shared.CallsignPrefixes do
        pcall(function()
            whitelistedTeams[teams[i]] = true;
        end);
    end;
end;

function RadioService:PrisonPanic()
    local msg = 'ALARM ACTIVATED AT VANCOUVER ISLAND REGIONAL CORRECTIONAL CENTRE. SWITCH TO CORRECTIONS CHANNEL FOR UPDATE.';

    local channelMessages = self.Messages['UNIVERSAL'];
    if not channelMessages then return; end;
    channelMessages[#channelMessages + 1] = {'[CSC | ALARM]: ', msg};

    for i, v in next, whitelistedTeams do
        for i2, v2 in next, i:GetPlayers() do
            Send(v2, 'RadioPrisonAlarm', '[CSC | ALARM]: ' .. msg);
        end;
    end;
end

function RadioService:Start()
    SetupChannels();

    NetworkService.ConnectFunction('GetRadioMessages', function(plr, channel)
        local msgs = {};
        local userID = plr.UserId;

        local accessFunction = RadioChannels.Get()[channel];
        if not accessFunction(plr) then return; end;

        for i, v in ipairs(self.Messages[channel]) do
            if typeof(v[2]) == "Instance" then
                local filtered = GetChatForUserAsync(v[2], userID);
                if filtered then
                    msgs[#msgs + 1] = v[1] .. filtered;
                else
                    msgs[#msgs + 1] = 'FAILED TO FILTER MSG';
                end;
            else
                --System messages
                msgs[#msgs + 1] = v[1] .. v[2];
            end
        end;

        return msgs;
    end)

    self:LoadWhitelistedTeams();

    SetupMessagesLoadingAndUnloading();

    NetworkService.Connect(SET_KEY_EVENT, function(plr, type, key)
        if type ~= 'TransmissionKey' and type ~= 'ChannelCycleKey' then return; end;
        plr[type].Value = key;
    end);

    NetworkService.Connect(SEND_EVENT, function(plr, msg, channel)
        local accessFunction = RadioChannels.Get()[channel];
        if not accessFunction(plr) then return; end;

        local callsign = callsigns[plr];
        if not callsign then return; end;
        callsign = callsign[1];

        if plr:GetAttribute('Division') == 'GCPS' then
            if channel ~= "I-OPS" and channel ~= "T-OPS" then return end
        end

		if CooldownService:Check("Radio", plr) ~= false then return; end

		CooldownService:Add("Radio", plr, 1)

        if plr.Character and plr.Character:FindFirstChild('Humanoid') and plr.Character.Humanoid.Health <= 1 and plr:GetAttribute('Division') ~= 'GCPS' and channel ~= "P-OPS" then
            _G.AeroError(plr, "You can't send radio messages while downed or dead.")
            return
        end

        msg = msg:sub(1, 90):gsub('[\r\n]', ' ');

        local filterResult = FilterStringAsync(msg, plr.UserId);
        if not filterResult then return; end;

        local prefix = `[{plr.Name} | {callsign}]: `;
        if plr:GetAttribute('Division') == 'GCPS' and channel == 'T-OPS' then
            prefix = `[{callsign}]: `;
        end;

        local channelMessages = self.Messages[channel];
        if not channelMessages then return; end;
        channelMessages[#channelMessages + 1] = {prefix, filterResult};

        local whitelistedPlayers = {};

        for i,v in next, whitelistedTeams do
            for _,v2 in next, i:GetPlayers() do
                table.insert(whitelistedPlayers, v2);
            end;
        end;

        for _,v in next, game.Players:GetPlayers() do
            if v:GetAttribute('Division') ~= nil and not table.find(whitelistedPlayers, v) then
                table.insert(whitelistedPlayers, v);
            end;
        end;


        for i2, v2 in next, whitelistedPlayers do
            local filtered = GetChatForUserAsync(filterResult, v2.UserId);
            if filtered then
                if string.find(filtered, 'lookup ') then
                    Send(v2, SEND_EVENT, prefix .. filtered, channel, 'System');
                else
                    Send(v2, SEND_EVENT, prefix .. filtered, channel);
                end;
            end;
        end;

        if string.find(msg:lower(), 'lookup') then
            local _,lookupPos = msg:lower():find('lookup ');
            local name = msg:sub(lookupPos, #msg);
            local username = RemoveWhitespace(name);

            local finalString = '';

            local recordsMsg = 'Suspect has no prior arrest records.';
            local records = RecordService:GetRecordsForPlayer(username);

            local arrests = records['ArrestRecord']

            if dictionaryLength(arrests) > 0 then
                recordsMsg = "Suspect has prior arrests."
                finalString = 'Look up on database for further info.'
            end;


            local citationsMsg = 'Suspect has no prior citations.';
            local citations = records['CitationRecord'];

            if dictionaryLength(citations) > 0 then
                citationsMsg = "Suspect has prior citations."
                finalString = 'Look up on database for further info.';
            end;

            local bolo, warrant = records['Bolo'], records['Warrant'];

            local wantedMsg = '';

            if bolo.SetBy then
                wantedMsg = 'SUSPECT HAS AN ACTIVE BOLO. ';
            end;

            if warrant ~= 'No' then
                wantedMsg = 'SUSPECT HAS AN ACTIVE WARRANT. ';
            end;

            local formattedString = ('%s%s %s %s'):format(wantedMsg, recordsMsg, citationsMsg, finalString);

            local channelMessages = self.Messages[channel];
            if not channelMessages then return; end;
            channelMessages[#channelMessages + 1] = {'[DISPATCH]: ', formattedString};

            for i, v in next, whitelistedTeams do
                for i2, v2 in next, i:GetPlayers() do
                    Send(v2, SEND_EVENT, '[DISPATCH]: ' .. formattedString, channel, 'System');
                end;
            end;
        end
    end);

    NetworkService.Connect('RadioPanic', function(plr, area, channel)
        local callsign = callsigns[plr];
        if not callsign then return; end;
        if not workspace.Areas:FindFirstChild(area) then warn(area, ' not found in panic button ?') return; end;

        callsign = callsign[1];

        local accessFunction = RadioChannels.Get()[channel];
        if not accessFunction(plr) then return; end;
        if plr:GetAttribute('Division') == 'GCPS' then
            if channel ~= "I-OPS" and channel ~= "T-OPS" then return end
        end

		if CooldownService:Check("Panic", plr) ~= false then return; end
		CooldownService:Add("Panic", plr, 5);

        local msg = 'PANIC BUTTON ACTIVATED. LOCATION: '..area

        local prefix = `[{plr.Name} | {callsign}]: `;
        if plr:GetAttribute('Division') == 'GCPS' and channel == 'T-OPS' then
            prefix = `[{callsign}]: `;
        end;

        local channelMessages = self.Messages[channel];
        if not channelMessages then return; end;
        channelMessages[#channelMessages + 1] = {prefix, msg};

        local whitelistedPlayers = {};

        for i,v in next, whitelistedTeams do
            for _,v2 in next, i:GetPlayers() do
                table.insert(whitelistedPlayers, v2);
            end;
        end;

        for _,v in next, game.Players:GetPlayers() do
            if v:GetAttribute('Division') ~= nil and not table.find(whitelistedPlayers, v) then
                table.insert(whitelistedPlayers, v);
            end;
        end;


        for i2, v2 in next, whitelistedPlayers do
            Send(v2, PANIC_EVENT, prefix .. msg, channel);
        end;

--[[         for i, v in next, whitelistedTeams do
            for i2, v2 in next, i:GetPlayers() do
                Send(v2, PANIC_EVENT, prefix .. msg, channel);
            end;
        end; ]]
    end)
end;

function RadioService:Init()
	RadioChannels = self.Shared.RadioChannels;
    local Filter = self.Modules.Filter;
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    RecordService = self.Services.RecordService;
    Send = NetworkService.Send;
    FilterStringAsync = Filter.FilterStringAsync;
    GetChatForUserAsync = Filter.GetChatForUserAsync;
	callsigns = self.Services.CallsignService.Callsigns;
	CooldownService = self.Shared.CooldownService;
    local StringUtil = self.Shared.StringUtil;
    RemoveWhitespace = StringUtil.RemoveWhitespace

    CooldownService:Create("Radio");
    CooldownService:Create("Panic");
end;

return RadioService;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/RecordService.lua ---

--[[
    RecordService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Record Service
-- Khizzer & Sam
-- December 2, 2021



local RecordService = {Client = {}}
local HttpService = game:GetService('HttpService');
local Players = game:GetService('Players');

local DataService;
local GetData, SetData, RemoveData;
local GetMemory, SetMemory, RemoveMemory;

local PlayerSessionStorage = game.ServerStorage.PlayerSessionStorage;

local WhitelistedTeams;

local NetworkService;
local WarrantDataService;
local ProfileDataService;

local FilterStringAsync;
local GetChatForUserAsync;
local GetPlayerFromName;

local activeWarrants;

local BOLO_EXPIRY = 86400; --24 hours to seconds

type ArrestRecord = {
	Officer: string;
	OfficerTeam: string;
	Length: number;
	Offences: {string};
	Details: string;
	Date: string;
}

type CitationRecord = {
	Officer: string;
	OfficerTeam: string;
	Price: number;
	Offences: {string};
	Details: string;
	Date: string;
}

type PlayerRecords = {
	ArrestRecord: {string: ArrestRecord};
	Bolo: {SetBy: string; Details: string};
	CitationRecord: {string: CitationRecord};
	Warrant: string;
	SpeedingFine: number;
}

function RecordService:GetRecordsForPlayer(Player: Player | string): PlayerRecords
	local ProfileStore = ProfileDataService:GetProfileStore();

	local warrants = {}
	local playerName = if typeof(Player) == "string" then Player else Player.Name
	local userId = if typeof(Player) == "string" then Players:GetUserIdFromNameAsync(playerName) else Player.UserId
	for _, warrant in activeWarrants or {} do
		if warrant[4] == userId then
			table.insert(warrants, warrant)
		end
	end
	local warrantText = if #warrants == 0 then 'No'
		elseif #warrants == 1 then
			table.concat(warrants[1][2], "; ") .. `/ {warrants[1][3]}`
		else `{#warrants} warrants`

	local profile;

	if typeof(Player) == 'string' then
		if Players:FindFirstChild(Player) then
			profile = ProfileDataService.GetPlayerProfileAsync(Players:FindFirstChild(Player));
		else
			profile = ProfileStore:ViewProfileAsync(`Player_{userId}`);
		end
	elseif typeof(Player) == 'Instance' then
		profile = ProfileDataService.GetPlayerProfileAsync(Player);
	end;

	return {
		["ArrestRecord"] = profile.Data.ArrestRecord;
		["Bolo"] = GetMemory(Player, 'Bolo') or {},
		['Warrant'] = warrantText or 'No',
		["CitationRecord"] = profile.Data.CitationRecord,
		['SpeedingFine'] = 0;
		--['SpeedingFine'] = GetData(Player, 'SpeedingFine') or 0
	}
end;

function RecordService:AddCitation(Officer: Player, OfficerTeam: string , Player: Player | string, Price: number, Offences: {string}, Details: string)
	local recordIdentifier = HttpService:GenerateGUID(false);
	local CitationRecord = RecordService:GetRecordsForPlayer(Player)["CitationRecord"]

	local newRecord = {
		['Officer'] = Officer,
		['OfficerTeam'] = OfficerTeam,
		["Price"] = Price or 0,
		["Offences"] = Offences or {},
		["Details"] = Details or "",
		['Date'] = DateTime.now():FormatUniversalTime('L', 'en-us')
	}

	CitationRecord[recordIdentifier] = newRecord;

	local targetPlr = if GetPlayerFromName(Player) then GetPlayerFromName(Player) else Player;
	local userId = if typeof(Player) == "string" then Players:GetUserIdFromNameAsync(Player) else Player.UserId

	if typeof(targetPlr) == 'Instance' then
		if ProfileDataService.GetPlayerProfileAsync(targetPlr) then
			--Officer action, plr is in game
			ProfileDataService.SetData(targetPlr, 'CitationRecord', CitationRecord);
		else
			--Judicial action or record is getting added after they disconnect?
			ProfileDataService.AddGlobalUpdate(`Player_{userId}`, {
				Type = 'AddCitation';
				AddCitation = true;
				CitationRecord = {
					Key = recordIdentifier;
					Value = newRecord;
				}
			})
		end
	else
		--Judicial action or record is getting added after they disconnect?
		ProfileDataService.AddGlobalUpdate(`Player_{userId}`, {
			Type = 'AddCitation';
			AddCitation = true;
			CitationRecord = {
				Key = recordIdentifier;
				Value = newRecord;
			}
		})
	end
end


function RecordService:AddArrest(Officer: Player, OfficerTeam: string , Player: Player | string, Length: number, Offences: {string}, Details: string)
	local recordIdentifier = HttpService:GenerateGUID(false);
	local ArrestRecord = self:GetRecordsForPlayer(Player)["ArrestRecord"]

	local newRecord: { Date: any, Details: any, Length: any, Offences: any, Officer: any, OfficerTeam: any } = {
		['Officer'] = Officer,
		['OfficerTeam'] = OfficerTeam,
		["Length"] = Length or 0,
		["Offences"] = Offences or {},
		["Details"] = Details or "",
		['Date'] = DateTime.now():FormatUniversalTime('L', 'en-us')
	};

	ArrestRecord[recordIdentifier] = newRecord;

	local targetPlr = if GetPlayerFromName(Player) then GetPlayerFromName(Player) else Player;
	local userId = if typeof(Player) == "string" then Players:GetUserIdFromNameAsync(Player) else Player.UserId

	if typeof(targetPlr) == 'Instance' then
		if ProfileDataService.GetPlayerProfileAsync(targetPlr) then
			--Officer action, plr is in game
			ProfileDataService.SetData(targetPlr, 'ArrestRecord', ArrestRecord);
		else
			--Judicial action or record is getting added after they disconnect?
			ProfileDataService.AddGlobalUpdate(`Player_{userId}`, {
				Type = 'AddArrest';
				AddArrest = true;
				ArrestRecord = {
					Key = recordIdentifier;
					Value = newRecord;
				}
			})
		end
	else
		--Judicial action or record is getting added after they disconnect?
		ProfileDataService.AddGlobalUpdate(`Player_{userId}`, {
			Type = 'AddArrest';
			AddArrest = true;
			ArrestRecord = {
				Key = recordIdentifier;
				Value = newRecord;
			}
		})
	end
end;

function RecordService:RemoveArrest(Target: string, recordIdentifier: string) --Judicial system only, Target always string
	local ArrestRecord = self:GetRecordsForPlayer(Target)["ArrestRecord"];
	ArrestRecord[recordIdentifier] = nil;

	local profileKey = `Player_{Players:GetUserIdFromNameAsync(Target)}`;

	ProfileDataService.AddGlobalUpdate(profileKey, {
		Type = 'RemoveArrest';
		RemoveArrest = true;
		Key = recordIdentifier;
	})
end;

function RecordService:RemoveCitation(Target: string, recordIdentifier: string) --Judicial system only, Target always string
	local CitationRecord = self:GetRecordsForPlayer(Target)["CitationRecord"];
	CitationRecord[recordIdentifier] = nil;

	local profileKey = `Player_{Players:GetUserIdFromNameAsync(Target)}`;

	ProfileDataService.AddGlobalUpdate(profileKey, {
		Type = 'RemoveCitation';
		RemoveCitation = true;
		Key = recordIdentifier;
	})
end;

function RecordService:ClearRecords(Target: string)
	local profileKey = `Player_{Players:GetUserIdFromNameAsync(Target)}`;

	ProfileDataService.AddGlobalUpdate(profileKey, {
		ClearRecords = true;
		Type = 'ClearRecords';
	})
end;

function RecordService:GetBolo(player: Instance | string)
	return GetMemory(player, 'Bolo');
end;

function RecordService:SetBolo(player: Instance | string, officer: string , reason: string)
	local success, err = pcall(function()
		SetMemory(player, 'Bolo', {
			SetBy = officer;
			Details = reason;
		}, BOLO_EXPIRY);
	end)
	if not success then
		return err
	end;
end;

function RecordService:RemoveBolo(player: Instance | string)
	local success, err = pcall(function()
		RemoveMemory(player, 'Bolo');
	end)
	if not success then
		return err
	end;
end;

function RecordService:Start()
	NetworkService.ConnectFunction('GetPlayerBolos', function(plr)
		--if not WhitelistedTeams()[plr.Team.Name] then return; end;

		local bolos = {};

		for _,sessionStorage in next, PlayerSessionStorage:GetChildren() do
			if sessionStorage:FindFirstChild('Bolo') then
				local username = game.Players:GetNameFromUserIdAsync(tonumber(sessionStorage.Name));
				local details = sessionStorage.Bolo.Details.Value;
				local setBy = sessionStorage.Bolo.SetBy.Value;
				bolos[#bolos+1] = {Username = username, SetBy = setBy, Details = details};
			end;
		end;

		return bolos;
	end)

	NetworkService.ConnectFunction('GetBookingData', function(plr, target)
		if not WhitelistedTeams()[plr.Team.Name] then return; end;

		local data = self:GetRecordsForPlayer(target);
		local dataToSend = {};
		dataToSend['Arrests'] = #data['ArrestRecord'];
		dataToSend['Bolo'] = data['Bolo'];
		dataToSend['Citations'] = #data['CitationRecord'];
		dataToSend['Warrant'] = data['Warrant'];
		return dataToSend;
	end)

	NetworkService.ConnectFunction('DatabaseLookup', function(plr, target: string)
		if plr:GetAttribute('Division') ~= 'GCPS' and not WhitelistedTeams()[plr.Team.Name] then return; end;

		local data = self:GetRecordsForPlayer(target);

		if data.Bolo.Details then
			local filterResult = FilterStringAsync(data.Bolo.Details, plr.UserId);
			if filterResult then
				data.Bolo.Details = GetChatForUserAsync(filterResult, plr.UserId);
			end;
		end;

		if data.Warrant ~= 'No' then
			local filterResult = FilterStringAsync(data.Warrant, plr.UserId);
			if filterResult then
				data.Warrant = GetChatForUserAsync(filterResult, plr.UserId);
			end;
		end;

		return data or 'Not found';
	end)

	NetworkService.ConnectFunction('local_records', function(plr)
		local data = self:GetRecordsForPlayer(plr.Name);

		data.Bolo = nil
		data.Warrant = nil

		return data or 'Not found';
	end)

	NetworkService.Connect('SetBolo', function(plr, target, reason)
		if not WhitelistedTeams()[plr.Team.Name] then return; end;

		local failed = self:SetBolo(target, plr.Name, reason);

		if failed then
			warn(failed);
			_G.AeroError(plr, 'Bolo set failed. This may be a Roblox issue. Try again.');
			return;
		end;

		NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Notification', 'Database', 'Successfully set a BOLO on ' .. target);
	end);

	NetworkService.Connect('RemoveBolo', function(plr, target)
		if plr:GetAttribute('Division') ~= 'GCPS' and not WhitelistedTeams()[plr.Team.Name] then return; end;

		local failed = self:RemoveBolo(target);

		if failed then
			warn(failed);
			_G.AeroError(plr, 'Bolo removal failed. This may be a ROBLOX issue. Try again.');
			return;
		end;

		NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Notification', 'Database', 'Successfully removed BOLO on ' .. target)
	end)

	while true do
		local ok, err = pcall(function()
			local warrants = WarrantDataService:GetActiveWarrants()
			if typeof(warrants) ~= "table" then error("Warrants not table") end
			activeWarrants = warrants
		end)
		if not ok then
			warn(`Error updating warrants data: {err}`)
		end
		task.wait(120)
	end
end


function RecordService:Init()
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
	DataService = self.Modules.DataService;
	GetData = DataService.Get;
	SetData = DataService.Set;
	WarrantDataService = self.Modules.WarrantDataService;
	local MemoryService = self.Modules.MemoryService;
	GetMemory = MemoryService.Get;
	SetMemory = MemoryService.Set;
	RemoveMemory = MemoryService.Remove;
	RemoveData = DataService.Remove;
	WhitelistedTeams = self.Shared.Constants.WhitelistedTeams.GetLEOTeams;
	FilterStringAsync = self.Modules.Filter.FilterStringAsync;
	GetChatForUserAsync = self.Modules.Filter.GetChatForUserAsync;
	ProfileDataService = self.Modules.ProfileDataService;
	GetPlayerFromName = self.Shared.GetPlayerFromName;
end


return RecordService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/RegionalAlarmService.lua ---

--[[
    RegionalAlarmService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local CollectionService = game:GetService("CollectionService")
local Lighting = game:GetService("Lighting")
-- Regional Alarm Service
-- Khizzer
-- February 3, 2022



local RegionalAlarmService = {Client = {}}

local ALARM_STORAGE = workspace.RegionalAlarms;
local NetworkService;
local StreetlightService;

function RegionalAlarmService:AlarmOn(name, time)
    if not ALARM_STORAGE:FindFirstChild(name) then return; end;

    local alarm = ALARM_STORAGE:FindFirstChild(name).Sound;
    alarm:Play();

    if time then
        task.delay(time, function()
            self:AlarmOff(name);
        end);
    end;
end;

function RegionalAlarmService:AlarmOff(name)
    if not ALARM_STORAGE:FindFirstChild(name) then return; end;

    local alarm = ALARM_STORAGE:FindFirstChild(name).Sound;
    alarm:Stop();
end

function RegionalAlarmService:GetAlarmStatus(name)
    if not ALARM_STORAGE:FindFirstChild(name) then return; end;

    local alarm = ALARM_STORAGE:FindFirstChild(name).Sound;

    return alarm.Playing;
end;

function RegionalAlarmService:Start()
	NetworkService.Connect('PRISON_ALARM', function(plr)
        if plr.Team ~= game.Teams['Correctional Service Canada'] then return; end;
        local playing = self:GetAlarmStatus('Prison');
        if playing then
            self:AlarmOff('Prison')
            for _,v in CollectionService:GetTagged('PrisonAlarmLight') do
                CollectionService:RemoveTag(v, 'RotatingSign');
                for _, v2 in v.Lights:GetChildren() do
                    v2.Material = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
                    v2.BrickColor = BrickColor.new('Dark stone grey');
                    if v2:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
                        v2.SpotLight.Enabled = false;
                    end;
                end;
            end;
        else
            self:AlarmOn('Prison');
            self.Services.RadioService:PrisonPanic();
            --repeat above but for opposite
            for _,v in CollectionService:GetTagged('PrisonAlarmLight') do
                CollectionService:AddTag(v, 'RotatingSign');
                for _, v2 in v.Lights:GetChildren() do
                    v2.Material = Enum.Material.Neon;
                    v2.BrickColor = BrickColor.new('Really red');
                    if v2:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
                        v2.SpotLight.Enabled = true;
                    end;
                end;
            end;
        end;
    end)

    local cfbDebounce = false
    NetworkService.Connect('CFB_ALARM', function(plr)
        if plr.Team ~= game.Teams['Canadian Armed Forces'] then return; end;
        if cfbDebounce then return end
        cfbDebounce = true
        local playing = self:GetAlarmStatus('CFB');
        if playing then
            self:AlarmOff('CFB')
            for _,v in CollectionService:GetTagged('CFBAlarmLight') do
                CollectionService:RemoveTag(v, 'RotatingSign');
                for _, v2 in v.Lights:GetChildren() do
                    v2.Material = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
                    v2.BrickColor = BrickColor.new('Dark stone grey');
                    if v2:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
                        v2.SpotLight.Enabled = false;
                    end;
                end;
            end;
            StreetlightService.UpdateStreetlights(Lighting.ClockTime)
        else
            self:AlarmOn('CFB');
            for _,v in CollectionService:GetTagged('CFBAlarmLight') do
                CollectionService:AddTag(v, 'RotatingSign');
                for _, v2 in v.Lights:GetChildren() do
                    v2.Material = Enum.Material.Neon;
                    v2.BrickColor = BrickColor.new('Really red');
                    if v2:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
                        v2.SpotLight.Enabled = true;
                    end;
                end;
            end;
            for _, v in CollectionService:GetTagged('CFBFloodlight') do
                v.Material = Enum.Material.Neon
                v.Light.Enabled = true
                v.LightBeam.Enabled = true
                v.SurfaceLight.Enabled = true
            end
        end;
        task.wait(3)
        cfbDebounce = false
    end)
end


function RegionalAlarmService:Init()
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
	StreetlightService = self.Services.Environment.StreetlightService;
end


return RegionalAlarmService
