--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/ResetService.lua ---

--[[
    ResetService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local ResetService = {Client = {}};

local RESET_EVENT = 'Reset';

local wait;
local tostring = tostring;
local newInstance = Instance.new;
local thumbnailType = Enum.ThumbnailType.HeadShot;
local thumbnailSize = Enum.ThumbnailSize.Size420x420;

local CombatService;
local RecordService;
local PlayerService;

local MEDICAL_TEAMS = {
    ['Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service'] = true,
    ['British Columbia Ambulance Service'] = true,
    ['Vancouver Coastal Health'] = true,
};
local MEDICAL_DIVISIONS = {
    ['12VFA'] = true,
};

local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService')
local Players = game:GetService("Players")

local WhitelistedTeams = require(ReplicatedStorage.Aero.Shared.Constants.WhitelistedTeams)
local respawningGUIPrefab = game:GetService('ServerStorage'):WaitForChild('Character'):WaitForChild('RespawningGUI');

function ResetService:Start()
    local NetworkService = self.NetworkService;

	self.Services.NetworkService.Connect(RESET_EVENT, function(plr)
        if plr:GetAttribute('HandcuffedBy') then return; end;

        local char = plr.Character;
        if not char then return; end;

        local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass('Humanoid');
        if not humanoid then return; end;

        local head = char:FindFirstChild('Head');
		if not head then return; end;

        if plr:FindFirstChild('respawningValue') then return; end;

		if humanoid.Sit then
			humanoid.Jump = true;
			wait(0.1);
		end;

        local respawning = newInstance('BoolValue');
        respawning.Name = 'respawningValue';
        respawning.Parent = plr;

        humanoid.WalkSpeed = 0;
        humanoid.JumpPower = 0;

        local respawningGUI = respawningGUIPrefab:Clone();
        local timeLabel = respawningGUI.RespawningLabel.TimeLabel;
        respawningGUI.Parent = head;
        respawningGUI.Adornee = head;
        for i = 5, 1, -1 do
            if plr:GetAttribute('HandcuffedBy') then
                respawningGUI:Destroy();
                respawning:Destroy();
                return;
            end;
            timeLabel.Text = tostring(i);
            wait(1);
        end;
        wait(0.1);
        if (plr :: Player):IsDescendantOf(Players) then
            plr:LoadCharacter();

            if plr.Team.Name == "Civilian" or plr.Team.Name == "Prisoner" then
                local suc, plrImage = pcall(Players.GetUserThumbnailAsync, Players, plr.UserId, thumbnailType, thumbnailSize);
                if not suc then plrImage = nil; end;
                if not humanoid:GetAttribute('SurpressNotifications') then
                    NetworkService.SendAll('Notification', 'Player Reset', plr.Name, plrImage, 'Black');
                end
                _G.Aero.Services.LogsService:AddLog('Kills', `{plr.Name} reset`);
            end
        end
        respawning:Destroy();
    end);

    NetworkService.Connect('RAGDOLL_RESPAWN', function(plr)
        if plr.Character.Humanoid.Health > 1 then return; end;

        NetworkService.Send(plr, "SetDownedGUI", false);
        plr:LoadCharacter();
        plr:SetAttribute('Ragdoll', nil);
        NetworkService.Send(plr ,'SetInventoryEnabled', true);
        CombatService:ResetCombat(plr);
        for _,v in plr:GetChildren() do
            if v:IsA('Tool') then
                v:Destroy();
            end;
        end;
        -- for _, v in PlayerService:GetPlayerSessionStorage(plr).DeathToolStorage do
        --     if v:IsA('Tool') then
        --         v:Destroy()
        --     end
        -- end

        local killerName = plr:GetAttribute('Killer');
        local killer = killerName and Players:FindFirstChild(killerName)
        local et = killer and WhitelistedTeams.GetEmergencyTeams()
        -- Death by emergency services or other organisation (i.e. NSEC)
        if (et and et[killer.Team.Name] == true) or (killer and killer:GetAttribute("Division") ~= nil and killer:GetAttribute('Division') ~= 'GCPS') then
            RecordService:RemoveBolo(plr);
            plr:SetAttribute("LifeStart", os.time())
        end
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('RAGDOLL_REVIVE', function(plr, target)
        if not (MEDICAL_TEAMS[plr.Team.Name] or MEDICAL_DIVISIONS[plr:GetAttribute('Division') or 'h']) then return; end;
        if plr == target then return; end;

        target:SetAttribute('Ragdoll', nil);
        target.Character.Humanoid.Health = 2;
        target.Character:SetAttribute('Revived', true);
        target.Character:SetAttribute('ReviveAt', os.time());
        target.Character:SetAttribute("DroppedMoney", nil);
        NetworkService.Send(target, 'DISABLE_RAGDOLL');
        NetworkService.Send(target, "SetDownedGUI", false);
        NetworkService.Send(target ,'SetInventoryEnabled', true);
        target:SetAttribute('Killer', nil);

        CollectionService:RemoveTag(target.Character.Head, 'Revive');
    end)
end;

function ResetService:Init()
    wait = self.Shared.Wait;
    CombatService = self.Services.CombatService;
    RecordService = self.Services.RecordService;
    PlayerService = self.Services.PlayerService;
end;

return ResetService;

-- Robbery Service
-- Khizzer
-- January 13, 2023



local RobberyService = {Client = {}}

local NetworkService;

--Concatenates a string to a string attribute
local function ConcatenateStringAttribute(instance: Instance, attributeName: string, appendedValue: string)
    if not instance:GetAttribute(attributeName) then
        instance:SetAttribute(attributeName, '!');
    end;
    instance:SetAttribute(attributeName, instance:GetAttribute(attributeName)..appendedValue);
end;

function RobberyService:Start()
    if game.PrivateServerId ~= "" and game.PrivateServerOwnerId ~= 0 and game.PrivateServerOwnerId ~= 71812450 then return end;

    NetworkService.Connect('FILL_DUFFEL_BAG_2', function(plr: Player, interactionPart: BasePart)
        if not typeof(interactionPart) == 'Instance' then return end;


    end)

	for _,v in next, script:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA("ModuleScript") then
            local wrappedModule = self:WrapModule(require(v));
        end;
    end;
end;


function RobberyService:Init()
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
end


return RobberyService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/RobberyServiceOld.lua ---

--[[
    RobberyServiceOld (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Robbery Service
-- Khizzer
-- July 23, 2021

local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService');
local HttpService = game:GetService('HttpService');

local RobberyService = {Client = {}}

local NetworkService;
local Date;
local NotificationService;
local RegionalAlarmService;

local Constants;
local START_BANK_ROBBERY_EVENT;
local DISPLAY_BANK_ROBBERY_EVENT;
local CLAIM_ROBBERY_MONEY_EVENT;
local STORE_ROBBERY_EVENT;

local DispatchService
local PartToRegion3;
local TableUtil;
local MoneyService;
local WebUtil;

local BANK_LOCATION = workspace.VaultDoor.interactionPart;

local Door;

local Robbery;
local WhitelistedTeams;

local robberyTools = game:GetService('ServerStorage').robberyTools;

local vaultInterior = workspace.BankRobbery;

local findPartsInRegion3WithWhitelist = workspace.FindPartsInRegion3WithWhiteList;
local insideRegion = vaultInterior.Region;

local MAXIMUM_BANK_ROBBERY_AMOUNT = 6250;

local function AddNumberAttribute(instance: Instance, name: string, limit: number, increment: number)
	local currentNumber = instance:GetAttribute(name);
	if not currentNumber then
		instance:SetAttribute(name, increment);
	else
        if currentNumber + increment > limit then instance:SetAttribute(name, limit); return 'LimitReached' end;
		if currentNumber <= (limit - 1) then
			instance:SetAttribute(name, currentNumber + increment);
		else
			return 'LimitReached'
		end;
	end;
end;

local function ConcatenateStringAttribute(instance: Instance, name: string, newString: string)
    if not instance:GetAttribute(name) then
        instance:SetAttribute(name, '!');
    end;
    instance:SetAttribute(name, instance:GetAttribute(name)..newString);
end;

function RobberyService:Start()
    local vaultDoor = Door.new(workspace.VaultDoor.Main);

	NetworkService.Connect('BankRobbery', function(plr, result)
        if ((BANK_LOCATION.Position - plr.Character.Torso.Position).Magnitude) > 10 then return; end;

        local lastRobbed = BANK_LOCATION:GetAttribute('LastRobbed');

        local timeNow = Date.new();
        local timeInSeconds = timeNow:ToSeconds();

        if timeInSeconds - lastRobbed < 300 then return; end;
        if not BANK_LOCATION:GetAttribute('BeingRobbed') then return; end;

        if result == 'Success' then
            BANK_LOCATION:SetAttribute('BeingRobbed', false);
            BANK_LOCATION:SetAttribute('LastRobbed', timeInSeconds);

            CollectionService:AddTag(vaultInterior.DuffelBag, 'DuffelBag');

            task.spawn(function()
                vaultDoor:Open(3);
                DispatchService:CreateCall('DISPATCH - POLICE', 'Royal Bank of Canada', string.format('%s has just started a robbery at the Vancouver branch of The Royal Bank of Canada', plr.Name))
            end)

            local moneyParts = vaultInterior.Money:GetChildren();

            local function EnableMoneyPart(part)
                CollectionService:AddTag(part, 'GrabMoney');
                part:SetAttribute('StoredMoney', math.random(1000, 2000));
            end;

            TableUtil.Shuffle(moneyParts);

            EnableMoneyPart(moneyParts[1]);
            EnableMoneyPart(moneyParts[2]);
            EnableMoneyPart(moneyParts[3]);

            task.spawn(function()
				task.wait(15)
				vaultDoor:Close();
                local region = PartToRegion3(insideRegion)
                local chars = {};

                for _,player in next, game.Players:GetPlayers() do
                    table.insert(chars ,player.Character);
                end;

                for _,v in next, findPartsInRegion3WithWhitelist(workspace, region, chars, 300) do
                    if v.Parent:IsA('Model') then
                        v.Parent:MoveTo(Vector3.new(1138.468, -0.468, -1326.179) + Vector3.new(math.random(-3,3), 0, math.random(-3,3)));
                    end;
                end;

                for _,v in next, vaultInterior.Money:GetChildren() do
                    CollectionService:RemoveTag(v, 'GrabMoney');
                    v:SetAttribute('Claimed', nil);
                    v:SetAttribute('StoredMoney', 0);
                end;

                CollectionService:RemoveTag(vaultInterior.DuffelBag, 'DuffelBag');

                task.delay(2, function()
                    RegionalAlarmService:AlarmOn('Bank', 50);
                end)
			end);

		elseif result == 'Failure' then
			DispatchService:CreateCall('DISPATCH - POLICE', 'Royal Bank of Canada', string.format('%s attempted and failed a robbery at the Vancouver branch of The Royal Bank of Canada', plr.Name))
            BANK_LOCATION:SetAttribute('BeingRobbed', false);
            BANK_LOCATION:SetAttribute('LastRobbed', timeInSeconds);
            RegionalAlarmService:AlarmOn('Bank', 50);
            return;
        else
            plr:Kick('clown');
        end;
    end);

    NetworkService.Connect(START_BANK_ROBBERY_EVENT, function(plr)
        if (BANK_LOCATION.Position - plr.Character.Torso.Position).Magnitude > 10 then return; end;

        if game.PrivateServerId ~= "" and game.PrivateServerOwnerId ~= 0 and game.PrivateServerOwnerId ~= 71812450 then _G.AeroError(plr, 'Robbing is disabled in private servers.') return end;
        -- if WhitelistedTeams.CountLEOs() < 1 then
        --     _G.AeroError(plr, "A cop must be in game in order to rob")
        --     return
        -- end

        local lastRobbed = BANK_LOCATION:GetAttribute('LastRobbed');

        if tick() - lastRobbed < 300 then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'This bank was robbed too recently. Wait '..math.ceil(300 - (tick() - lastRobbed))..' seconds.');
            return;
        end;

        BANK_LOCATION:SetAttribute('BeingRobbed', true);
        NetworkService.Send(plr, DISPLAY_BANK_ROBBERY_EVENT);
        NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Notification', 'Heads up', 'You have to complete the puzzle within 60 seconds or the robbery will fail.', nil, 'Blue');

        task.delay(60, function()
            if BANK_LOCATION:GetAttribute('BeingRobbed') == false then return end

            BANK_LOCATION:SetAttribute('BeingRobbed', false);
            BANK_LOCATION:SetAttribute('LastRobbed', tick());
            if plr and plr.Parent == game.Players then
                _G.AeroError(plr, "You took too long to complete the puzzle.")
                DispatchService:CreateCall('DISPATCH - POLICE', 'Royal Bank of Canada', string.format('%s attempted and failed a robbery at the Vancouver branch of The Royal Bank of Canada', plr.Name))
            end
            RegionalAlarmService:AlarmOn('Bank', 50);
        end)
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('GET_DUFFEL_BAG', function(plr, interactionPart)
        plr:SetAttribute('LastRobbed', tick());
        if game.PrivateServerId ~= "" and game.PrivateServerOwnerId ~= 0  and game.PrivateServerOwnerId ~= 71812450 then _G.AeroError(plr, 'Robbing is disabled in private servers.') return end;

        local interactionPart = vaultInterior.DuffelBag;

        if not CollectionService:HasTag(interactionPart, 'DuffelBag') then return; end;

        local rootPart = plr.Character:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart');
        if not rootPart then return; end;

        if (rootPart.Position - interactionPart.Position).Magnitude > 7 then return; end;

        local backpack = plr.Backpack;
        local character = plr.Character;

        if backpack:FindFirstChild('Duffel Bag') then return; end;
        if character:FindFirstChild('Duffel Bag') then return; end;

        local clone = robberyTools['Duffel Bag']:Clone();
        clone:SetAttribute('ToolSource', `{plr.Name} (Bank) ({DateTime.now():FormatUniversalTime('L', 'en-us')})`)
        clone.Parent = plr.Backpack;
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('FILL_DUFFEL_BAG', function(plr, interactionPart)
        if game.PrivateServerId ~= "" and game.PrivateServerOwnerId ~= 0  and game.PrivateServerOwnerId ~= 71812450 then _G.AeroError(plr, 'Robbing is disabled in private servers.') return end;

        if not plr.Character:FindFirstChild('Duffel Bag') then return; end;
        if not CollectionService:HasTag(interactionPart, 'GrabMoney') then return; end;

        local claimed = interactionPart:GetAttribute('Claimed');
        if claimed then
            if string.find(claimed, plr.Name) then return; end;
        end;

        local rootPart = plr.Character:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart');
        if not rootPart then return; end;

        local duffelBag = plr.Character:FindFirstChild('Duffel Bag');
        if not duffelBag then return; end;

        if (rootPart.Position - interactionPart.Position).Magnitude > 7 then return; end;

        ConcatenateStringAttribute(interactionPart, 'Claimed', plr.Name);

        local result = AddNumberAttribute(duffelBag, 'Money' , MAXIMUM_BANK_ROBBERY_AMOUNT, interactionPart:GetAttribute('StoredMoney'));

        if result == 'LimitReached' then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Notification', 'Limit reached', 'Your duffel bag has been filled to its limit!', nil, 'Red')
        end;
    end)



    NetworkService.Connect(CLAIM_ROBBERY_MONEY_EVENT, function(plr, interactionPart)
        if game.PrivateServerId ~= "" and game.PrivateServerOwnerId ~= 0  and game.PrivateServerOwnerId ~= 71812450 then _G.AeroError(plr, 'Robbing is disabled in private servers.') return end;

        if (plr.Character.Torso.Position - interactionPart.Position).Magnitude > 8 then return; end;

        if not interactionPart:FindFirstAncestor('BankRobberyClaimSpots') then return; end;

        local backpack = plr:WaitForChild('Backpack');
        local robberyBag = backpack:FindFirstChild('Duffel Bag') or plr.Character:FindFirstChild('Duffel Bag');

        if not robberyBag then return; end;
        local moneyAmount = robberyBag:GetAttribute('Money');
        robberyBag:Destroy();

        if tick() - plr:GetAttribute('LastRobbed') < 5 then
            MoneyService:SubtractMoney(plr, moneyAmount);
            return;
        end;

        MoneyService:AddMoney(plr, moneyAmount);
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect(STORE_ROBBERY_EVENT, function(plr, interactionPart)
        if game.PrivateServerId ~= "" and game.PrivateServerOwnerId ~= 0  and game.PrivateServerOwnerId ~= 71812450 then _G.AeroError(plr, 'Robbing is disabled in private servers.') return end;

        if not interactionPart then return; end;
        if (interactionPart.Position - plr.Character.Torso.Position).Magnitude > 10 then return; end;
        local location = interactionPart:GetAttribute('Location');
        if not location then return; end;

        local robbery = Robbery.new(plr, function()
        NetworkService.Send(plr, 'FinishedStoreRobbery')
        NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Robbery', 'Successful robbery');
        end, function()
        NetworkService.Send(plr, 'FailedStoreRobbery')
        NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Robbery', 'Failed robbery');
        end, location)
        while true do
            wait(2)
            if robbery.Money < 625 then
                robbery:AddMoney(20)
            else
                break;
            end;
        end
        robbery:Finish();
    end)
end;


function RobberyService:Init()
	DispatchService = self.Services.DispatchService;
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    NotificationService = self.Services.NotificationService;
    FastRemoveFirstValue = self.Shared.TableUtil.FastRemoveFirstValue;
    Door = self:WrapModule(require(script.Parent.Environment.DoorService:WaitForChild('Door')));
    Date = self.Shared.Date;
    Constants = self.Shared.Constants.Robbery;
    START_BANK_ROBBERY_EVENT = Constants['START_BANK_ROBBERY_EVENT']
    DISPLAY_BANK_ROBBERY_EVENT = Constants['DISPLAY_BANK_ROBBERY_EVENT']
    CLAIM_ROBBERY_MONEY_EVENT = Constants['CLAIM_ROBBERY_MONEY_EVENT'];
    STORE_ROBBERY_EVENT = Constants['STORE_ROBBERY_EVENT'];
    Robbery = self.Modules.Robbery;
    PartToRegion3 = self.Shared.PartToRegion3;
    TableUtil = self.Shared.TableUtil;
    RegionalAlarmService = self.Services.RegionalAlarmService;
    MoneyService = self.Services.MoneyService;
    WebUtil = self.Modules.WebUtil;
    WhitelistedTeams = self.Shared.Constants.WhitelistedTeams;
end


return RobberyService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/RobberyService_contents/GasStation.lua ---

--[[
    GasStation (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → RobberyService
    Parent: RobberyService
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Gas Station
-- Khizzer
-- June 12, 2023

local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService');

local NetworkService;
local DispatchService;
local WhitelistedTeams;

local GasStation = {}

-- local CIVILIAN_TEAM = game.Teams.Civilian;

local COOLDOWN = 300;

local MIN_AMOUNT = 3750;
local MAX_AMOUNT = 7500;

local DUFFEL_BAG;
function GasStation:ConnectEvents()
    NetworkService.Connect('GasRobberyStarted', function(plr: Player, interactionPart: Part & {GlitchDetect: Part?})
        plr:SetAttribute('LastRobbed', tick());

        -- if plr.Team ~= CIVILIAN_TEAM then return end;

        if typeof(interactionPart) ~= 'Instance' then return end;
        if not interactionPart:IsA('Part') then return end;
        if not CollectionService:HasTag(interactionPart, 'GasStationRobbery') then return; end;

        if plr:DistanceFromCharacter(interactionPart.Position) > 10 then return end;
        -- if WhitelistedTeams.CountLEOs() < 1 then
        --     _G.AeroError(plr, "A cop must be in game in order to rob")
        --     return
        -- end

        if interactionPart:FindFirstChild("GlitchDetect") then
            for _, part in workspace:GetPartsInPart(interactionPart.GlitchDetect) do
                if part:IsDescendantOf(plr.Character) then
                    _G.AeroError(plr, "You must be inside of the gas station to rob it")
                    return
                end
            end
        end

        local currentTimestamp = DateTime.now().UnixTimestamp;
        if currentTimestamp - (interactionPart:GetAttribute('LastRobbed') or 0) < COOLDOWN then
            _G.AeroError(plr, `This gas station was robbed too recently. Wait {math.ceil(COOLDOWN - (currentTimestamp - (interactionPart:GetAttribute('LastRobbed') or 0)))} seconds.`);
            return;
        end;

        interactionPart:SetAttribute('LastRobbed', currentTimestamp);
        interactionPart:SetAttribute('CurrentRobber', plr.Name);
        NetworkService.Send(plr, 'GasStationRobbery', interactionPart);

        local location = interactionPart:GetAttribute('Location');
        DispatchService:CreateCall('DISPATCH - POLICE', location, `Gas station robbery in progress at {location} by {plr.Name}`)
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('GasRobberySuccess', function(plr: Player, interactionPart: Part)
        -- if plr.Team ~= CIVILIAN_TEAM then return end;
        if typeof(interactionPart) ~= 'Instance' then return end;
        if not interactionPart:IsA('Part') then return end;
        if not CollectionService:HasTag(interactionPart, 'GasStationRobbery') then return; end;
        if interactionPart:GetAttribute('CurrentRobber') ~= plr.Name then return end;

        if plr:DistanceFromCharacter(interactionPart.Position) > 10 then return end;

        local duffelBag = DUFFEL_BAG:Clone();
        duffelBag:SetAttribute('ToolSource', `{plr.Name} (Gas Station) ({DateTime.now():FormatUniversalTime('L', 'en-us')})`)
        if plr.UserId == 155746202 or plr.UserId == 1201532 or plr.UserId == 2655738155 or plr.UserId == 423786704 then
            duffelBag:SetAttribute('Money', math.random(MIN_AMOUNT, MIN_AMOUNT+250))
        else
            duffelBag:SetAttribute('Money', math.random(MIN_AMOUNT, MAX_AMOUNT))
        end
        duffelBag.Parent = plr.Backpack;

        interactionPart:SetAttribute('CurrentRobber', nil);
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('GasRobberyFail', function(plr: Player, interactionPart: Part)
        -- if plr.Team ~= CIVILIAN_TEAM then return end;

        if typeof(interactionPart) ~= 'Instance' then return end;
        if not interactionPart:IsA('Part') then return end;
        if not CollectionService:HasTag(interactionPart, 'GasStationRobbery') then return; end;
        if interactionPart:GetAttribute('CurrentRobber') ~= plr.Name then return end;

        if plr:DistanceFromCharacter(interactionPart.Position) > 10 then return end;

        interactionPart:SetAttribute('CurrentRobber', nil);
    end)
end;

function GasStation:Start()
    self:ConnectEvents();
end;

function GasStation:Init()
    DispatchService = self.Services.DispatchService;
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    WhitelistedTeams = self.Shared.Constants.WhitelistedTeams;
    DUFFEL_BAG = self.ServerAssets['Duffel Bag'];
end;


return GasStation

-- Robux Transaction Service
-- Khizzer
-- January 15, 2022

local MarketplaceService = game:GetService('MarketplaceService');

local NetworkService;
local Gamepasses;

local RobuxTransactionService = {Client = {}}

local GAMEPASSES = {
    [27439586] = 'OwnsRadio',
    [60041107] = 'OwnsBillboard',
    [63874450] = 'X2Income',
    [63874646] = 'X2Stamina',
    [27639201] = 'ProtestSign',
    [27639235] = 'TirePump',
    [27639249] = 'PAL'
}

function RobuxTransactionService:Start()
	MarketplaceService.PromptGamePassPurchaseFinished:Connect(function(plr, gamepassId, purchased)
        if purchased then
            plr:SetAttribute(GAMEPASSES[gamepassId], true);
        end;
    end);

    NetworkService.Connect('GamepassGift', function(plr, userId, gamepassKey)
        local gamepassTable = Gamepasses.RegularGamepasses[gamepassKey] or Gamepasses.GearGamepasses[gamepassKey];

        if not gamepassTable then return end;

        plr:SetAttribute('GiftedGamepassRecipient', userId);
        MarketplaceService:PromptProductPurchase(plr, gamepassTable.Product);
    end)
end;


function RobuxTransactionService:Init()
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    Gamepasses = self.Shared.Constants.Gamepasses;
end


return RobuxTransactionService

--[[
    ServerLocationService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")

-- Server Location Service
-- Khizzer
-- October 27, 2023


local LOCATION_ENDPOINT = 'http://ip-api.com/json/?fields=continentCode,countryCode,city';

local ServerLocationService = {Client = {}}

type locationResult = {
    city: string;
    continentCode: string;
    countryCode: string;
}

local function GetLocation(): string
    local succ, res: locationResult = pcall(function()
        return HttpService:JSONDecode(HttpService:GetAsync(LOCATION_ENDPOINT));
    end)

    if not succ then
        warn(res);
        task.wait(5);
        return GetLocation();
    end;

    workspace:SetAttribute('LocationCode', `{res.continentCode}-{res.countryCode}`);
    workspace:SetAttribute('LocationCity', res.city);
end;


function ServerLocationService:Start()
    GetLocation();
end


function ServerLocationService:Init()

end


return ServerLocationService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/SnowPlowService.lua ---

--[[
    SnowPlowService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Snow Plow Service
-- Khizzer
-- November 20, 2022



local SnowPlowService = {Client = {}}

local NetworkService;

local TRANSLINK_TEAM = game:GetService('Teams').Translink;
local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService')

local directions = {
    Up = 'Vertical';
    Down = 'Vertical';
    Left = 'Horizontal';
    Centre = 'Horizontal';
    Right = 'Horizontal';
};

function SnowPlowService:Start()
	NetworkService.Connect('SetSnowPlow', function(player, direction)
        if not player.Team == TRANSLINK_TEAM then return; end;
        local car = player.Car.Value;
        if not car then return; end;
        local snowPlowState = car.Config.State:FindFirstChild('SnowPlow');
        if not snowPlowState then return; end;
        local directionType = directions[direction];
        if not directionType then return; end;

        if snowPlowState:GetAttribute(directionType) == direction then return; end;

        snowPlowState:SetAttribute(directionType, direction);

        local weldToMove = directionType == 'Vertical' and car.Body.SnowPlow.Stick.Vertical.Ball.PivotConnection or car.Body.SnowPlow.Stick.Horizontal.Joint.ConnectingJoint;

        TweenService:Create(weldToMove, TweenInfo.new(1, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear), {C0 = weldToMove:GetAttribute(direction)}):Play();

        if direction == 'Up' then
            car.Body.SnowPlow.Plow.Detection.PlowServer.Enabled = false;
        elseif direction == 'Down' then
            car.Body.SnowPlow.Plow.Detection.PlowServer.Enabled = true;
        end;
        --weldToMove.C0 *= weldToMove:GetAttribute(direction);
    end);
end


function SnowPlowService:Init()
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
end


return SnowPlowService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/SpeedCameraService.lua ---

--[[
    SpeedCameraService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Speed Camera Service
-- Khizzer
-- November 14, 2021



local SpeedCameraService = {}
local NetworkService;
local DataService;

local CastWithWhitelist;
local ConvertSpeed;
local mathFloor = math.floor;

local MoneyService;


local RAY_DIRECTION = Vector3.new(0, -20, 0)

function IssueFine(plr, speedLimit, recordedSpeed)
	if
		plr.Team.Name == "Canadian Armed Forces"
		or _G.Aero.Shared.INSETest(plr)
		or plr:GetAttribute("Division") == "GCPS"
	then
		return
	end

	local difference = recordedSpeed - speedLimit;
	if difference <= 3 then
		return;
	elseif difference >= 10 and difference <= 20 then
		NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Notification', 'Speeding', "You've been issued a fine for speeding! Pay it off at VPD or BCSS.", nil, 'Red');
		local existingFine = DataService.Get(plr, 'SpeedingFine');
		if not existingFine then
			DataService.Set(plr, 'SpeedingFine', 100);
			plr:SetAttribute('SpeedingFine', 100);
		else
			DataService.Set(plr, 'SpeedingFine', existingFine + 100);
			plr:SetAttribute('SpeedingFine', existingFine + 100);
		end;
	elseif difference >= 20 then
		NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Notification', 'Speeding', "You've been issued a fine for speeding! Pay it off at VPD or BCSS.", nil, 'Red');
		local existingFine = DataService.Get(plr, 'SpeedingFine');
		if not existingFine then
			DataService.Set(plr, 'SpeedingFine', 250);
			plr:SetAttribute('SpeedingFine', 250);
		else
			DataService.Set(plr, 'SpeedingFine', existingFine + 250);
			plr:SetAttribute('SpeedingFine', existingFine + 250);
		end;
	end;
end;

function SpeedCameraService:Start()
	NetworkService.Connect('PayFine', function(plr)
		if not plr:GetAttribute('SpeedingFine') then return; end;

		local fine = plr:GetAttribute('SpeedingFine');

		local money = plr.Money;

		if money.Value < fine then NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'You do not have enough money!') return; end;

		MoneyService:SubtractMoney(plr, fine);
		plr:SetAttribute('SpeedingFine', nil);

		NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Notification', 'Payment Complete', 'You have paid your speeding fine of $'..tostring(fine), nil, 'Green');

		DataService.Remove(plr, 'SpeedingFine');
	end)

	task.spawn(function()
		while true do
			task.wait(0.2)
			for _,v in next, workspace.SpeedCameras:GetChildren() do
				local raycastParams = RaycastParams.new();
				raycastParams.FilterDescendantsInstances = {workspace.Cars};
				raycastParams.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Whitelist;

				local raycastResult = CastWithWhitelist(v.Position, RAY_DIRECTION, raycastParams);
				if raycastResult then
					local carPart = raycastResult.Instance;
					local Body = carPart:FindFirstAncestor('Body');
					if Body then
						local car = Body.Parent;
						local config = car.Config;
						if config:FindFirstChild('ELSPatterns') then
							if config.ELSPatterns.CurrentPattern.Value == nil then --If ELS is off
								for _,plr in next, game.Players:GetPlayers() do
									if plr.Car.Value == car and not plr:GetAttribute('SpeedTriggered') then
										local speed = mathFloor(ConvertSpeed(carPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity.Magnitude))
										local speedLimit = v:GetAttribute('SpeedLimit')
										if speed > speedLimit then
											plr:SetAttribute('SpeedTriggered', true);
											--IssueFine(plr, speedLimit, speed);
											NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Notification', 'WARNING', 'You were caught '..tostring(speed - speedLimit)..' KPH above the speed limit of '..tostring(speedLimit)..' KPH.', nil, 'Red')
											task.wait(2);
											plr:SetAttribute('SpeedTriggered', nil);
										end;
									end;
								end;
							end;
						else
							for _,plr in next, game.Players:GetPlayers() do
								if plr.Car.Value == car and not plr:GetAttribute('SpeedTriggered') then
									local speed = mathFloor(ConvertSpeed(carPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity.Magnitude))
									local speedLimit = v:GetAttribute('SpeedLimit')
									if speed > speedLimit then
										plr:SetAttribute('SpeedTriggered', true);
										IssueFine(plr, speedLimit, speed);
										task.wait(2);
										plr:SetAttribute('SpeedTriggered', nil);
									end;
								end;
							end;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end;
	end)
end;

function SpeedCameraService:Init()
	CastWithWhitelist = self.Shared.Raycast.CastWithWhitelist;
	ConvertSpeed = self.Shared.ConvertSpeed;
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
	DataService = self.Modules.DataService;
	MoneyService = self.Services.MoneyService;
end;


return SpeedCameraService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/TeamChangeService.lua ---

--[[
    TeamChangeService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Team Change Service
-- Khizzer
-- December 7, 2021



local TeamChangeService = {Client = {}}

local NetworkService;
local DeveloperCheck;
local GangService;
local ToolService;
local LogsService;

function TeamChangeService:Start()
	NetworkService.Connect('ChangeTeam', function(plr, team)
        if team == plr.Team and plr:GetAttribute('Division') == nil then return; end;
		if plr.Team == game.Teams.Prisoner then return; end;
        if not team:GetAttribute('GroupID') then return; end;
        if not team:GetAttribute('MinimumRank') then return; end;
        if plr:GetAttribute('HandcuffedBy') then return; end;
        if plr:GetAttribute('GrabbedBy') then return; end;

        if plr:GetAttribute('Ragdoll') then return; end; --Stops them changing teams to keep their tools while dead

        if not typeof(team) == "Instance" then return; end;

        local groupID = team:GetAttribute('GroupID');
        local minRank = team:GetAttribute('MinimumRank');
        local shouldLog = if plr:GetAttribute("Division") == "GCPS" and team.Name == "Civilian" then false else true

        if plr:GetRankInGroup(groupID) < minRank and not DeveloperCheck(plr) then return; end;
        if team:FindFirstChild('Condition') and not DeveloperCheck(plr) then
            if not require(team.Condition)(plr) then return end;
        end

        -- Allied forces
        local setDivision = nil;
        if team.Name == 'Canadian Armed Forces' and plr:GetRankInGroup(8236432) == 3 then
            setDivision = 'Allied Forces';
        end;

        if team.Name == 'Civilian' then
            --If he is switching from police etc to civilian
            plr:SetAttribute('GiveBackCivilianTools', true);
        end;
        if plr.Team.Name == 'Civilian' and plr:GetAttribute('Division') == nil then
            --If he is a civilian switching onto police etc
            ToolService:SaveCivilianTools(plr);
        end;

        plr:SetAttribute('Division', nil);

		plr.Team = team;
        if setDivision then plr:SetAttribute('Division', setDivision); end;
		plr:LoadCharacter();
        plr:SetAttribute('LastVehicle', nil);
        if shouldLog then
            LogsService:AddLog('Teams', `{plr.Name} joined {team.Name}`);
        end

        GangService:RemovePlayer(plr);
    end)
end


function TeamChangeService:Init()
    DeveloperCheck = self.Shared.DeveloperCheck;
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    GangService = self.Services.GangService;
    ToolService = self.Services.ToolService;
    LogsService = self.Services.LogsService;
end


return TeamChangeService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Teams/MedicService.lua ---

--[[
    MedicService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Teams
    Parent: Teams
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Medic Service
-- Khizzer
-- March 4, 2024


local NetworkService;

local MEDICAL_TEAMS = {'Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service', 'Vancouver Coastal Health', 'British Columbia Ambulance Service'};

local MedicService = {}

function MedicService:Start()
    NetworkService.Connect('MedicGear', function(plr, gear)
        if not table.find(MEDICAL_TEAMS, plr.Team.Name) and plr:GetAttribute('Division') ~= '12VFA' then return; end;

        local char = plr.Character;

        if gear == 'Gloves' then --Make this better in future when more gear is added
            if not char:FindFirstChild('MedicGloves') then
                local gloves = self.ServerAssets.MedicGloves:Clone();

                for _, arm in next, gloves:GetChildren() do
                    arm:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(plr.Character[arm.Name].CFrame);

                    for _,v in next, arm:GetChildren() do
                        if v:IsA('BasePart') then
                            local weld = Instance.new('WeldConstraint');
                            weld.Part0 = arm.PrimaryPart;
                            weld.Part1 = v;
                            weld.Parent = v;
                            v.Massless = true;
                            v.Anchored = false;
                        end;
                    end;

                    local weld = Instance.new('WeldConstraint');
                    weld.Part0 = arm.PrimaryPart;
                    weld.Part1 = plr.Character[arm.Name];
                    weld.Parent = plr.Character[arm.Name];
                end;

                gloves.Parent = plr.Character;
            else
                char.MedicGloves:Destroy();
            end
        end
    end)
end

function MedicService:Init()
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
end


return MedicService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Teams/SpecialistService.lua ---

--[[
    SpecialistService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Teams
    Parent: Teams
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local Debris = game:GetService('Debris');
local Players = game:GetService('Players');
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage');
local RunService = game:GetService('RunService');

local Comm = require(ReplicatedStorage.Packages.Comm)
local ServerComm = Comm.ServerComm.new(ReplicatedStorage, "Specialist")

local Properties = {
  IsGCPS = ServerComm:CreateProperty("IsGCPS", false),
  IsINSE = ServerComm:CreateProperty("IsINSE", false),
  GCPSFirearm = ServerComm:CreateProperty("GCPSFirearm", false),
  GCPSZipcuffs = ServerComm:CreateProperty("GCPSZipcuffs", false),
  GCPSElevatedFirearm = ServerComm:CreateProperty("GCPSElevatedFirearm", false),
}

local SpecialistService = {
  Properties = Properties
}

local WebUtil;
local CarService;
local NotificationService;

local TeamsToTrack = {'Provincial Court', 'Civilian', 'Legislative Assembly'}
local CstgBase = `https://napoleon.cstg.uk`
local CstgKey = `aed3256fdb6343d2a8aad5e7ed2fd439`

local TrelloPerms = {}

local function createSmokePart(cf: CFrame): Part & {
  Smoke: Smoke
}
  local part = Instance.new("Part")
  part.Anchored = true
  part.CanCollide = false
  part.Transparency = 1
  part.Size = Vector3.new(1, 1, 1)
  part.CFrame = cf

  local smoke = Instance.new("Smoke")
  smoke.Name = "Smoke"
  smoke.Color = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
  smoke.Opacity = 1
  smoke.RiseVelocity = 1
  smoke.Size = 10
  smoke.TimeScale = 1
  smoke.Enabled = true
  smoke.Parent = part

  part.Parent = workspace
  return part
end

function SpecialistService:_updateTrelloPerms()
  local ok, err = pcall(function()
    local data = WebUtil.GetJSON(`{CstgBase}/trello-perms?key={CstgKey}`)
    if data == nil then
      error(`HTTP Error`)
    end
    if typeof(data) ~= "table" then
      print(data)
      error(`Expected table, got {typeof(data)}`)
    end
    TrelloPerms = data

    for perm, users in TrelloPerms do
      if not Properties[perm] then continue end
      Properties[perm]:ClearForList(Players:GetPlayers())
      for _, user in users do
        local player = tonumber(user) and Players:GetPlayerByUserId(tonumber(user))
        if not player then continue end
        Properties[perm]:SetFor(player, true)
      end
    end
  end)
  if not ok then
    warn(`Error updating SpecialistService Trello perms: {err}`)
  end
end

function SpecialistService:_updateTrackingList()
  if RunService:IsStudio() or game.PrivateServerId ~= "" then
    return
  end

  local pouOk, pouErr = pcall(function()
    local list = {};

    for _,v in next, Players:GetPlayers() do
      if not table.find(TeamsToTrack, v.Team.Name) then continue end
      table.insert(list, v.Name)
    end

    WebUtil.SendJSON('http://51.195.198.17:3000/govtOfficialUpdate', {
      key = 'F7MqvU5npDBU4WnYYmnUz7Hduimh67HsJv',
      Players = list,
    })
  end)
  if not pouOk then
    warn(`Error updating POU tracking list: {pouErr}`)
  end

  local cstgOk, cstgErr = pcall(function()
    local list = {}

    for _, player in Players:GetPlayers() do
      local ref = `{player.Name}:{player.UserId}`
      local teamName = player.Team.Name
      local job = player:GetAttribute('CurrentJob')
      local division = player:GetAttribute('Division')

      if not list[teamName] then list[teamName] = {} end
      table.insert(list[teamName], ref)

      if division ~= nil then
        if not list[division] then list[division] = {} end
        table.insert(list[division], ref)
      end
      if job ~= nil then
        if not list[job] then list[job] = {} end
        table.insert(list[job], ref)
      end
    end

    WebUtil.SendJSON(`{CstgBase}/player-list?key={CstgKey}`, {
      list
    })
  end)
  if not cstgOk then
    warn(`Error updating CSTG tracking list: {cstgErr}`)
  end
end

function SpecialistService._playerAdded(plr)
  for slug, property in Properties do
    if SpecialistService:Check(plr, slug) then
      property:SetFor(plr, true)
    end
  end
end

function SpecialistService:Check(plr, perm)
  if not TrelloPerms[perm] then
    return false
  end

  return table.find(TrelloPerms[perm], tostring(plr.UserId)) ~= nil
end

function SpecialistService:Start()
  local NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;

  NetworkService.Connect('DEPLOY_SMOKESCREEN', function(plr)
    local car = plr.Car.Value
    if not car then return end
    if car.Config:GetAttribute("SmokeScreen") ~= true then return end
    if car.Config:GetAttribute("SsCooldown") and car.Config:GetAttribute("SsCooldown") > os.time() then return end
    car.Config:SetAttribute("SsCooldown", os.time() + (if plr:GetAttribute("Developer") == true then 60 else 300))

    local cf = car.Chassis.Mass.CFrame
    local part1 = createSmokePart(cf)
    local part2 = createSmokePart(car.Chassis.Mass.CFrame * CFrame.new(10, 0, 0))
    local part3 = createSmokePart(car.Chassis.Mass.CFrame * CFrame.new(-10, 0, 0))

    task.wait(30)
    part1.Smoke.Enabled = false
    part2.Smoke.Enabled = false
    part3.Smoke.Enabled = false
    Debris:AddItem(part1, 60)
    Debris:AddItem(part2, 60)
    Debris:AddItem(part3, 60)
  end)

  NetworkService.Connect('intelFeatures/despawnCar', function(plr)
    if plr:GetAttribute("Division") ~= "GCPS" then return end
    CarService.ClearCars(plr)
    NotificationService.Send(plr, "Cars cleared", "Your cars have been despawned, as though you reset", nil, 'Blue')
  end)

  NetworkService.Connect('intelFeatures/refreshAvatar', function(plr)
    if plr:GetAttribute("Division") ~= "GCPS" then return end;
    local description = Players:GetHumanoidDescriptionFromUserId(plr.UserId);
    (plr.Character.Humanoid :: Humanoid):ApplyDescription(description);
    NotificationService.Send(plr, "Avatar refreshed", "Your avatar has been refreshed", nil, 'Blue');
  end);

  NetworkService.Connect('intelFeatures/phantomCar', function(plr)
    if plr:GetAttribute("Division") ~= "GCPS" then return end
    local car = plr.Car.Value
    if not car then
      return _G.AeroError(plr, "No current car spawned")
    elseif car:GetAttribute('BeingTowed') then
      return _G.AeroError(plr, "Your car is being towed")
    elseif car:GetAttribute('Owner') ~= plr.Name then
      return _G.AeroError(plr, "You can't use this on someone else's car")
    elseif car:GetAttribute('LastDriver') ~= nil and car:GetAttribute('LastDriver') ~= plr.Name then
      return _G.AeroError(plr, "Your car has been stolen")
    end

    local carReg = car:GetAttribute('LicensePlate')

    if car:GetAttribute("Phantom") then
      car:SetAttribute("Phantom", nil)
      return NotificationService.Send(plr, "Phantom", `Your car ({carReg}) is no longer in phantom mode.`, nil, 'Blue')
    end

    car:SetAttribute("Phantom", true)
    return NotificationService.Send(plr, "Phantom", `Your car ({carReg}) is now in phantom mode.`, nil, 'Blue')
  end)

  NetworkService.Connect('intelWarps/CDMain', function(plr, noNotif)
    if plr:GetAttribute("Division") ~= "GCPS" then return end
    if plr.Character:FindFirstChild("ForceField") then plr.Character.ForceField:Destroy() end

    local n = Random.new():NextInteger(1, 2)
    local pos = workspace[`cityCiv{n}`].CFrame * CFrame.new(Vector3.new(0, 6, 0))

    local ff = Instance.new("ForceField")
    ff.Visible = true
    plr.Character:PivotTo(pos)
    ff.Parent = plr.Character
    task.delay(workspace[`cityCiv{n}`].Duration, function() ff:Destroy() end)

    local suc, plrImage = pcall(Players.GetUserThumbnailAsync, Players, plr.UserId, Enum.ThumbnailType.HeadShot, Enum.ThumbnailSize.Size420x420);
    if not suc then plrImage = nil; end;
    if noNotif ~= true and not plr.Character.Humanoid:GetAttribute('SurpressNotifications') then
      NetworkService.SendAll('Notification', 'Player Reset', plr.Name, plrImage, 'Black');
    end
  end)

  NetworkService.Connect('intelWarps/CDWest', function(plr, noNotif)
    if plr:GetAttribute("Division") ~= "GCPS" then return end
    if plr.Character:FindFirstChild("ForceField") then plr.Character.ForceField:Destroy() end

    local n = Random.new():NextInteger(1, 2)
    local pos = workspace[`wvCiv{n}`].CFrame * CFrame.new(Vector3.new(0, 6, 0))

    local ff = Instance.new("ForceField")
    ff.Visible = true
    plr.Character:PivotTo(pos)
    ff.Parent = plr.Character
    task.delay(workspace[`cityCiv{n}`].Duration, function() ff:Destroy() end)

    local suc, plrImage = pcall(Players.GetUserThumbnailAsync, Players, plr.UserId, Enum.ThumbnailType.HeadShot, Enum.ThumbnailSize.Size420x420);
    if not suc then plrImage = nil; end;
    if noNotif ~= true and not plr.Character.Humanoid:GetAttribute('SurpressNotifications') then
      NetworkService.SendAll('Notification', 'Player Reset', plr.Name, plrImage, 'Black');
    end
  end)

  NetworkService.Connect('intelWarps/GoTo', function(plr, location)
    if plr:GetAttribute("Division") ~= "GCPS" then return end
    local part
    if location == "Warehouse" then
      part = "WarehouseIntel"
    elseif location == "VPD" then
      part = "VpdIntel"
    elseif location == "1972" then
      part = "Intel1972"
    elseif location == "CFB" then
      part = "CFBIntel"
      elseif location == "BCSS" then
        part = "IntelBCSS"
    end
    if not part then return end
    local pos = workspace[part].CFrame * CFrame.new(Vector3.new(0, 5, 0))
    plr.Character:PivotTo(pos)
  end)

  Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(SpecialistService._playerAdded)

  while true do
    SpecialistService:_updateTrelloPerms()
    SpecialistService:_updateTrackingList()
    task.wait(90)
  end
end

function SpecialistService:Init()
  WebUtil = self.Modules.WebUtil
  CarService = self.Services.CarService
  NotificationService = self.Services.NotificationService
end

return SpecialistService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/TeleportService.lua ---

--[[
    TeleportService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Teleport Service
-- Khizzer
-- December 9, 2022

local CollectionService = game:GetService("CollectionService")

local TeleportService = {Client = {}}

local NetworkService;

function TeleportService:Start()
	NetworkService.Connect('Teleport', function(plr: Player, part: BasePart)
        if not typeof(part) == 'Instance' then return; end;
        if part.ClassName ~= 'Part' then return; end;

        if not CollectionService:HasTag(part, 'Teleport') then return; end;

        local destination = part.Parent.Destination;
        plr:RequestStreamAroundAsync(destination.Position, 100);

        --Choose random vector3 near destination
        local randomVector = Vector3.new(math.random(-5, 5), 1, math.random(-5, 5));
        local randomDestination = destination.Position + randomVector;

        --Teleport player
        plr.Character:PivotTo(CFrame.new(randomDestination));
    end)
end


function TeleportService:Init()
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
end


return TeleportService
